// ==UserScript==
// @name         ulepszator
// @namespace    http://tampermonkey.net/
// @version      0.1.1
// @description  try to take over the world!
// @author       You
// @match        https://*.margonem.pl/
// @grant        none
// ==/UserScript==

const ALLOWED_RARITIES = ["common"];
const MAX_REAGENTS = 25;
const HOTKEY = "j";

const CL = {
  ONE_HAND_WEAPON: 1,
  TWO_HAND_WEAPON: 2,
  ONE_AND_HALF_HAND_WEAPON: 3,
  DISTANCE_WEAPON: 4,
  HELP_WEAPON: 5,
  WAND_WEAPON: 6,
  ORB_WEAPON: 7,
  ARMOR: 8,
  HELMET: 9,
  BOOTS: 10,
  GLOVES: 11,
  RING: 12,
  NECKLACE: 13,
  SHIELD: 14,
  NEUTRAL: 15,
  CONSUME: 16,
  GOLD: 17,
  KEYS: 18,
  QUEST: 19,
  RENEWABLE: 20,
  ARROWS: 21,
  TALISMAN: 22,
  BOOK: 23,
  BAG: 24,
  BLESS: 25,
  UPGRADE: 26,
  RECIPE: 27,
  COINAGE: 28,
  QUIVER: 29,
  OUTFITS: 30,
  PETS: 31,
  TELEPORTS: 32,
};
const ALLOWED_ITEM_TYPES = [
  CL.ONE_HAND_WEAPON,
  CL.TWO_HAND_WEAPON,
  CL.ONE_AND_HALF_HAND_WEAPON,
  CL.DISTANCE_WEAPON,
  CL.HELP_WEAPON,
  CL.WAND_WEAPON,
  CL.ORB_WEAPON,
  CL.ARMOR,
  CL.HELMET,
  CL.BOOTS,
  CL.GLOVES,
  CL.RING,
  CL.NECKLACE,
  CL.SHIELD,
  CL.QUIVER,
];

(function () {
  let windowEnabled = false;

  const init = () => {
    try {
      if (!window.Engine.allInit) {
        setTimeout(init, 500);
        return;
      }
    } catch (error) {
      setTimeout(init, 500);
    }

    setup();
  };

  const setupCSS = () => {
    const css = `
      .upgrader-crafting-window {
        display: none !important;
      }
      .menu-item--yellow {
        background:rgb(57, 100, 17) !important;
        color: #fff !important;
        border-radius: 5px !important;
        padding: 5px !important;
      }
      .upgrader-label {
          position: absolute;
          top: 18px;
          left: 8px;
          height: 16px;
          width: 32px;
          text-align: center;
          color: yellow;
          pointer-events: none;
          text-shadow: -2px 0 black, 0 2px black, 2px 0 black, 0 -2px black;
          font-size: 0.75rem;
      }
    `;
    const style = document.createElement("style");
    style.appendChild(document.createTextNode(css));
    document.head.appendChild(style);
  };

  const setup = () => {
    setupCSS();
    setupHandler();
    initItemContextMenu();
    markItemAsUpgraded();
  };

  const setupHandler = () => {
    window.document.addEventListener("keydown", async (event) => {
      const isInputActive = ["TEXTAREA", "MAGIC_INPUT", "INPUT"].includes(
        document.activeElement.tagName
      );
      if (isInputActive) return;

      if (event.key === HOTKEY) {
        const upgradedItemId = getUpgradedItemId();
        const upgradedItem = Engine.items.getItemById(upgradedItemId);

        if (!upgradedItem) {
          message("Nie znaleziono wybranego przedmiotu.");
          return;
        }

        const reagents = getReagents();
        if (reagents.length === 0) {
          message("Nie znaleziono odpowiednich składników.");
          return;
        }

        toggleEnhancementWindow();
        const chunks = chunkReagents(reagents);
        await setEnhancedItem(upgradedItemId);

        for (const chunk of chunks) {
          await setReagents(upgradedItemId, chunk);
          const enhanceItemResponse = await enhanceItem(upgradedItemId, chunk);

          const { count, limit } =
            enhanceItemResponse.enhancement.usages_preview;
          message(
            `Ulepszono przedmiot ${upgradedItem.name}. Pozostało ${count} z ${limit} ulepszeń. Poziom ulepszenia: ${enhanceItemResponse.enhancement.progressing.upgradeLevel}.`
          );

          await sleep(300);
        }

        toggleEnhancementWindow();
      }
    });
  };

  const markItemAsUpgraded = (prevId) => {
    const upgradedItemId = getUpgradedItemId();
    const upgradedItem = Engine.items.getItemById(upgradedItemId);

    if (!upgradedItem) return;

    if (prevId) {
      const prevItem = Engine.items.getItemById(prevId);
      if (!prevItem) return;
      // $(`.item-id-${prevId}`).removeClass("upgraded-item");
      $(`.item-id-${prevId}`).find(".upgrader-label").remove();
    }

    const label = $(`<div class="upgrader-label">U</div>`);
    $(`.item-id-${upgradedItemId}`).append(label);
  };

  const initItemContextMenu = () => {
    const ogShowPopupMenu = Engine.interface.showPopupMenu;
    Engine.interface.showPopupMenu = function (menu, e) {
      const itemId = getItemIdFromClassName(e.currentTarget?.className);

      if (!itemId) {
        return ogShowPopupMenu.call(this, menu, e);
      }

      const item = Engine.items.getItemById(itemId);
      const currentSelectedItemId = getUpgradedItemId();

      if (!ALLOWED_ITEM_TYPES.includes(item?.cl)) {
        return ogShowPopupMenu.call(this, menu, e);
      }

      const menuItem =
        itemId === currentSelectedItemId
          ? [
              "Anuluj ulepszanie",
              () => {
                if (!currentSelectedItemId) return;
                setUpgradedItemId("");
                markItemAsUpgraded(currentSelectedItemId);

                message(`Anulowano ulepszanie przedmiotu ${item.name}`);
              },
              { button: { cls: "menu-item--red" } },
            ]
          : [
              "Ulepsz ten przedmiot",
              () => {
                setUpgradedItemId(itemId);
                markItemAsUpgraded(currentSelectedItemId);

                message(`Ulepszanie przedmiotu ${item.name}`);
              },
              { button: { cls: "menu-item--yellow" } },
            ];

      const updatedMenu = [menuItem, ...menu];
      ogShowPopupMenu.call(this, updatedMenu, e);
    };
  };

  const setUpgradedItemId = (itemId) => {
    window.localStorage.setItem(`upgrader-charId-${Engine.hero.d.id}`, itemId);
  };

  const getUpgradedItemId = () => {
    return window.localStorage.getItem(`upgrader-charId-${Engine.hero.d.id}`);
  };

  const getItemIdFromClassName = (className) => {
    if (!className) return null;

    const match = className.match(/item-id-(\d+)/);
    if (match) {
      return match[1];
    }
    return null;
  };

  const toggleEnhancementWindow = () => {
    if (windowEnabled) {
      Engine.crafting.window.wnd.$.removeClass("upgrader-crafting-window");
      Engine.interface.clickCrafting();
      windowEnabled = false;
      return;
    }

    Engine.crafting.window.wnd.$.addClass("upgrader-crafting-window");
    Engine.interface.clickCrafting();
    windowEnabled = true;
  };

  const getReagents = () => {
    const reagents = Engine.items
      .fetchLocationItems("g")
      .reduce((acc, item) => {
        const isAllowedRarity = ALLOWED_RARITIES.includes(
          item._cachedStats.rarity
        );
        const isAllowedType = ALLOWED_ITEM_TYPES.includes(item.cl);
        const canBeUsed =
          !item._cachedStats.hasOwnProperty("artisan_worthless");
        const isUpgraded = item._cachedStats.hasOwnProperty(
          "enhancement_upgrade_lvl"
        );

        if (
          isAllowedRarity &&
          isAllowedType &&
          item._cachedStats.rarity &&
          canBeUsed &&
          !isUpgraded
        ) {
          acc.push(item.id);
        }

        return acc;
      }, []);

    return [...new Set(reagents)];
  };

  const chunkReagents = (reagents) => {
    const chunks = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < reagents.length; i += MAX_REAGENTS) {
      chunks.push(reagents.slice(i, i + MAX_REAGENTS));
    }

    return chunks;
  };

  const setEnhancedItem = (itemId) => {
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      _g(`enhancement&action=status&item=${itemId}`, (data) => {
        resolve(data);
      });
    });
  };

  const setReagents = (itemId, reagentIds) => {
    const reagents = reagentIds.join(",");
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      _g(
        `enhancement&action=progress_preview&item=${itemId}&ingredients=${reagents}`,
        (data) => {
          resolve(data);
        }
      );
    });
  };

  const enhanceItem = (itemId, reagentIds) => {
    if (!itemId || !reagentIds) return;
    const reagents = reagentIds.join(",");

    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      _g(
        `enhancement&action=progress&item=${itemId}&ingredients=${reagents}`,
        (data) => {
          resolve(data);
        }
      );
    });
  };

  const sleep = (ms) => {
    return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
  };

  init();
})();

// ==UserScript==
// @name         Zap+
// @version      1.0
// @description  AutoGrp z losowym dodawaniem
// @author       Besiak
// @match        https://*.margonem.pl/
// @grant        none
// ==/UserScript==

(function(Engine) {
    'use strict';
    const ALLOWED_RELATIONS = [2, 4, 5];

function is_chat_focused() {
    const activeElement = document.activeElement;
    return activeElement.tagName === "INPUT" ||
           activeElement.tagName === "TEXTAREA" ||
           activeElement.isContentEditable;
}
    function is_he_in_party(id) {
        if (!Engine.party) return false;
        if (Engine.party.getLeaderId() !== Engine.hero.d.id) return true;
        for (let i = 0; i < Object.keys(Engine.party.getMembers()).length; i++) {
            if (Object.keys(Engine.party.getMembers())[i] == id) return true;
        }
        return false;
    }

    function canInvite(player) {
        return ALLOWED_RELATIONS.includes(player.d.relation);
    }

    const getPlayerIds = () => {
        return Object.entries(Engine.others.getDrawableList())
            .filter(
                ([_, entry]) => entry.isPlayer && canInvite(entry)
            )
            .map(([_, entry]) => ({ ...entry, sort: Math.random() }))
            .sort((a, b) => a.sort - b.sort) // losowe sortowanie
            .map((entry) => entry.d.id); // zwraca id gracza
    };

    function invitePlayer(playerId) {
        if (!is_chat_focused() && !is_he_in_party(playerId)) {
            _g("party&a=inv&id=" + playerId);
        }
    }

    function Ginvite() {
        const playerIds = getPlayerIds();
        for (let i = 0; i < playerIds.length; i++) {
            invitePlayer(playerIds[i]);
        }
    }

    document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
        if (e.keyCode === 66) {// klawisz B
            Ginvite();
        }
    });

})(window.Engine);

// ==UserScript==
// @name         AutoUcieczka NI
// @version      1.0
// @description  200zl ten dodatek kosztowal jak cos
// @author       yetrr
// @match        https://*.margonem.pl/*
// @grant        none
// ==/UserScript==

let storage;

const AUTO_FLEE = {
    updateStorage: () => localStorage.setItem(`autoflee/${window.getCookie("mchar_id")}`, JSON.stringify(storage)),
    createInputContainer: (target) => {
        return $("<div>")
            .css({
                width: '100%',
                margin: '4px 0',
                display: 'flex',
                alignItems: 'center',
                fontSize: '13px',
                fontWeight: 'bold'
            })
            .appendTo(target);
    },
    createBox: () => {
        const visibility = storage.visible ? "block" : "none";

        const box = $('<div id="flee-box">')
            .draggable({
                containment: "window",
                scroll: false,
                stop: (event, ui) => {
                    storage.position = {
                        x: ui.position.left,
                        y: ui.position.top
                    };
                    AUTO_FLEE.updateStorage();
                }
            })
            .css({
                zIndex: 11,
                width: "150px",
                height: "130px",
                background: "black",
                position: "absolute",
                border: "2px solid green",
                margin: "2px",
                left: storage.position.x,
                top: storage.position.y,
                display: visibility
            })
            .appendTo(".game-window-positioner");

        $("<div>")
            .text("UCIECZKA")
            .css({
                marginTop: '16px',
                textAlign: 'center',
                fontWeight: 'bold',
                fontSize: '20px',
                color: 'white'
            })
            .appendTo(box);

        const itemContainer = $("<div>")
            .css({
                height: "32px",
                width: "100%",
                display: "flex",
                alignItems: "center",
                justifyContent: "center",
                marginTop: "16px"
            })
            .appendTo(box);

        const itemMenu = $('<div>')
            .droppable({
                accept: ".item",
                drop: function (event, ui) {
                    const itemName = ui.draggable.attr("data-name");

                    const item = Object.values(Engine.items.fetchLocationItems('g')).find(item => {
                        return item.name === itemName;
                    });

                    if (!item) {
                        window.message("Nie znaleziono przedmiotu!");
                    } else if (item.cl !== 32) {
                        window.message("Wybrany przedmiot nie jest teleportem!");
                    } else {
                        $(this).css("background", "url(https://micc.garmory-cdn.cloud/obrazki/itemy/" + item.icon + ")");
                        storage.tp = item.name;
                        AUTO_FLEE.updateStorage();
                        window.message("Zapisano!");
                    }
                    event.stopPropagation();
                },
            })
            .css({
                width: "32px",
                height: "32px",
                background: "gray",
                border: "1px solid white"
            })
            .appendTo(itemContainer);

        const item = Object.values(Engine.items.fetchLocationItems("g")).find(item => item.name === storage.tp);
        if (item) itemMenu.css("background", "url(https://micc.garmory-cdn.cloud/obrazki/itemy/" + item.icon + ")");

        const deltaContainer = AUTO_FLEE.createInputContainer(box), deltaVal = storage.level;
        deltaContainer.css({"justifyContent": "center"})
        $(`<input id="flee-delta" type="text">`).val(deltaVal).css({width: "32px", padding: "0", textAlign: "center"}).appendTo(deltaContainer);

        const stateContainer = AUTO_FLEE.createInputContainer(box), stateVal = storage.enabled ? "checked" : "";
        $(`<input type="checkbox" id="flee-state" ${stateVal}>`).appendTo(stateContainer);
        $(`<label for="flee-state">Uciekanie ${stateVal ? "włączone" : "wyłączone"}</label>`).css("color", stateVal ? "lime" : "red").appendTo(stateContainer);
    },
    createBoxEvents: () => {
        $(".map_ball").on("contextmenu", function () {
            storage.visible = !storage.visible;
            AUTO_FLEE.updateStorage();
            $('#flee-box').toggle();
            return false;
        });
        $('input[id="flee-state"]').on("click", function () {
            const target = $(this).is(":checked");
            storage.enabled = !storage.enabled;
            AUTO_FLEE.updateStorage();
            $('label[for="flee-state"]').text(
                target ? "Uciekanie włączone" : "Uciekanie wyłączone"
            ).css(
                "color", target ? "lime" : "red"
            );
        });
        $('input[id="flee-delta"]').on("change", function () {
            const parsed = parseInt($(this).val());

            if (isNaN(parsed)) {
                window.message("Wprowadzono niepoprawną wartość!");
                $(this).val(5);
            } else {
                storage.level = parsed;
                AUTO_FLEE.updateStorage();
            }
        });
    },
    createGameEvents: () => {
        (old => {
            window.Engine.communication.parseJSON = function (data) {
                old.apply(this, arguments);

                if (storage.enabled && data.f && data.f.init && data.f.current) {
                    const shouldRun = Object.values(data.f.w).find(warrior => {
                        return !warrior.npc && warrior.team !== data.f.myteam && warrior.lvl > Engine.hero.d.lvl + storage.level;
                    });

                    if (shouldRun) {
                        const item = Object.values(window.Engine.items.fetchLocationItems("g")).find(item => {
                            return item._cachedStats.action && item._cachedStats.action === "flee" && !hasTimeLimit(item);
                        });

                        if (!item) {
                            window.message("Brak ucieczki");
                            return;
                        }
                        window._g(`moveitem&st=1&id=${item.id}`, () => {
                            if (!storage.tp) return;

                            const teleport = Object.values(window.Engine.items.fetchLocationItems("g")).find(item => {
                                return item.name === storage.tp && !hasTimeLimit(item);
                            });

                            if (!teleport) {
                                window.message("Brak teleportu lub cooldown");
                                return;
                            }
                            window._g(`moveitem&st=1&id=${teleport.id}`);
                        });
                    }
                }
            }
        })(window.Engine.communication.parseJSON);
    },
    init: () => {
        AUTO_FLEE.createBox();
        AUTO_FLEE.createBoxEvents();
    }
}

function hasTimeLimit(item) {
    const match = item.stat.match(/timelimit=\d+,(\d+)/);
    if (!match) {
        return;
    }
    const now = unix_time(true);
    const timelimit = +match[1];
    const diff = Math.ceil(timelimit - now);
    return diff > 0;
}

function waitFor(condition, interval = 100) {
    const promise = (resolve, reject) => {
        if (condition()) {
            resolve();
        } else {
            setTimeout(() => promise(resolve, reject), interval);
        }
    };
    return new Promise(promise);
}

waitFor(() => {
    if (window.Engine && window.Engine.firstLoadInit2 && !window.afterEvents && window.getCookie) {
        window.afterEvents = true;
        storage = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(`autoflee/${window.getCookie("mchar_id")}`)) || {
            position: {x: 0, y: 0},
            level: 5,
            tp: "Zwój teleportacji na Kwieciste Przejście",
            enabled: false,
            visible: true
        };
        AUTO_FLEE.createGameEvents();
    }
    return window.Engine && window.Engine.allInit;
}).then(() => {
    AUTO_FLEE.init();
});


// ==UserScript==
// @name         Margonem AutoExp (NWT) + Mikstury
// @namespace    http://tampermonkey.net/
// @version      1.3
// @description  AutoExp z GUI, automatycznym leczeniem i wsparciem dla nowego interfejsu Margonem (NWT)
// @author       ChatGPT
// @match        https://*.margonem.pl/
// @grant        none
// ==/UserScript==

(function () {
    'use strict';

    let botRunning = false;
    let interval = null;

    // === KONFIGURACJA ===
    const healPercent = 0.6; // Leczenie gdy HP < 60%
    const potionSlot = 2; // Slot mikstury (1–10)

    // === GUI ===
    function createGui() {
        const box = document.createElement("div");
        box.id = "autoexp-panel";
        box.style.position = "fixed";
        box.style.top = "100px";
        box.style.right = "20px";
        box.style.width = "200px";
        box.style.background = "rgba(0,0,0,0.85)";
        box.style.border = "2px solid #666";
        box.style.color = "#fff";
        box.style.padding = "10px";
        box.style.zIndex = "9999";
        box.style.fontFamily = "Arial, sans-serif";
        box.innerHTML = `
            <h4 style="margin-top:0; font-size:16px; text-align:center;">🧠 AutoExp Bot</h4>
            <p style="font-size:12px;">💊 Leczy, gdy HP < ${Math.floor(healPercent * 100)}%</p>
            <p style="font-size:12px;">⚔️ Atakuje i chodzi automatycznie</p>
            <button id="toggleBot" style="width:100%; margin-top:8px; padding:6px;">▶️ Włącz Bota</button>
            <div id="botStatus" style="margin-top:8px; font-size:12px;">Status: <span style="color:red;">Wyłączony</span></div>
        `;
        document.body.appendChild(box);

        document.getElementById("toggleBot").onclick = () => {
            if (botRunning) stopBot();
            else startBot();
        };
    }

    function updateGuiStatus() {
        const statusEl = document.getElementById("botStatus");
        const btn = document.getElementById("toggleBot");
        if (!statusEl || !btn) return;

        if (botRunning) {
            statusEl.innerHTML = `Status: <span style="color:lime;">Włączony</span>`;
            btn.textContent = "⏹️ Wyłącz Bota";
        } else {
            statusEl.innerHTML = `Status: <span style="color:red;">Wyłączony</span>`;
            btn.textContent = "▶️ Włącz Bota";
        }
    }

    // === BOT LOGIKA ===
    function getNearestNpc() {
        let nearest = null;
        let minDist = Infinity;

        for (let id in g.npcs) {
            const npc = g.npcs[id];
            if (npc && npc.d && npc.typ === 1 && npc.hp > 0) {
                const dist = Math.abs(npc.x - hero.x) + Math.abs(npc.y - hero.y);
                if (dist < minDist) {
                    minDist = dist;
                    nearest = npc;
                }
            }
        }

        return nearest;
    }

    function attackNpc(npc) {
        if (npc) {
            _g(`fight&a=${npc.id}`);
            console.log(`[AutoExp] Atakuję: ${npc.nick}`);
        }
    }

    function walkRandom() {
        if (hero.moving) return;

        const directions = [
            { x: hero.x + 1, y: hero.y },
            { x: hero.x - 1, y: hero.y },
            { x: hero.x, y: hero.y + 1 },
            { x: hero.x, y: hero.y - 1 }
        ];

        const choice = directions[Math.floor(Math.random() * directions.length)];
        _g(`m${choice.x},${choice.y}`);
        console.log(`[AutoExp] Ruch losowy (${choice.x}, ${choice.y})`);
    }

    function usePotion() {
        // Automatyczne użycie mikstury z paska
        _g(`u${potionSlot}`);
        console.log(`[AutoExp] Wypito miksturę z slotu ${potionSlot}`);
    }

    function autoExp() {
        if (typeof g === "undefined" || !g.npcs) return;

        if (isFight || hero.moving) return;

        // Leczenie
        if (hero.hp < hero.maxhp * healPercent) {
            usePotion();
            return;
        }

        // Walka lub ruch
        const npc = getNearestNpc();
        if (npc) {
            const dist = Math.abs(npc.x - hero.x) + Math.abs(npc.y - hero.y);
            if (dist <= 1) {
                attackNpc(npc);
            } else {
                _g(`m${npc.x},${npc.y}`);
                console.log(`[AutoExp] Idę do moba: ${npc.nick}`);
            }
        } else {
            walkRandom();
        }
    }

    function startBot() {
        if (botRunning) return;
        interval = setInterval(autoExp, 1000);
        botRunning = true;
        updateGuiStatus();
        console.log("[AutoExp] Bot uruchomiony.");
    }

    function stopBot() {
        if (!botRunning) return;
        clearInterval(interval);
        botRunning = false;
        updateGuiStatus();
        console.log("[AutoExp] Bot zatrzymany.");
    }

    // Start po załadowaniu
    window.addEventListener('load', () => {
        setTimeout(createGui, 2000);
        console.log("[AutoExp] GUI załadowane.");
    });

})();

    function stworzMenu() {

                </div>

                <button id="dom-toggle" style="width: 100%; padding: 6px; border: none; border-radius: 4px; cursor: pointer; font-weight: bold; background: ${localStorage.getItem('dom_active') === 'true' ?                 <button id="dom-reset" style="width: 100%; padding: 4px; border: none; border-radius: 4px; cursor: pointer; font-weight: bold; background: #f39c12; color: #000;">RESET TRASY</button>
            </div>
        `;
        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.innerHTML = menuHTML;
        document.body.appendChild(div);

        document.getElementById('exp-select').addEventListener('change', function() {
            const exp = expowiska[this.value];
            if(exp) {
                document.getElementById('dom-maps').value = exp.maps;
                localStorage.setItem('dom_maps', exp.maps);

                document.getElementById('dom-blacklist').value = exp.blacklist;
                localStorage.setItem('dom_blacklist', exp.blacklist);

                const dojscieValue = exp.dojscie || "";
                document.getElementById('dom-dojscie-maps').value = dojscieValue;
                localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_maps', dojscieValue);

                const minLvl = exp.minLvl !== undefined ? exp.minLvl : 1;
                const maxLvl = exp.maxLvl !== undefined ? exp.maxLvl : 300;

                document.getElementById('dom-min').value = minLvl;
                localStorage.setItem('dom_min_lvl', minLvl);

                document.getElementById('dom-max').value = maxLvl;
                localStorage.setItem('dom_max_lvl', maxLvl);
            }
        });

        document.getElementById('dom-min').addEventListener('input', (e) => localStorage.setItem('dom_min_lvl', e.target.value));
        document.getElementById('dom-max').addEventListener('input', (e) => localStorage.setItem('dom_max_lvl', e.target.value));
        document.getElementById('dom-maps').addEventListener('input', (e) => localStorage.setItem('dom_maps', e.target.value));
        document.getElementById('dom-blacklist').addEventListener('input', (e) => localStorage.setItem('dom_blacklist', e.target.value));
        document.getElementById('dom-dojscie-maps').addEventListener('input', (e) => localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_maps', e.target.value));
        document.getElementById('dom-dojscie-toggle').addEventListener('change', (e) => localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_enabled', e.target.checked));

        document.getElementById('dom-toggle').addEventListener('click', function() {
            const stan = localStorage.getItem('dom_active') === 'true';
            localStorage.setItem('dom_active', (!stan).toString());
            this.innerText = !stan ? 'WŁĄCZONY' : 'WYŁĄCZONY';
            this.style.background = !stan ? '#27ae60' : '#c0392b';
        });

        document.getElementById('dom-reset').addEventListener('click', function() {
            if (typeof Engine !== 'undefined' && Engine.map && Engine.map.d) {
                const aktualnaMapaId = parseInt(Engine.map.d.id, 10);
                const isDojscieActive = localStorage.getItem('dom_dojscie_enabled') === 'true';

                const dojscieTrasa = (localStorage.getItem('dom_dojscie_maps') || "").split(/[\s,]+/).map(id => parseInt(id.trim(), 10)).filter(id => !isNaN(id));
                const mainTrasa = (localStorage.getItem('dom_maps') || "").split(/[\s,]+/).map(id => parseInt(id.trim(), 10)).filter(id => !isNaN(id));

                let indexDojscie = dojscieTrasa.indexOf(aktualnaMapaId);
                let indexMain = mainTrasa.indexOf(aktualnaMapaId);

                if (isDojscieActive && indexDojscie !== -1) {
                    localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_finished', 'false');
                    localStorage.setItem('dom_step', indexDojscie.toString());
                    //alert(`Trasa zsynchronizowana!\nZnaleziono Cię na mapie DOJŚCIA: ${aktualnaMapaId} (Krok: ${indexDojscie + 1}).\nBot dokończy najpierw Dojście (bez bicia).`);
                } else if (indexMain !== -1) {
                    if (isDojscieActive) localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_finished', 'true');
                    localStorage.setItem('dom_step', indexMain.toString());
                    //alert(`Trasa zsynchronizowana!\nZnaleziono Cię na GŁÓWNEJ TRASIE: ${aktualnaMapaId} (Krok: ${indexMain + 1}).`);
                } else {
                    localStorage.setItem('dom_step', '0');
                    localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_finished', 'false');
                    alert(`Brak obecnej mapy (${aktualnaMapaId}) w Dojściu oraz Głównej Trasie.\nZresetowano wszystko do początku.`);
                }
            } else {
                localStorage.setItem('dom_step', '0');
                localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_finished', 'false');
                alert("Zresetowano krok trasy do zera.");
            }
        });

        const menuEl = document.getElementById('bot-menu');
        const headerEl = document.getElementById('bot-menu-header');
        let isDragging = false;
        let offsetX = 0; let offsetY = 0;
        headerEl.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => { isDragging = true; offsetX = e.clientX - menuEl.getBoundingClientRect().left; offsetY = e.clientY - menuEl.getBoundingClientRect().top; });
        document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => { if (isDragging) { menuEl.style.left = (e.clientX - offsetX) + 'px'; menuEl.style.top = (e.clientY - offsetY) + 'px'; } });
        document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => { if (isDragging) { isDragging = false; localStorage.setItem('dom_menu_x', parseInt(menuEl.style.left, 10)); localStorage.setItem('dom_menu_y', parseInt(menuEl.style.top, 10)); } });
    }

    function glownaLogikaAPI() {
        try {
            if (typeof Engine === 'undefined' || !Engine.hero || !Engine.npcs || !Engine.map) return;

            const isBotActive = localStorage.getItem('dom_active') === 'true'; // Sprawdzanie czy bot w ogóle włączony

            const aktualnaMapaId = parseInt(Engine.map.d.id, 10);
            const mapInfoEl = document.getElementById('bot-map-info');
            if (mapInfoEl) mapInfoEl.innerText = `Mapa: ${aktualnaMapaId}`;

            const isDojscieActive = localStorage.getItem('dom_dojscie_enabled') === 'true';
            let isDojscieFinished = localStorage.getItem('dom_dojscie_finished') === 'true';

            let dojscieTrasa = (localStorage.getItem('dom_dojscie_maps') || "").split(/[\s,]+/).map(id => parseInt(id.trim(), 10)).filter(id => !isNaN(id));
            let mainTrasa = (localStorage.getItem('dom_maps') || "").split(/[\s,]+/).map(id => parseInt(id.trim(), 10)).filter(id => !isNaN(id));

            if (isDojscieActive && !isDojscieFinished && mainTrasa.includes(aktualnaMapaId)) {
                console.log("[BOT] Wszedłem na główną trasę! Koniec pacyfistycznego dojścia.");
                localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_finished', 'true');
                isDojscieFinished = true;
                localStorage.setItem('dom_step', mainTrasa.indexOf(aktualnaMapaId).toString());
            }

            const moznaBic = !(isDojscieActive && !isDojscieFinished);

            // --- INTELIGENTNY AUTO-BERSERK (Zależny od statusu Bota) ---
            if (isBotActive && moznaBic) {
                // Gdy bot jest ON i jesteśmy na Głównej Trasie -> Upewnij się, że Berserk JEST WŁĄCZONY
                const berserkIconDisabled = document.querySelector('div.gargonem-pocket-berserk-icon.disabled[tip-id="562"]');
                if (berserkIconDisabled && Date.now() - ostatniBerserk > 4000) {
                    ostatniBerserk = Date.now();
                    berserkIconDisabled.click();
                }
            } else {
                // Gdy bot jest WYŁĄCZONY albo jesteśmy na Pacyfistycznym Dojściu -> Upewnij się, że Berserk JEST WYŁĄCZONY
                const berserkIconEnabled = document.querySelector('div.gargonem-pocket-berserk-icon:not(.disabled)[tip-id="562"]');
                if (berserkIconEnabled && Date.now() - ostatniBerserk > 4000) {
                    ostatniBerserk = Date.now();
                    berserkIconEnabled.click();
                }
            }
            // -----------------------------------------------------------

            // Przerywamy chodzenie/bicie, jeśli bot wyłączony
            if (!isBotActive) return;

            const teraz = Date.now();
            if (teraz < ostatniaAkcja) return;

            let trasa;
            if (isDojscieActive && !isDojscieFinished) {
                trasa = [...dojscieTrasa];
                if (mainTrasa.length > 0) trasa.push(mainTrasa[0]);
            } else {
                trasa = mainTrasa;
            }

            if (aktualnaMapaId !== lastMapId) {
                let currentStep = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('dom_step') || "0");
                if (currentStep >= trasa.length) currentStep = 0;

                let expectedNextMap = trasa[(currentStep + 1) % trasa.length];

                if (aktualnaMapaId === expectedNextMap) {
                    localStorage.setItem('dom_step', ((currentStep + 1) % trasa.length).toString());
                } else {
                    let idx = trasa.indexOf(aktualnaMapaId);
                    if (idx !== -1) localStorage.setItem('dom_step', idx.toString());
                }
                lastMapId = aktualnaMapaId;
            }

            // Odklinowywanie
            if (Engine.hero.opt && Engine.hero.opt.go) {
                if (Engine.hero.d.x === lastHeroX && Engine.hero.d.y === lastHeroY) stuckCounter++;
                else stuckCounter = 0;
                lastHeroX = Engine.hero.d.x; lastHeroY = Engine.hero.d.y;
                if (stuckCounter > 12) {
                    Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: Engine.hero.d.x + (Math.random() > 0.5 ? 4 : -4), y: Engine.hero.d.y + (Math.random() > 0.5 ? 4 : -4) });
                    stuckCounter = 0; ostatniaAkcja = teraz + 1000; return;
                }
            }

            // Auto-szybka walka
            if (Engine.battle && Engine.battle.show) {
                const fastFightBtn = document.querySelector('.auto-fight-btn');
                if (fastFightBtn && fastFightBtn.offsetParent !== null) fastFightBtn.click();
                return;
            }

            let najblizszyMob = null;
            let minDystans = Infinity;

            if (moznaBic) {
                const minLvl = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('dom_min_lvl'), 10);
                const maxLvl = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('dom_max_lvl'), 10);
                const blacklist = localStorage.getItem('dom_blacklist').split(/[\s,]+/).filter(Boolean);

                for (const [idString, npc] of Object.entries(Engine.npcs.check())) {
                    if (blacklist.includes(idString)) continue;

                    if (npc.d && (npc.d.type === 2 || npc.d.type === 3) && npc.d.lvl >= minLvl && npc.d.lvl <= maxLvl) {
                        if (czyDostepny(npc.d.x, npc.d.y)) {
                            let dist = Math.max(Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.x - npc.d.x), Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.y - npc.d.y));
                            if (dist < minDystans) {
                                minDystans = dist;
                                najblizszyMob = { id: idString, name: npc.d.nick || npc.d.name || "Nieznany", x: npc.d.x, y: npc.d.y };
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            if (najblizszyMob) {
                console.log(`[BOT] Podchodzę do: ${najblizszyMob.name} (ID: ${najblizszyMob.id})`);
                Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: najblizszyMob.x, y: najblizszyMob.y });
                ostatniaAkcja = teraz + 800;
            } else {
                let currentStep = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('dom_step') || "0");
                if (currentStep >= trasa.length) currentStep = 0;
                let nextStep = (currentStep + 1) % trasa.length;
                let nastepnaMapaId = trasa[nextStep];
                let celBramka = Engine.map.gateways.getList().find(b => b.d && parseInt(b.d.id) === nastepnaMapaId);

                if (celBramka) {
                    let x = parseInt(celBramka.d.x);
                    let y = parseInt(celBramka.d.y);

                    let distToGateway = Math.max(Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.x - x), Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.y - y));

                    if (distToGateway === 0) {
                        ostatniaAkcja = teraz + 500;
                        const range = 3;
                        const randomX = Engine.hero.d.x + (Math.floor(Math.random() * (range * 2 + 1)) - range);
                        const randomY = Engine.hero.d.y + (Math.floor(Math.random() * (range * 2 + 1)) - range);
                        Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: randomX, y: randomY });
                    } else if (distToGateway < 3) {
                        if (typeof celBramka.onclick === 'function') celBramka.onclick({ stopPropagation: ()=>{}, preventDefault: ()=>{} });
                        ostatniaAkcja = teraz + 5000;
                    } else {
                        Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: x, y: y });
                        ostatniaAkcja = teraz + 2000;
                    }
                }
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error("[AUTO-HUNTER ERROR COUGHT]", error);
        }
    }

    setTimeout(stworzMenu, 2000);
    setInterval(glownaLogikaAPI, 500);
})();
