    // ==========================================
    // ZMIENNE STANU BOTA
    // ==========================================
    let questNames = Object.keys(QUESTS_DATABASE);
    let currentQuestName = localStorage.getItem('margo_quest_active_name') || questNames[0];
    if (!QUESTS_DATABASE[currentQuestName]) currentQuestName = questNames[0];

    // Odczytywanie zapisanego kroku dla obecnego questa
    let currentStepIndex = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('margo_quest_step_' + currentQuestName), 10) || 0;
    // Zabezpieczenie: jeśli zmienisz długość questa w kodzie, bot wróci do zera żeby się nie zepsuć
    if (currentStepIndex >= (QUESTS_DATABASE[currentQuestName] ? QUESTS_DATABASE[currentQuestName].length : 0)) {
        currentStepIndex = 0;
    }

    let isRunning = false;
    let sequenceInterval = null;
    let lastActionTime = 0;

    // Zmienna pamiętająca, czy bot włączył Berserka w skrypcie
    let botBerserkActive = false;

    // ==========================================
    // WBUDOWANY SYSTEM A* I SKANOWANIE ŚCIAN
    // ==========================================
    let cachedColMethod = null;
    let skanerMapId = null;

    function odnajdzUkrytaFunkcjeScian(w, h) {
        let col = Engine.map.col;
        if (!col) return null;
        if (typeof col.check === 'function') return (x, y) => col.check(x, y);
        if (typeof col.checkCollision === 'function') return (x, y) => col.checkCollision(x, y);
        if (typeof col.get === 'function') return (x, y) => {
            let val = col.get(x, y);
            return val !== 0 && val !== '0' && val !== false && val !== undefined && val !== null;
        };
        for (let key in col) {
            let ukryteDane = col[key];
            if (ukryteDane && (typeof ukryteDane === 'string' || Array.isArray(ukryteDane))) {
                if (ukryteDane.length === w * h) {
                    return (x, y) => {
                        let v = ukryteDane[x + y * w];
                        return v !== '0' && v !== 0 && v !== ' ';
                    };
                }
            }
        }
        if (typeof col === 'object') return (x, y) => col[x] && col[x][y];
        return null;
    }

    function czyPoleZablokowane(x, y) {
        if (typeof Engine === 'undefined' || !Engine.map || !Engine.map.d) return true;
        const w = Engine.map.d.x;
        const h = Engine.map.d.y;

        if (x < 0 || y < 0 || x >= w || y >= h) return true;

        if (skanerMapId !== Engine.map.d.id) {
            cachedColMethod = odnajdzUkrytaFunkcjeScian(w, h);
            skanerMapId = Engine.map.d.id;
        }

        if (cachedColMethod) return cachedColMethod(x, y);

        if (Engine.map.d.col && typeof Engine.map.d.col === 'string') {
            return Engine.map.d.col.charAt(x + y * w) !== '0';
        }
        return false;
    }

    function szukajDrogi(startX, startY, celX, celY, isBlockedFunc) {
        if (startX === celX && startY === celY) return [];

        let openSet = [{ x: startX, y: startY, g: 0, f: Math.abs(startX - celX) + Math.abs(startY - celY), parent: null }];
        let closedSet = new Set();
        let openMap = new Map();

        function getId(x, y) { return x + "," + y; }
        openMap.set(getId(startX, startY), openSet[0]);

        let iterations = 0;

        while (openSet.length > 0) {
            iterations++;
            if (iterations > 1500) return null;

            let minIndex = 0;
            for (let i = 1; i < openSet.length; i++) {
                if (openSet[i].f < openSet[minIndex].f) minIndex = i;
            }

            let current = openSet[minIndex];
            openSet.splice(minIndex, 1);
            openMap.delete(getId(current.x, current.y));

            if (current.x === celX && current.y === celY) {
                let path = [];
                let curr = current;
                while(curr.parent) { path.push({x: curr.x, y: curr.y}); curr = curr.parent; }
                return path.reverse();
            }

            closedSet.add(getId(current.x, current.y));

            let sasiedzi = [
                {x: current.x, y: current.y - 1}, {x: current.x, y: current.y + 1},
                {x: current.x - 1, y: current.y}, {x: current.x + 1, y: current.y}
            ];

            for (let s of sasiedzi) {
                if (isBlockedFunc(s.x, s.y) && !(s.x === celX && s.y === celY)) continue;

                let sId = getId(s.x, s.y);
                if (closedSet.has(sId)) continue;

                let g = current.g + 1;
                let existing = openMap.get(sId);

                if (!existing) {
                    let newNode = { x: s.x, y: s.y, g: g, f: g + Math.abs(s.x - celX) + Math.abs(s.y - celY), parent: current };
                    openSet.push(newNode);
                    openMap.set(sId, newNode);
                } else if (g < existing.g) {
                    existing.g = g;
                    existing.f = g + Math.abs(s.x - celX) + Math.abs(s.y - celY);
                    existing.parent = current;
                }
            }
        }
        return null;
    }
    // ==========================================

    // Pobieranie aktualnego lvla gracza
    function getHeroLevel() {
        if (typeof Engine !== 'undefined' && Engine.hero && Engine.hero.d) return Engine.hero.d.lvl;
        if (typeof hero !== 'undefined' && hero.lvl) return hero.lvl;
        return 1;
    }

    // Funkcja pobierająca aktualną sekwencję kroków
    function getActiveSequence() {
        return QUESTS_DATABASE[currentQuestName] || [];
    }

    // Ulepszona funkcja pomocnicza do interakcji
    function forceInteract(target) {
        if (!target) return;

        let mockEvent = { preventDefault: () => {}, stopPropagation: () => {}, button: 2 };

        if (typeof target.onclick === 'function') {
            target.onclick(mockEvent);
        } else if (target.d && target.d.isGw) {
            let gwObj = Engine.map.gateways.getList().find(g => g.d && g.d.id === target.d.id);
            if (gwObj && typeof gwObj.onclick === 'function') gwObj.onclick(mockEvent);
        } else if (target.emit) {
            target.emit('interact');
        } else if (typeof Engine !== 'undefined' && Engine.hero && typeof Engine.hero.interact === 'function') {
            Engine.hero.interact(target.d.id);
        } else {
            console.warn("[Bot] Obiekt nie posiada wspieranej metody interakcji!");
        }
    }

    function rebuildStepSelect() {
        const stepSelect = document.getElementById('quest-step-select');
        if (!stepSelect) return;

        stepSelect.innerHTML = '';
        const sequence = getActiveSequence();

        sequence.forEach((step, index) => {
            let opt = document.createElement('option');
            opt.value = index;
            opt.innerText = `[Krok ${index + 1}] ${step.desc}`;
            stepSelect.appendChild(opt);
        });
        stepSelect.value = currentStepIndex;
    }

    function updateDisplay() {
        const statusEl = document.getElementById('quest-bot-status');
        const stepEl = document.getElementById('quest-bot-step');
        const stepSelect = document.getElementById('quest-step-select');
        const sequence = getActiveSequence();

        // ++ ZAPISYWANIE AKTUALNEGO KROKU DO PAMIĘCI PRZEGLĄDARKI ++
        localStorage.setItem('margo_quest_step_' + currentQuestName, currentStepIndex);

        if (stepSelect) stepSelect.value = currentStepIndex;

        if (currentStepIndex >= sequence.length) {
            if (stepEl) stepEl.innerText = "Quest ukończony! 🎉";
            if (statusEl) {
                statusEl.innerText = "Zakończono";
                statusEl.style.color = "#2ecc71";
            }
            isRunning = false;
            clearInterval(sequenceInterval);
            const toggleBtn = document.getElementById('quest-toggle-btn');
            if (toggleBtn) {
                toggleBtn.innerHTML = "▶ START";
                toggleBtn.style.background = "#27ae60";
            }
            return;
        }

        const currentStep = sequence[currentStepIndex];
        if (stepEl && currentStep) {
            stepEl.innerText = `Krok ${currentStepIndex + 1}: ${currentStep.desc || currentStep.type || currentStep.action}`;
        }
    }

    // ==========================================
    // GŁÓWNA PĘTLA PROCESUJĄCA KROKI
    // ==========================================
    function processSequence() {// ==================================================
        // --- [ANTY-CAPTCHA: AUTOMATYCZNE WYKRYWANIE] ---
        // ==================================================
        let preCaptcha = document.querySelector('.pre-captcha.show');
        if (preCaptcha) {
            let timeEl = preCaptcha.querySelector('.captcha-pre-info__time');
            if (timeEl) {
                let timeLeft = parseInt(timeEl.innerText, 10);
                if (timeLeft <= 10) {
                    if (isRunning) {
                        console.log("[Bot] Ostrzeżenie: Captcha za <=10s! Automatyczna pauza.");
                        let toggleBtn = document.getElementById('quest-toggle-btn');
                        if (toggleBtn) toggleBtn.click(); // Symuluje wciśnięcie PAUZY w UI bota

                        let statusEl = document.getElementById('quest-bot-status');
                        if (statusEl) {
                            statusEl.innerText = "Wstrzymano (CAPTCHA)";
                            statusEl.style.color = "#e74c3c"; // Czerwony kolor uwagi
                        }
                    }
                    return; // Zablokuj dalsze wykonywanie kodu z tego interwału
                }
            }
        }
        // ==================================================
        let now = Date.now();
        if (now < lastActionTime) return;

        const currentMap = Engine.map.d ? parseInt(Engine.map.d.id, 10) : 0;

        if (typeof Engine !== 'undefined' && Engine.battle && Engine.battle.show) {
            let fastFightBtn = document.querySelector('.auto-fight-btn');
            if (!Engine.battle._botAutoFought) {
                if (fastFightBtn) {
                    fastFightBtn.click();
                    Engine.battle._botAutoFought = true;
                    lastActionTime = now + 1500;
                } else {
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                }
            } else {
                lastActionTime = now + 500;
            }
            return;
        } else if (typeof Engine !== 'undefined' && Engine.battle) {
            Engine.battle._botAutoFought = false;
        }

        const sequence = getActiveSequence();
        if (currentStepIndex >= sequence.length) {
            updateDisplay();
            return;
        }

        let step = sequence[currentStepIndex];
        updateDisplay();

        // Skróty do współrzędnych gracza (często używane przy A*)
        const graczX = Engine.hero.d.x;
        const graczY = Engine.hero.d.y;

        switch (step.type || step.action) {
                // ==================================================
            // CASE: LOSOWY KROK (bez sprawdzania czy doszedł)
            // ==================================================
            case 'random_step': {
                // Wyznaczamy 4 sąsiadujące kratki (góra, dół, lewo, prawo)
                let sasiedzi = [
                    { x: graczX, y: graczY - 1 },
                    { x: graczX, y: graczY + 1 },
                    { x: graczX - 1, y: graczY },
                    { x: graczX + 1, y: graczY }
                ];

                // Filtrujemy tylko te, w które da się wejść (używamy Twojej funkcji skanującej ściany)
                let dostepne = sasiedzi.filter(p => !czyPoleZablokowane(p.x, p.y));

                if (dostepne.length > 0) {
                    // Wybieramy losową wolną kratkę
                    let losowePole = dostepne[Math.floor(Math.random() * dostepne.length)];
                    console.log(`[Bot] Wykonuję ślepy krok na [${losowePole.x}, ${losowePole.y}]`);
                    Engine.hero.autoGoTo(losowePole);
                } else {
                    console.warn("[Bot] Brak wolnego miejsca na losowy krok wokół gracza!");
                }

                // NATYCHMIASTOWE ZALICZENIE KROKU (Bez sprawdzania dystansu)
                currentStepIndex++;

                // Dajemy serwerowi 1000ms na przetworzenie ruchu, cofnięcie postaci i wyświetlenie dialogu,
                // zanim bot odpali kolejny krok z JSON-a
                lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                break;
            }

            case 'dialog_text':
                let dialogueOptions = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.dialogue-window-answer, .dialog-answer, .answer'))
                                           .filter(el => el.offsetParent !== null);

                if (dialogueOptions.length > 0) {
                    let foundIndex = dialogueOptions.findIndex(el => {
                        let textContent = el.innerText || el.textContent;
                        return textContent.toLowerCase().includes(step.text.toLowerCase());
                    });

                    if (foundIndex !== -1) {
                        if (typeof Engine !== 'undefined' && Engine.dialogue && typeof Engine.dialogue.choose === 'function') {
                            try {
                                Engine.dialogue.choose(foundIndex);
                                currentStepIndex++;
                                lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                                break;
                            } catch(e) {
                                console.error("[Bot] Błąd Engine.dialogue.choose:", e);
                            }
                        }
                        dialogueOptions[foundIndex].click();
                        currentStepIndex++;
                        lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                    } else {
                        console.warn(`[Bot] Nie znaleziono opcji dialogowej zawierającej: "${step.text}"`);
                        lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                    }
                } else {
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                }
                break;

            case 'path':
                let nowTimePath = Date.now();
                if (!step.maps || step.maps.length === 0) {
                    console.error("[Bot] Błąd: Brak tablicy maps w akcji 'path'.");
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    break;
                }

                // 1. USTALENIE CELU (sprawdzamy czy to zwykła tablica, czy tablica w tablicy)
                let isMultiPath = Array.isArray(step.maps[0]);

                // Ostatnia mapa z pierwszej dostępnej ścieżki to nasz ostateczny cel
                let finalMap = isMultiPath ? step.maps[0][step.maps[0].length - 1] : step.maps[step.maps.length - 1];

                let pathStatusEl = document.getElementById('quest-bot-status');
                if (pathStatusEl) {
                    pathStatusEl.innerText = `Trasa: Cel -> ${finalMap}`;
                    pathStatusEl.style.color = "#3498db";
                }

                // 2. SPRAWDZENIE CZY JESTEŚMY U CELU
                if (currentMap === finalMap) {
                    console.log(`[Bot] Dotarto do celu trasy: ${finalMap}`);
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = nowTimePath + 500;
                    break;
                }

                // 3. SZUKANIE NASTĘPNEJ MAPY
                let nextMapId = null;

                if (isMultiPath) {
                    // ZAAWANSOWANE: Znajdź pierwszą ścieżkę, która zawiera obecną mapę,
                    // i na której obecna mapa NIE JEST jej ostatnim elementem
                    let activePath = step.maps.find(p => p.includes(currentMap) && p.indexOf(currentMap) < p.length - 1);
                    if (activePath) {
                        nextMapId = activePath[activePath.indexOf(currentMap) + 1];
                    }
                } else {
                    // KLASYCZNE: Zwykła płaska tablica
                    let mapIndex = step.maps.indexOf(currentMap);
                    if (mapIndex !== -1 && mapIndex < step.maps.length - 1) {
                        nextMapId = step.maps[mapIndex + 1];
                    }
                }

                // 4. IDZIEMY DO BRAMKI
                if (nextMapId !== null) {
                    let gates = Engine.map.gateways.getList();
                    let celBramka = gates.find(g => g.d && (parseInt(g.d.target) === nextMapId || parseInt(g.d.id) === nextMapId));

                    if (celBramka) {
                        let dX = Math.abs(graczX - celBramka.d.x);
                        let dY = Math.abs(graczY - celBramka.d.y);

                        if (dX > 1 || dY > 1) {
                            Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: celBramka.d.x, y: celBramka.d.y });
                            lastActionTime = nowTimePath + 800;
                        } else {
                            forceInteract(celBramka);
                            console.log(`[Bot] Podążam trasą. Przechodzę na mapę: ${nextMapId}`);
                            lastActionTime = nowTimePath + 2500;
                        }
                    } else {
                        console.warn(`[Bot] Na trasie, ale nie widzę bramki na mapę ${nextMapId}!`);
                        if (pathStatusEl) pathStatusEl.innerText = `Brak przejścia do ${nextMapId}`;
                        lastActionTime = nowTimePath + 1000;
                    }
                } else {
                    console.warn(`[Bot] Zgubiłem się! Obecna mapa (${currentMap}) nie należy do trasy.`);
                    if (pathStatusEl) {
                        pathStatusEl.innerText = `Zgubiono trasę!`;
                        pathStatusEl.style.color = "#e74c3c";
                    }
                    lastActionTime = nowTimePath + 2000;
                }
                break;

            case 'hunt':
                let nowTime = Date.now();
                if (step.killedCount === undefined) step.killedCount = 0;

                let uiKills = -1, uiTarget = step.targetCount || 0, uiDone = false;
                let missionElements = document.querySelectorAll('.one-quest-mission.mission-type-2 .one-name');
                for (let el of missionElements) {
                    let text = el.innerText.trim();
                    let searchPhrases = step.uiName ? [step.uiName] : step.mobs;
                    if (searchPhrases.some(m => text.toLowerCase().includes(m.toLowerCase()))) {
                        if (el.closest('.one-quest-mission').classList.contains('quest-done')) uiDone = true;
                        let match = text.match(/\((\d+)\/(\d+)\)/);
                        if (match) { uiKills = parseInt(match[1], 10); uiTarget = parseInt(match[2], 10); }
                        break;
                    }
                }
                if (uiKills !== -1) { step.killedCount = uiKills; step.targetCount = uiTarget; }

                if (uiDone || (step.targetCount > 0 && step.killedCount >= step.targetCount)) {
                    console.log(`[Hunt] Quest ukończony!`);
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = nowTime + 500;
                    break;
                }

                let npcs = Object.values(Engine.npcs.check());
                let kandydaci = [];

                // Dodano wyliczanie matematycznego dystansu w pierwszej kolejności
                for (let n of npcs) {
                    if (n.d && (n.d.type === 2 || n.d.type === 3) && step.mobs.some(m => n.d.nick.toLowerCase().includes(m.toLowerCase()))) {
                        let prosta = Math.abs(graczX - n.d.x) + Math.abs(graczY - n.d.y);
                        kandydaci.push({ obj: n, prosta: prosta });
                    }
                }

                // Optymalizacja A* z poprzednich wersji:
                kandydaci.sort((a, b) => a.prosta - b.prosta);

                let tMob = null;
                let minDystans = Infinity;

                for (let mob of kandydaci) {
                    if (mob.prosta >= minDystans) break;
                    let sciezka = szukajDrogi(graczX, graczY, mob.obj.d.x, mob.obj.d.y, czyPoleZablokowane);
                    if (sciezka !== null) {
                        let dystansKrokowy = sciezka.length;
                        if (dystansKrokowy < minDystans) {
                            minDystans = dystansKrokowy;
                            tMob = mob.obj;
                        }
                    }
                }

                let isMoving = (Engine.hero.opt && Engine.hero.opt.go);

                if (tMob) {
                    let dX = Math.abs(graczX - tMob.d.x);
                    let dY = Math.abs(graczY - tMob.d.y);

                    if (dX > 1 || dY > 1) {
                        if (!isMoving) {
                            console.log(`[Hunt] Biegnę do: ${tMob.d.nick} na [${tMob.d.x}, ${tMob.d.y}]`);
                            Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: tMob.d.x, y: tMob.d.y });
                            lastActionTime = nowTime + 1000;
                        } else {
                            lastActionTime = nowTime + 500;
                        }
                    } else {
                        // BOT DECYDUJE: Jeśli berserk OFF to bije ręcznie. Jeśli ON, tylko stoi.
                        if (!botBerserkActive) {
                            console.log(`[Hunt] Biję (Aktywny atak): ${tMob.d.nick}`);
                            forceInteract(tMob);
                            if (uiKills === -1) step.killedCount++;
                            lastActionTime = nowTime + 2000;
                        } else {
                            console.log(`[Hunt] Stoję i czekam aż zaatakuje mnie ${tMob.d.nick} (Berserk)...`);
                            lastActionTime = nowTime + 1000;
                        }
                    }
                } else {
                    console.log("[Hunt] Nie widzę mobów z bezpieczną ścieżką, szukam bramki.");
                    if(step.maps && step.maps.length > 0) {
                        if(step.currentRouteIndex === undefined) step.currentRouteIndex = 0;
                        let nextMapId = step.maps[step.currentRouteIndex + 1];
                        let gates = Engine.map.gateways.getList();
                        let celBramka = gates.find(g => g.d && (parseInt(g.d.target) === nextMapId || parseInt(g.d.id) === nextMapId));

                        if (celBramka) {
                            console.log(`[Hunt] Idę do bramki na mapę: ${nextMapId}`);
                            Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: celBramka.d.x, y: celBramka.d.y });
                            lastActionTime = nowTime + 1000;
                        } else {
                            step.currentRouteIndex = (step.currentRouteIndex + 1) % step.maps.length;
                            lastActionTime = nowTime + 1000;
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;

            case 'bramka':
                if (currentMap === step.targetMapId) {
                    console.log(`[Bot] Jesteśmy na mapie: ${step.targetMapId}. Przechodzę dalej.`);
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                    break;
                }
                let gates = Engine.map.gateways.getList();
                let celBramka = gates.find(b =>
                    b.d &&
                    (parseInt(b.d.id) === step.targetMapId || parseInt(b.d.target) === step.targetMapId)
                );

                if (celBramka) {
                    let dX = Math.abs(graczX - celBramka.d.x);
                    let dY = Math.abs(graczY - celBramka.d.y);

                    if (dX > 1 || dY > 1) {
                        Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: celBramka.d.x, y: celBramka.d.y });
                        lastActionTime = now + 800;
                    } else {
                        forceInteract(celBramka);
                        console.log(`[Bot] Kliknięto bramkę prowadzącą do ID: ${step.targetMapId}`);
                        lastActionTime = now + 2500;
                    }
                } else if (step.x !== undefined && step.y !== undefined) {
                    Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: step.x, y: step.y });
                    lastActionTime = now + 800;
                } else {
                    console.warn(`[Bot] Nie widzę bramki o ID: ${step.targetMapId}`);
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                }
                break;

            case 'sleep':
                let sleepTime = step.time || 1000;
                console.log(`[Bot] Śpię przez ${sleepTime}ms`);
                lastActionTime = now + sleepTime;
                currentStepIndex++;
                break;

            case 'craft_close':
                let craftCloseBtn = document.querySelector('.barter-window.window-on-peak .close-button');
                if (craftCloseBtn) {
                    craftCloseBtn.click();
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                } else {
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                }
                break;

            case 'craft_use':
                let allButtons = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.button'));
                let useBtn = allButtons.find(b => b.innerText.trim() === "Użyj");
                if (useBtn) {
                    useBtn.click();
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                } else {
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                }
                break;

            case 'craft_item':
                let recipes = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.crafting-recipe-in-list'));
                let targetRecipe = recipes.find(el => {
                    let nameEl = el.querySelector('.name');
                    return nameEl && nameEl.innerText.includes(step.itemName);
                });

                if (targetRecipe) {
                    if (targetRecipe.classList.contains('active')) {
                        let craftBtn = document.querySelector('.do-recipe');
                        if (craftBtn) {
                            craftBtn.click();
                            currentStepIndex++;
                            lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                        } else {
                            lastActionTime = now + 500;
                        }
                    } else {
                        targetRecipe.click();
                        lastActionTime = now + 500;
                    }
                } else {
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                }
                break;

            case 'move_bag':
                let sourceItem = document.querySelector(`.item-tpl-${step.tpl}`);
                let targetSlot = document.querySelector(`.${step.target}`);
                if (sourceItem && targetSlot) {
                    let sRect = sourceItem.getBoundingClientRect();
                    let tRect = targetSlot.getBoundingClientRect();
                    sourceItem.dispatchEvent(new MouseEvent('mousedown', { bubbles: true, clientX: sRect.left + 16, clientY: sRect.top + 16 }));
                    document.dispatchEvent(new MouseEvent('mousemove', { bubbles: true, clientX: tRect.left + 16, clientY: tRect.top + 16 }));
                    targetSlot.dispatchEvent(new MouseEvent('mouseup', { bubbles: true, clientX: tRect.left + 16, clientY: tRect.top + 16 }));
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                } else {
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                }
                break;

            case 'shop_close':
                let allWindows = document.querySelectorAll('.c-window');
                let shopWindow = Array.from(allWindows).find(win => {
                    let header = win.querySelector('.header-label .text');
                    return header && header.innerText.includes("Sklep");
                });

                if (shopWindow) {
                    let closeBtn = shopWindow.querySelector('.close-button-corner-decor .close-button');
                    if (closeBtn) {
                        closeBtn.click();
                        currentStepIndex++;
                        lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                    } else {
                        currentStepIndex++;
                        lastActionTime = now + 500;
                    }
                } else {
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                }
                break;

            case 'shop_buy':
                let itemToBuy = document.querySelector(`.shop-items .item-id-${step.itemId}`);
                if (itemToBuy) {
                    itemToBuy.click();
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                } else {
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                }
                break;

            case 'shop_accept':
                let acceptBtn = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.finalize-button .button'))
                                     .find(el => el.innerText.includes("Akceptuj"));

                if (acceptBtn) {
                    acceptBtn.click();
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                } else {
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                }
                break;

            case 'alert_confirm':
                let btnClass = (step.option === 'no') ? '.alert-cancel-hotkey' : '.alert-accept-hotkey';
                let alertBtn = document.querySelector(btnClass);

                if (alertBtn) {
                    if (step.forceSave) {
                        // -- OPCJA 1: OKNO ODŚWIEŻA GRĘ --
                        // Wymuszamy twardy zapis do pamięci przeglądarki przed samym kliknięciem
                        currentStepIndex++;
                        localStorage.setItem('margo_quest_step_' + currentQuestName, currentStepIndex);
                        updateDisplay();

                        alertBtn.click(); // Po tym gra zrobi F5, ale my mamy już zapisany krok
                        lastActionTime = now + 5000; // Dajemy dużo czasu, bo strona zgaśnie
                    } else {
                        // -- OPCJA 2: STANDARDOWE OKNO --
                        // Działa asynchronicznie, bez przeładowania całej gry
                        alertBtn.click();
                        currentStepIndex++;
                        lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                    }
                } else {
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                }
                break;

            case 'choose_prof':
                let outfitCards = document.querySelectorAll('.outfit-card');

                if (outfitCards.length > 0) {
                    let targetCard = Array.from(outfitCards).find(card => {
                        let textEl = card.querySelector('.text');
                        return textEl && textEl.innerText.trim().toLowerCase() === step.profName.toLowerCase();
                    });

                    if (targetCard) {
                        let borderEl = targetCard.querySelector('.outfit-border');

                        if (borderEl && borderEl.classList.contains('active')) {
                            let confirmBtn = document.querySelector('.button.confirmButton');

                            if (confirmBtn && !confirmBtn.classList.contains('disable')) {
                                confirmBtn.click();
                                currentStepIndex++;
                                lastActionTime = now + 1500;
                            } else {
                                lastActionTime = now + 300;
                            }
                        } else {
                            targetCard.click();
                            lastActionTime = now + 500;
                        }
                    } else {
                        lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                    }
                } else {
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                }
                break;

            case 'follow_arrow':
                if (!window._celQuesta && typeof Engine.targets.getTargets === 'function') {
                    let tgts = Engine.targets.getTargets();
                    let k = Object.keys(tgts)[0];
                    if (k && tgts[k]) window._celQuesta = { x: tgts[k].x, y: tgts[k].y };
                }

                if (window._celQuesta) {
                    let cel = window._celQuesta;
                    let distX = Math.abs(graczX - cel.x);
                    let distY = Math.abs(graczY - cel.y);

                    // Zastosowano Skaner Ścian zamiast starego Engine.map.col.check()
                    let isCollision = czyPoleZablokowane(cel.x, cel.y);
                    let targetDist = isCollision ? 1 : 0;

                    if (distX <= targetDist && distY <= targetDist) {
                        currentStepIndex++;
                        lastActionTime = now + 500;
                    } else {
                        Engine.hero.autoGoTo(cel);
                        lastActionTime = now + 800;
                    }
                } else {
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                }
                break;

            // ==================================================
            // CASE: RUCH NA WSPÓŁRZĘDNE
            // ==================================================
            case 'move': {
                let mDistX = Math.abs(graczX - step.x);
                let mDistY = Math.abs(graczY - step.y);

                // Jeśli jesteśmy dokładnie na docelowym polu (0 dystansu)
                if (mDistX === 0 && mDistY === 0) {
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 200;
                } else {
                    Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: step.x, y: step.y });
                    lastActionTime = now + 800; // Lekko skrócony czas, by bot szedł płynniej
                }
                break;
            }

            case 'talk':
                let npcsTalk = Object.values(Engine.npcs.check()).filter(n => n.d && n.d.nick.toLowerCase().includes(step.nick.toLowerCase()));
                let gws = Engine.map.gateways.getList().filter(g => g.d && g.tip && g.tip[0].toLowerCase().includes(step.nick.toLowerCase()));

                let talkCandidates = [
                    ...npcsTalk.map(n => ({ d: n.d, obj: n, type: 'npc' })),
                    ...gws.map(g => ({ d: g.d, obj: g, type: 'gateway' }))
                ];

                if (step.x !== undefined && step.y !== undefined) {
                    talkCandidates = talkCandidates.filter(c => c.d.x === step.x && c.d.y === step.y);
                }

                // Dodano logikę zoptymalizowanego A* do podchodzenia do NPC
                talkCandidates.forEach(c => {
                    c.prosta = Math.abs(graczX - c.d.x) + Math.abs(graczY - c.d.y);
                });
                talkCandidates.sort((a, b) => a.prosta - b.prosta);

                let tTarget = null;
                let minTalkDist = Infinity;

                for (let c of talkCandidates) {
                    if (c.prosta >= minTalkDist) break;
                    let sciezka = szukajDrogi(graczX, graczY, c.d.x, c.d.y, czyPoleZablokowane);
                    if (sciezka !== null) {
                        if (sciezka.length < minTalkDist) {
                            minTalkDist = sciezka.length;
                            tTarget = c;
                        }
                    }
                }

                if (tTarget) {
                    let dX = Math.abs(graczX - tTarget.d.x);
                    let dY = Math.abs(graczY - tTarget.d.y);

                    if (dX > 1 || dY > 1) {
                        Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: tTarget.d.x, y: tTarget.d.y });
                        lastActionTime = now + 800;
                    } else {
                        let interactObj = (tTarget.type === 'npc') ? tTarget.obj : { d: tTarget.d, onclick: tTarget.obj.onclick };
                        forceInteract(interactObj);
                        currentStepIndex++;
                        lastActionTime = now + 1500;
                    }
                } else {
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                }
                break;

            case 'attack':
                let npcsAttack = Object.values(Engine.npcs.check());
                let aTarget = null;

                if (step.targetId) {
                    aTarget = npcsAttack.find(n => n.d && n.d.id === step.targetId);
                } else {
                    // Dodano logikę zoptymalizowanego A* dla precyzyjnego ataku
                    let candidates = npcsAttack.filter(n => {
                        if (!n.d || !(n.d.type === 2 || n.d.type === 3) || !n.d.nick.toLowerCase().includes(step.nick.toLowerCase())) return false;
                        if (step.x !== undefined && step.y !== undefined) {
                            return n.d.x === step.x && n.d.y === step.y;
                        }
                        return true;
                    }).map(n => ({ obj: n, prosta: Math.abs(graczX - n.d.x) + Math.abs(graczY - n.d.y) }));

                    candidates.sort((a,b) => a.prosta - b.prosta);
                    let minAttackDist = Infinity;

                    for(let c of candidates) {
                        if(c.prosta >= minAttackDist) break;
                        let sciezka = szukajDrogi(graczX, graczY, c.obj.d.x, c.obj.d.y, czyPoleZablokowane);
                        if (sciezka !== null) {
                            if(sciezka.length < minAttackDist) {
                                minAttackDist = sciezka.length;
                                aTarget = c.obj;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    if (aTarget) step.targetId = aTarget.d.id;
                }

                if (aTarget) {
                    let dX = Math.abs(graczX - aTarget.d.x);
                    let dY = Math.abs(graczY - aTarget.d.y);

                    if (dX > 1 || dY > 1) {
                        Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: aTarget.d.x, y: aTarget.d.y });
                        lastActionTime = now + 800;
                    } else {
                        forceInteract(aTarget);
                        lastActionTime = now + 2000;
                    }
                } else {
                    if (step.targetId) {
                        console.log(`[Bot] Cel pokonany! Przechodzę dalej.`);
                        currentStepIndex++;
                        delete step.targetId;
                        lastActionTime = now + 500;
                    } else {
                        let questStatus = document.getElementById('quest-bot-status');
                        if (questStatus) questStatus.innerText = "Czekam na potwora...";
                        lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                    }
                }
                break;

            case 'equip':
                let itemElement = document.querySelector(`.item-tpl-${step.tpl}.inventory-item`);
                if (itemElement) {
                    let event = new MouseEvent('dblclick', { bubbles: true, cancelable: true, view: window });
                    itemElement.dispatchEvent(event);
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                } else {
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                }
                break;

            case 'dialog':
                let opcje = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.dialogue-window-answer, .dialog-answer, .answer'))
                                 .filter(el => el.offsetParent !== null);

                if (opcje.length > 0) {
                    if (typeof Engine !== 'undefined' && Engine.dialogue && typeof Engine.dialogue.choose === 'function') {
                        try {
                            Engine.dialogue.choose(step.option - 1);
                            currentStepIndex++;
                            lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                            break;
                        } catch(e) {}
                    }

                    if (opcje.length >= step.option) {
                        opcje[step.option - 1].click();
                        currentStepIndex++;
                        lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                    } else {
                        lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                    }
                } else {
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                }
                break;

            case 'wait_map':
                if (Engine.map && Engine.map.d && Engine.map.d.name.includes(step.mapName)) {
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                } else {
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                }
                break;

            case 'berserk':
                let isEnabled = step.enabled !== false;
                let targetLvl = step.lvl || 1;
                let heroLvl = getHeroLevel();
                let minLvl = targetLvl - heroLvl;
                let maxLvl = 13;

                // Zapisujemy w pamięci bota stan berserka - to kontroluje czy bot sam klika
                botBerserkActive = isEnabled;

                if (typeof window._g === 'function') {
                    window._g(`settings&action=update&id=34&v=${isEnabled ? 1 : 0}`);
                    window._g(`settings&action=update&id=35&v=${isEnabled ? 1 : 0}`);

                    if (isEnabled) {
                        window._g(`settings&action=update&id=34&key=lvlmin&v=${minLvl}`);
                        window._g(`settings&action=update&id=35&key=lvlmin&v=${minLvl}`);
                        window._g(`settings&action=update&id=34&key=lvlmax&v=${maxLvl}`);
                        window._g(`settings&action=update&id=35&key=lvlmax&v=${maxLvl}`);
                    }
                }

                console.log(`[Bot] Berserk: ${isEnabled ? 'WŁ (Od: ' + targetLvl + ' lvl)' : 'WYŁ'}`);

                currentStepIndex++;
                lastActionTime = now + 500;
                break;
        }
    }

    // ==========================================
    // INICJALIZACJA I UI
    // ==========================================
    function initBot() {
        let initTimer = setInterval(() => {
            if (typeof Engine !== 'undefined' && Engine.targets) {
                clearInterval(initTimer);

                const origAdd = Engine.targets.addArrow;
                const origDel = Engine.targets.deleteArrow;

                Engine.targets.addArrow = function(...args) {
                    if (args[2] && args[2].x !== undefined) {
                        window._celQuesta = { x: args[2].x, y: args[2].y };
                    }
                    return origAdd.apply(this, args);
                };

                Engine.targets.deleteArrow = function(id) {
                    window._celQuesta = null;
                    return origDel.apply(this, arguments);
                };

                createUI();
            }
        }, 1000);
    }

    function createUI() {
        let savedX = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('margo_quest_x'), 10) || 20;
        let savedY = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('margo_quest_y'), 10) || 350;

        const menuHTML = `
            <div id="quest-bot-menu" style="position: fixed; top: ${savedY}px; left: ${savedX}px; z-index: 999999; background: rgba(20, 20, 20, 0.95); border: 2px solid #f39c12; color: #fff; font-family: Tahoma, sans-serif; font-size: 11px; padding: 12px; border-radius: 6px; width: 190px; box-shadow: 0 0 10px rgba(0,0,0,0.8);">
                <div id="quest-bot-header" style="cursor: move; user-select: none; font-weight: bold; text-align: center; margin-bottom: 8px; border-bottom: 1px solid #444; padding-bottom: 5px; color: #f39c12;">Quest Bot Multi (A*) 📜</div>
                <div id="quest-bot-status" style="text-align: center; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: #7f8c8d;">Wstrzymano</div>
                <div id="quest-bot-step" style="text-align: center; color: #3498db; font-size: 10px; margin-bottom: 8px; min-height: 25px; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center;">Gotowy do rozpoczęcia</div>

                <div style="margin-bottom: 6px;">
                    <label style="font-size: 9px; color: #aaa; display:block; margin-bottom:2px;">Wybierz Quest:</label>
                    <select id="quest-active-select" style="width: 100%; padding: 4px; background: #34495e; color: #ecf0f1; border: 1px solid #2c3e50; border-radius: 4px; font-size: 10px; cursor: pointer;">
                    </select>
                </div>

                <div style="margin-bottom: 10px;">
                    <label style="font-size: 9px; color: #aaa; display:block; margin-bottom:2px;">Krok zadania:</label>
                    <select id="quest-step-select" style="width: 100%; padding: 4px; background: #2c3e50; color: #ecf0f1; border: 1px solid #34495e; border-radius: 4px; font-size: 10px; cursor: pointer;">
                    </select>
                </div>

                <div style="display: flex; gap: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px;">
                    <button id="quest-prev-btn" title="Cofnij o jeden krok" style="flex: 1; padding: 6px; border: none; border-radius: 4px; cursor: pointer; background: #34495e; color: #fff;">⏪</button>
                    <button id="quest-toggle-btn" style="flex: 2; padding: 6px; border: none; border-radius: 4px; cursor: pointer; font-weight: bold; background: #27ae60; color: #fff;">▶ START</button>
                    <button id="quest-next-btn" title="Pomiń krok" style="flex: 1; padding: 6px; border: none; border-radius: 4px; cursor: pointer; background: #34495e; color: #fff;">⏩</button>
                </div>

                <div style="display: flex; gap: 5px;">
                    <button id="quest-reset-btn" style="width: 100%; padding: 4px; border: none; border-radius: 4px; cursor: pointer; font-weight: bold; background: #c0392b; color: #fff;">↺ RESET OD NOWA</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;

        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.innerHTML = menuHTML;
        document.body.appendChild(div);

        const questSelect = document.getElementById('quest-active-select');
        questNames.forEach(name => {
            let opt = document.createElement('option');
            opt.value = name;
            opt.innerText = name;
            if(name === currentQuestName) opt.selected = true;
            questSelect.appendChild(opt);
        });

        rebuildStepSelect();

        questSelect.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            currentQuestName = e.target.value;
            localStorage.setItem('margo_quest_active_name', currentQuestName);

            // Pobieramy zapamiętany krok dla NOWO wybranego questa
            currentStepIndex = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('margo_quest_step_' + currentQuestName), 10) || 0;
            const sequence = getActiveSequence();
            if (currentStepIndex >= sequence.length) currentStepIndex = 0;

            sequence.forEach(s => { if(s.targetId) delete s.targetId; });
            rebuildStepSelect();
            updateDisplay();
        });

        document.getElementById('quest-step-select').addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            currentStepIndex = parseInt(e.target.value, 10);
            updateDisplay();
        });

        document.getElementById('quest-toggle-btn').addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            const sequence = getActiveSequence();
            if (currentStepIndex >= sequence.length) return;

            isRunning = !isRunning;
            if (isRunning) {
                // Gdy startujemy bota, domyślnie przyjmujemy że aktywnie atakuje
                botBerserkActive = false;
                e.target.innerHTML = "⏸ PAUZA";
                e.target.style.background = "#e67e22";
                document.getElementById('quest-bot-status').innerText = "W Trakcie...";
                document.getElementById('quest-bot-status').style.color = "#f39c12";
                sequenceInterval = setInterval(processSequence, 300);
            } else {
                e.target.innerHTML = "▶ START";
                e.target.style.background = "#27ae60";
                document.getElementById('quest-bot-status').innerText = "Wstrzymano";
                document.getElementById('quest-bot-status').style.color = "#7f8c8d";
                clearInterval(sequenceInterval);
            }
        });

        document.getElementById('quest-prev-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {
            if (currentStepIndex > 0) { currentStepIndex--; updateDisplay(); }
        });

        document.getElementById('quest-next-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {
            const sequence = getActiveSequence();
            if (currentStepIndex < sequence.length - 1) { currentStepIndex++; updateDisplay(); }
        });

        document.getElementById('quest-reset-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {
            isRunning = false;
            clearInterval(sequenceInterval);
            currentStepIndex = 0;
            const sequence = getActiveSequence();
            sequence.forEach(s => { if(s.targetId) delete s.targetId; });
            document.getElementById('quest-toggle-btn').innerHTML = "▶ START";
            document.getElementById('quest-toggle-btn').style.background = "#27ae60";
            document.getElementById('quest-bot-status').innerText = "Zresetowano";
            document.getElementById('quest-bot-status').style.color = "#7f8c8d";
            updateDisplay();
        });

        updateDisplay();

        // Przeciąganie okna
        const menuEl = document.getElementById('quest-bot-menu');
        const headerEl = document.getElementById('quest-bot-header');
        let isDragging = false, offsetX = 0, offsetY = 0;

        headerEl.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
            if(['BUTTON', 'SELECT', 'OPTION'].includes(e.target.tagName)) return;
            isDragging = true;
            offsetX = e.clientX - menuEl.getBoundingClientRect().left;
            offsetY = e.clientY - menuEl.getBoundingClientRect().top;
        });
        document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => { if (isDragging) { menuEl.style.left = (e.clientX - offsetX) + 'px'; menuEl.style.top = (e.clientY - offsetY) + 'px'; } });
        document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => { if (isDragging) { isDragging = false; localStorage.setItem('margo_quest_x', parseInt(menuEl.style.left, 10)); localStorage.setItem('margo_quest_y', parseInt(menuEl.style.top, 10)); } });
    }

    // ==========================================
    // ANTY-CAPTCHA (Nasłuchiwanie ręcznego kliknięcia)
    // ==========================================
    document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        let btn = e.target.closest('.captcha-pre-info__button .button');
        if (btn && btn.innerText.includes("Rozwiąż")) {
            if (isRunning) {
                console.log("[Bot] Ręczne wywołanie captchy! Automatyczna pauza.");
                let toggleBtn = document.getElementById('quest-toggle-btn');
                if (toggleBtn) toggleBtn.click(); // Symuluje wciśnięcie PAUZY w UI bota

                let statusEl = document.getElementById('quest-bot-status');
                if (statusEl) {
                    statusEl.innerText = "Wstrzymano (CAPTCHA)";
                    statusEl.style.color = "#e74c3c";
                }
            }
        }
    });

    initBot();

})();

// ==UserScript==
// @name         MargoPack - Panel Dodatków
// @version      2.0
// @description  Zbiór dodatków z panelem zarządzania (Dark Motyw, Ramki, HUD, Nametagi i inne)
// @author       Gemini & Authors of scripts
// @match        http://*.margonem.pl/*
// @match        https://*.margonem.pl/*
// @match        http://*.margonem.com/*
// @match        https://*.margonem.com/*
// @grant        none
// ==/UserScript==

(function($) {
    'use strict';

    // ==========================================
    // KONFIGURACJA I ZARZĄDZANIE
    // ==========================================

    const STORAGE_KEY = 'margo_pack_config_v1';
    
    // Domyślne ustawienia
    const defaults = {
        hud: true,          // Procenty HP/EXP
        yellowExp: true,    // Żółty komunikat expa
        msgMove: true,      // Komunikaty wyżej (fade)
        borders: true,      // Ramki itemów
        darkTheme: true,    // Motyw Dark
        nametags: true,     // Lepsze nametagi
        hpBar: true         // Pasek HP nad postacią
    };

    // Pobranie ustawień
    let config = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY)) || defaults;

    const saveConfig = () => {
        localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(config));
        message('<span style="color:lime">Zapisano ustawienia! Odśwież stronę (F5), aby zastosować zmiany.</span>');
    };

    // Globalne utility (używane przez kilka modułów)
    Math.decimal = function(a, b) {
        var c = Math.pow(10, b);
        var d = Math.round(a * c) / c;
        return d;
    };

    // ==========================================
    // INTERFEJS PANELU
    // ==========================================

    const createPanel = () => {
        // Style panelu
        $('<style>').text(`
            #margoPackBtn { position: absolute; top: 5px; right: 250px; z-index: 400; cursor: pointer; background: url(https://i.imgur.com/PdbX48r.png) -368px 0; width: 20px; height: 20px; border: 1px solid #444; border-radius: 3px; box-shadow: 0 0 5px #000; }
            #margoPackBtn:hover { filter: brightness(1.2); }
            #margoPackPanel { display: none; position: absolute; top: 50%; left: 50%; transform: translate(-50%, -50%); width: 300px; background: #1a1a1a; border: 2px solid #444; color: #eee; z-index: 999; padding: 10px; font-family: Arial, sans-serif; box-shadow: 0 0 15px #000; }
            #margoPackPanel h3 { text-align: center; margin: 0 0 10px 0; color: gold; border-bottom: 1px solid #444; padding-bottom: 5px; }
            .mp-option { margin-bottom: 8px; display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background: #222; padding: 5px; border-radius: 4px; }
            .mp-option:hover { background: #2a2a2a; }
            .mp-btn { display: block; width: 100%; padding: 8px; margin-top: 10px; background: #2c5e2e; color: white; border: none; cursor: pointer; text-align: center; font-weight: bold; }
            .mp-btn:hover { background: #3c7e3e; }
            .mp-close { position: absolute; top: 5px; right: 10px; cursor: pointer; color: #888; }
            .mp-close:hover { color: #fff; }
        `).appendTo('head');

        // Przycisk otwierający
        $('<div id="margoPackBtn" tip="Panel Dodatków"></div>').appendTo('body').click(() => {
            $('#margoPackPanel').fadeToggle();
        });

        // HTML Panelu
        let panelHtml = `<div id="margoPackPanel"><div class="mp-close">X</div><h3>Panel Dodatków</h3>`;
        
        const labels = {
            hud: "Procenty HP/EXP (Paski)",
            yellowExp: "Żółty komunikat EXP",
            msgMove: "Lepsze komunikaty (Fade)",
            borders: "Ramki Itemów (Peszosła)",
            darkTheme: "Motyw Margo Dark",
            nametags: "Lepsze Nicki (Kolory)",
            hpBar: "Pasek HP nad postacią"
        };

        for (let key in defaults) {
            let checked = config[key] ? 'checked' : '';
            panelHtml += `
                <div class="mp-option">
                    <span>${labels[key]}</span>
                    <input type="checkbox" id="mp_chk_${key}" ${checked}>
                </div>
            `;
        }

        panelHtml += `<button class="mp-btn" id="mpSave">ZAPISZ I ZAMKNIJ</button></div>`;
        $('body').append(panelHtml);

        // Obsługa zdarzeń
        $('#margoPackPanel .mp-close').click(() => $('#margoPackPanel').fadeOut());
        
        $('#mpSave').click(() => {
            for (let key in defaults) {
                config[key] = $(`#mp_chk_${key}`).is(':checked');
            }
            saveConfig();
            $('#margoPackPanel').fadeOut();
        });
    };

    // ==========================================
    // MODULES (Kod użytkownika podzielony na części)
    // ==========================================

    const Modules = {
        hud: function() {
            window.setProcentValue = function() {
                //Procent życia
                var life = Math.decimal(hero.hp / hero.maxhp * 100, 1);
                //Procent expa
                var exp1 = Math.pow(hero.lvl - 1, 4);
                var exp2 = Math.pow(hero.lvl, 4);
                var exp = Math.decimal((hero.exp - exp1) / (exp2 - exp1) * 100, 1);
                //Uaktualnienie pasków
                $("#hpProcent").html(life + "%").attr("tip", $("#life1").attr("tip"));
                $("#expProcent").html(exp + "%").attr("tip", $("#exp1").attr("tip"));
            };
            $("<span id='hpProcent'></span>").css({position: 'absolute','z-index': '303',width: 114,textAlign: 'center','font-size': '10px'}).appendTo("#life1");
            $("<span id='expProcent'></span>").css({position: 'absolute','z-index': '303',width: 114,textAlign: 'center','font-size': '10px'}).appendTo("#exp1");
            setInterval(setProcentValue, 200);
        },

        yellowExp: function() {
            window.pexp = function(ile) {
                return Math.decimal(Math.decimal((hero.exp + ile - Math.pow(hero.lvl - 1, 4)) / (Math.pow(hero.lvl, 4) - Math.pow(hero.lvl - 1, 4)) * 100, 5) - Math.decimal((hero.exp - Math.pow(hero.lvl - 1, 4)) / (Math.pow(hero.lvl, 4) - Math.pow(hero.lvl - 1, 4)) * 100, 5), 2);
            };
            var tmpBattleMsgUhoa = battleMsg;
            window.battleMsg = function(c, t) {
                var ret = tmpBattleMsgUhoa(c, t);
                if (c.search(/\+exp=/) >= 0) {
                    var ile = c.slice(c.search("exp=") + 4);
                    message("+" + ile + "(" + pexp(parseInt(ile)) + "%)");
                }
                return ret;
            }
        },

        msgMove: function() {
            var fafmess = message;
            window.message = function(c) {
                fafmess(c);
                log(c);
                $("#msg").css({top: parseInt($("#msg").css("top")) - 250})
            }
            window.fadeMsg = function() {
                for (var a in g.msg) {
                    if (typeof(g.msg[a]) == "function") { continue }
                    g.msg[a].t--;
                    var c = g.msg[a].t;
                    if (c > 0) {
                        if (c < 25 && !$.fx.off) { g.msg[a].e.css("opacity", c / 25) }
                    } else {
                        g.msg[a].e.remove();
                        delete g.msg[a];
                        $("#msg").absCenter();
                        $("#msg").css({top: parseInt($("#msg").css("top")) - 250})
                        for (var b in g.msg) { g.msg[b].s = false }
                    }
                }
            }
        },

                saveConfig: function(q) {
                    if (q) {
                        var d = new Date();
                        d.setTime(d.getTime() + 3600000 * 24 * 30);
                        setCookie("_BC", q, d);
                    }
                    $('#_BC_style').remove();
                    $('<style id="_BC_style">.itemHighlighter {background-image: url(' + (getCookie('_BC').search('http://') > -1 ? getCookie('_BC') : _BC.images[getCookie('_BC')][0]) + ') !important;}#_BC_config {overflow: auto; background: url(/img/paper512.jpg); width: 512px; height: 512px; position: absolute; z-index: 303; display: none; text-align: center;}#_BC_config h1 {position: relative; background: rgba(0,0,0,0.3);margin: 10px;padding:3px;font-family: Arial;font-size: 20px;font-weight: 400;} #_BC_config h1 div {font-size: 12px; position: absolute; left: 2px; top: 3px; color: black;}._BC_window {padding: 5px; display: inline-block; text-align: center; margin: 5px; border: 1px black dotted;color: black; font-size: 12px; font-family: arial;} ._BC_window.selected {background: rgba(100,100,0,0.3);} </style>').appendTo('head');
                },
                run: function() {
                    if (!getCookie('_BC')) { _BC.saveConfig('0'); } else { _BC.saveConfig(); }
                    $('<div id="_BC_config"></div>').appendTo('#centerbox');
                    $('<h1>Konfiguracja obramowań itemów</h1>').appendTo('#_BC_config');
                    $('<div>[zamknij]</div>').click(function() { $('#_BC_config').fadeOut(); }).appendTo('#_BC_config h1');
                    $('<span> [konfiguracja]</span>').css({cursor: 'pointer',fontSize: 12,color: 'red'}).click(function() { $('#_BC_config').show(); config_cancel(); }).appendTo('#cfg_options #opt13');
                    for (var i in _BC.images) {
                        $('<div class="_BC_window' + (getCookie('_BC') == i ? ' selected' : '') + '"' + (_BC.images[i][2] ? ' tip="' + _BC.images[i][2] + '"' : "") + ' iid="' + i + '"><img src="' + _BC.images[i][0] + '" /><br>Autor: <b>' + _BC.images[i][1] + '</b></div>').appendTo('#_BC_config');
                    }
                    $('._BC_window').off('click').on('click', function() {
                        var t = $(this);
                        $('._BC_window').removeClass('selected');
                        _BC.saveConfig(t.attr('iid'));
                        t.addClass('selected');
                    });
                }
            };
            _BC.run();
        },

                        if (e[i].nick !== undefined) {
                            if (e[i].relation === "fr") { $(`<style>#RelationBorder${e[i].id}{color: limegreen !important;}</style>`).appendTo('head'); }
                            if (e[i].relation === "cl-fr") { $(`<style>#RelationBorder${e[i].id}{color: limegreen !important;}</style>`).appendTo('head'); }
                            if (e[i].relation === "en") { $(`<style>#RelationBorder${e[i].id}{color: red !important;}</style>`).appendTo('head'); }
                            if (e[i].relation === "cl") { $(`<style>#RelationBorder${e[i].id}{color: limegreen !important;}</style>`).appendTo('head'); }
                            if (e[i].relation === "cl-en") { $(`<style>#RelationBorder${e[i].id}{color: red !important;}</style>`).appendTo('head'); }
                            
                            var AFK = e[i].stasis == "1" ? "[AFK] " : "";
                            var Zast = e[i].guest === "1" ? " [Z]" : "";
                            var ProfesjaNazwa = ({m: 'Mag', h: 'Łowca', b: 'Tancerz Ostrzy', w: 'Wojownik', t: 'Tropiciel', p: 'Paladyn'})[e[i].prof];
                            $('#other' + e[i].id).html('<div class="BoxNickname"><span class="Nametag" id="RelationBorder' + e[i].id + '" tip="' + ProfesjaNazwa + '"><b>' + AFK + '' + e[i].nick + ' ' + e[i].lvl + '' + e[i].prof + '' + Zast + '</b></span></div>');

        hpBar: function() {
            $(`<style id="soft-hp-style">
                .SoftHpBar { position: absolute; z-index: 500; font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 11px; font-weight: bold; color: white; text-shadow: 0 0 3px #000, 0 0 3px #000, 0 0 3px #000; text-align: center; left: 50%; transform: translateX(-50%); top: 52px; pointer-events: none; white-space: nowrap; }
            </style>`).appendTo('head');

            function refreshHpOverlay() {
                var $hero = $('#hero');
                if ($hero.length === 0 || typeof hero === "undefined") return;
                var $hpBar = $('#my-hp-bar');
                if ($hpBar.length === 0) {
                    $hero.append('<div id="my-hp-bar" class="SoftHpBar"></div>');
                    $hpBar = $('#my-hp-bar');
                }
                var percent = Math.floor((hero.hp / hero.maxhp) * 100);
                $hpBar.text(percent + '%');
                if (percent < 50) { $hpBar.css('color', '#ff4444'); } else { $hpBar.css('color', 'white'); }
            }
            setInterval(refreshHpOverlay, 200);
        }

    if (config.hpBar) Modules.hpBar();
