    // Inicjalizacja domyślnych wartości w localStorage
    const defaults = {
        'dom_min_lvl': '16', 'dom_max_lvl': '25', 'dom_maps': expowiska["Nieumarli Torneg (16-25)"].maps,
        'dom_blacklist': expowiska["Nieumarli Torneg (16-25)"].blacklist, 'dom_dojscie_maps': expowiska["Nieumarli Torneg (16-25)"].dojscie,
        'dom_dojscie_enabled': 'false', 'dom_dojscie_finished': 'false', 'dom_active': 'false', 'dom_step': '0'
    };
    Object.keys(defaults).forEach(k => { if (!localStorage.getItem(k)) localStorage.setItem(k, defaults[k]); });

    let ostatniaAkcja = 0;
    let lastMapId = 0;
    let lastHeroX = 0;
    let lastHeroY = 0;
    let stuckCounter = 0;
    let ostatniBerserk = 0;

    document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
        if (e.key === 'F9') {
            const menu = document.getElementById('bot-menu');
            if (menu) menu.style.display = (menu.style.display === 'none' ? 'block' : 'none');
        }
    });

    function czyDostepny(targetX, targetY) {
        if (typeof Engine !== 'undefined' && Engine.map && Engine.map.pathfinder) {
            const path = Engine.map.pathfinder.findPath(Engine.hero.d.x, Engine.hero.d.y, targetX, targetY);
            return path !== null && path.length > 0;
        }
        return true;
    }

    function stworzMenu() {
        const istniejaceMenu = document.getElementById('bot-menu');
        if (istniejaceMenu) istniejaceMenu.remove();

        const savedX = localStorage.getItem('dom_menu_x') || '20';
        const savedY = localStorage.getItem('dom_menu_y') || '20';

        const menuHTML = `
            <div id="bot-menu" style="position: fixed; top: ${savedY}px; left: ${savedX}px; z-index: 999999; background: rgba(20, 20, 20, 0.95); border: 2px solid #ff0055; color: #fff; font-family: 'Arial', sans-serif; font-size: 12px; padding: 12px; border-radius: 8px; width: 180px; box-shadow: 0 0 20px rgba(0,0,0,0.5);">
                <div id="bot-menu-header" style="cursor: move; user-select: none; font-weight: bold; text-align: center; margin-bottom: 8px; border-bottom: 1px solid #444; padding-bottom: 6px; color: #ff0055; font-size: 13px;">Bot v50.11 ⚡</div>
                <div id="bot-map-info" style="text-align: center; color: #3498db; font-size: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px; font-weight: bold;">Mapa: Ładowanie...</div>

                <div style="margin-bottom: 10px;">
                    <label style="display:block; margin-bottom: 4px;">Wybierz expowisko:</label>
                    <select id="exp-select" style="width: 100%; background: #333; color: #fff; border: 1px solid #555; padding: 4px; font-size: 11px;">
                        <option value="">-- Wybierz trasę --</option>
                        ${Object.keys(expowiska).map(name => `<option value="${name}">${name}</option>`).join('')}
                    </select>
                </div>

                <div style="margin-bottom: 6px;"><label>Min Lvl:</label><input type="number" id="dom-min" value="${localStorage.getItem('dom_min_lvl')}" style="width: 45px; float: right; background: #333; color: #fff; border: 1px solid #555; text-align: center;"></div>
                <div style="margin-bottom: 6px;"><label>Max Lvl:</label><input type="number" id="dom-max" value="${localStorage.getItem('dom_max_lvl')}" style="width: 45px; float: right; background: #333; color: #fff; border: 1px solid #555; text-align: center;"></div>

                <div style="margin-bottom: 10px; padding: 4px; border: 1px dashed #ff9900; border-radius: 4px; background: rgba(255, 153, 0, 0.1);">
                    <label style="display:block; margin-bottom: 4px; color: #ffcc00;"><input type="checkbox" id="dom-dojscie-toggle" ${localStorage.getItem('dom_dojscie_enabled') === 'true' ? 'checked' : ''}> Dojście (bez bicia):</label>
                    <textarea id="dom-dojscie-maps" style="width: 100%; height: 30px; background: #333; color: #fff; border: 1px solid #555; font-size: 11px; resize: vertical; box-sizing: border-box; padding: 4px;" placeholder="ID map dojścia...">${localStorage.getItem('dom_dojscie_maps')}</textarea>
                </div>

                <div style="margin-bottom: 10px;">
                    <label style="display:block; margin-bottom: 4px;">Trasa Główna (ID):</label>
                    <textarea id="dom-maps" style="width: 100%; height: 40px; background: #333; color: #fff; border: 1px solid #555; font-size: 11px; resize: vertical; box-sizing: border-box; padding: 4px;">${localStorage.getItem('dom_maps')}</textarea>
                </div>

                <div style="margin-bottom: 10px;">
                    <label style="display:block; margin-bottom: 4px;">Blacklista mobów (ID):</label>
                    <textarea id="dom-blacklist" style="width: 100%; height: 40px; background: #333; color: #fff; border: 1px solid #555; font-size: 11px; resize: vertical; box-sizing: border-box; padding: 4px;">${localStorage.getItem('dom_blacklist')}</textarea>
                </div>

                <button id="dom-toggle" style="width: 100%; padding: 6px; border: none; border-radius: 4px; cursor: pointer; font-weight: bold; background: ${localStorage.getItem('dom_active') === 'true' ? '#27ae60' : '#c0392b'}; color: #fff; margin-bottom: 5px;">${localStorage.getItem('dom_active') === 'true' ? 'WŁĄCZONY' : 'WYŁĄCZONY'}</button>
                <button id="dom-reset" style="width: 100%; padding: 4px; border: none; border-radius: 4px; cursor: pointer; font-weight: bold; background: #f39c12; color: #000;">RESET TRASY</button>
            </div>
        `;
        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.innerHTML = menuHTML;
        document.body.appendChild(div);

        document.getElementById('exp-select').addEventListener('change', function() {
            const exp = expowiska[this.value];
            if(exp) {
                document.getElementById('dom-maps').value = exp.maps;
                localStorage.setItem('dom_maps', exp.maps);
                document.getElementById('dom-blacklist').value = exp.blacklist;
                localStorage.setItem('dom_blacklist', exp.blacklist);
                const dojscieValue = exp.dojscie || "";
                document.getElementById('dom-dojscie-maps').value = dojscieValue;
                localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_maps', dojscieValue);
                const minLvl = exp.minLvl !== undefined ? exp.minLvl : 1;
                const maxLvl = exp.maxLvl !== undefined ? exp.maxLvl : 300;
                document.getElementById('dom-min').value = minLvl;
                localStorage.setItem('dom_min_lvl', minLvl);
                document.getElementById('dom-max').value = maxLvl;
                localStorage.setItem('dom_max_lvl', maxLvl);
            }
        });

        document.getElementById('dom-min').addEventListener('input', (e) => localStorage.setItem('dom_min_lvl', e.target.value));
        document.getElementById('dom-max').addEventListener('input', (e) => localStorage.setItem('dom_max_lvl', e.target.value));
        document.getElementById('dom-maps').addEventListener('input', (e) => localStorage.setItem('dom_maps', e.target.value));
        document.getElementById('dom-blacklist').addEventListener('input', (e) => localStorage.setItem('dom_blacklist', e.target.value));
        document.getElementById('dom-dojscie-maps').addEventListener('input', (e) => localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_maps', e.target.value));
        document.getElementById('dom-dojscie-toggle').addEventListener('change', (e) => localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_enabled', e.target.checked));

        document.getElementById('dom-toggle').addEventListener('click', function() {
            const stan = localStorage.getItem('dom_active') === 'true';
            localStorage.setItem('dom_active', (!stan).toString());
            this.innerText = !stan ? 'WŁĄCZONY' : 'WYŁĄCZONY';
            this.style.background = !stan ? '#27ae60' : '#c0392b';
        });

        document.getElementById('dom-reset').addEventListener('click', function() {
            if (typeof Engine !== 'undefined' && Engine.map && Engine.map.d) {
                const aktualnaMapaId = parseInt(Engine.map.d.id, 10);
                const isDojscieActive = localStorage.getItem('dom_dojscie_enabled') === 'true';
                const dojscieTrasa = (localStorage.getItem('dom_dojscie_maps') || "").split(/[\s,]+/).map(id => parseInt(id.trim(), 10)).filter(id => !isNaN(id));
                const mainTrasa = (localStorage.getItem('dom_maps') || "").split(/[\s,]+/).map(id => parseInt(id.trim(), 10)).filter(id => !isNaN(id));

                let indexDojscie = dojscieTrasa.indexOf(aktualnaMapaId);
                let indexMain = mainTrasa.indexOf(aktualnaMapaId);

                if (isDojscieActive && indexDojscie !== -1) {
                    localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_finished', 'false');
                    localStorage.setItem('dom_step', indexDojscie.toString());
                } else if (indexMain !== -1) {
                    if (isDojscieActive) localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_finished', 'true');
                    localStorage.setItem('dom_step', indexMain.toString());
                } else {
                    localStorage.setItem('dom_step', '0');
                    localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_finished', 'false');
                    alert(`Brak obecnej mapy (${aktualnaMapaId}) w Dojściu oraz Głównej Trasie.\nZresetowano wszystko do początku.`);
                }
            } else {
                localStorage.setItem('dom_step', '0');
                localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_finished', 'false');
                alert("Zresetowano krok trasy do zera.");
            }
        });

        const menuEl = document.getElementById('bot-menu');
        const headerEl = document.getElementById('bot-menu-header');
        let isDragging = false;
        let offsetX = 0; let offsetY = 0;
        headerEl.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => { isDragging = true; offsetX = e.clientX - menuEl.getBoundingClientRect().left; offsetY = e.clientY - menuEl.getBoundingClientRect().top; });
        document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => { if (isDragging) { menuEl.style.left = (e.clientX - offsetX) + 'px'; menuEl.style.top = (e.clientY - offsetY) + 'px'; } });
        document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => { if (isDragging) { isDragging = false; localStorage.setItem('dom_menu_x', parseInt(menuEl.style.left, 10)); localStorage.setItem('dom_menu_y', parseInt(menuEl.style.top, 10)); } });
    }

    function glownaLogikaAPI() {
        try {
            if (typeof Engine === 'undefined' || !Engine.hero || !Engine.npcs || !Engine.map) return;

            const teraz = Date.now();
            if (teraz < ostatniaAkcja) return;

            if (Engine.hero.opt && Engine.hero.opt.go) {
                if (Engine.hero.d.x === lastHeroX && Engine.hero.d.y === lastHeroY) {
                    stuckCounter++;
                } else {
                    stuckCounter = 0;
                }
                lastHeroX = Engine.hero.d.x;
                lastHeroY = Engine.hero.d.y;

                if (stuckCounter > 8) {
                    Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: Engine.hero.d.x + (Math.random() > 0.5 ? 3 : -3), y: Engine.hero.d.y + (Math.random() > 0.5 ? 3 : -3) });
                    stuckCounter = 0;
                    ostatniaAkcja = teraz + 1200;
                }
                return;
            }

            if (Engine.battle && Engine.battle.show) {
                const fastFightBtn = document.querySelector('.auto-fight-btn');
                if (fastFightBtn && fastFightBtn.offsetParent !== null) {
                    fastFightBtn.click();
                    ostatniaAkcja = teraz + 600;
                }
                return;
            }

            const isBotActive = localStorage.getItem('dom_active') === 'true';
            const aktualnaMapaId = parseInt(Engine.map.d.id, 10);

            if (aktualnaMapaId !== lastMapId) {
                const mapInfoEl = document.getElementById('bot-map-info');
                if (mapInfoEl) mapInfoEl.innerText = `Mapa: ${aktualnaMapaId}`;
            }

            const isDojscieActive = localStorage.getItem('dom_dojscie_enabled') === 'true';
            let isDojscieFinished = localStorage.getItem('dom_dojscie_finished') === 'true';

            let dojscieTrasa = (localStorage.getItem('dom_dojscie_maps') || "").split(/[\s,]+/).map(id => parseInt(id.trim(), 10)).filter(id => !isNaN(id));
            let mainTrasa = (localStorage.getItem('dom_maps') || "").split(/[\s,]+/).map(id => parseInt(id.trim(), 10)).filter(id => !isNaN(id));

            if (isDojscieActive && !isDojscieFinished && mainTrasa.includes(aktualnaMapaId)) {
                localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_finished', 'true');
                isDojscieFinished = true;
                localStorage.setItem('dom_step', mainTrasa.indexOf(aktualnaMapaId).toString());
            }

            const moznaBic = !(isDojscieActive && !isDojscieFinished);

            if (teraz - ostatniBerserk > 4000) {
                ostatniBerserk = teraz;
                if (isBotActive && moznaBic) {
                    const berserkIconDisabled = document.querySelector('div.gargonem-pocket-berserk-icon.disabled[tip-id="562"]');
                    if (berserkIconDisabled) berserkIconDisabled.click();
                } else {
                    const berserkIconEnabled = document.querySelector('div.gargonem-pocket-berserk-icon:not(.disabled)[tip-id="562"]');
                    if (berserkIconEnabled) berserkIconEnabled.click();
                }
            }

            if (!isBotActive) return;

            let trasa;
            if (isDojscieActive && !isDojscieFinished) {
                trasa = [...dojscieTrasa];
                if (mainTrasa.length > 0) trasa.push(mainTrasa[0]);
            } else {
                trasa = mainTrasa;
            }

            if (aktualnaMapaId !== lastMapId) {
                let currentStep = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('dom_step') || "0");
                if (currentStep >= trasa.length) currentStep = 0;
                let expectedNextMap = trasa[(currentStep + 1) % trasa.length];

                if (aktualnaMapaId === expectedNextMap) {
                    localStorage.setItem('dom_step', ((currentStep + 1) % trasa.length).toString());
                } else {
                    let idx = trasa.indexOf(aktualnaMapaId);
                    if (idx !== -1) localStorage.setItem('dom_step', idx.toString());
                }
                lastMapId = aktualnaMapaId;
            }

            let najblizszyMob = null;
            let minDystans = Infinity;

            if (moznaBic) {
                const minLvl = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('dom_min_lvl'), 10);
                const maxLvl = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('dom_max_lvl'), 10);
                const blacklist = localStorage.getItem('dom_blacklist').split(/[\s,]+/).filter(Boolean);

                for (const [idString, npc] of Object.entries(Engine.npcs.check())) {
                    if (blacklist.includes(idString)) continue;

                    if (npc.d && (npc.d.type === 2 || npc.d.type === 3) && npc.d.lvl >= minLvl && npc.d.lvl <= maxLvl) {
                        if (czyDostepny(npc.d.x, npc.d.y)) {
                            let dist = Math.max(Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.x - npc.d.x), Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.y - npc.d.y));
                            if (dist < minDystans) {
                                minDystans = dist;
                                najblizszyMob = { id: idString, name: npc.d.nick || npc.d.name || "Nieznany", x: npc.d.x, y: npc.d.y };
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            if (najblizszyMob) {
                Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: najblizszyMob.x, y: najblizszyMob.y });
                ostatniaAkcja = teraz + 700;
            } else {
                let currentStep = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('dom_step') || "0");
                if (currentStep >= trasa.length) currentStep = 0;
                let nextStep = (currentStep + 1) % trasa.length;
                let nastepnaMapaId = trasa[nextStep];
                let celBramka = Engine.map.gateways.getList().find(b => b.d && parseInt(b.d.id) === nastepnaMapaId);

                if (celBramka) {
                    let x = parseInt(celBramka.d.x);
                    let y = parseInt(celBramka.d.y);
                    let distToGateway = Math.max(Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.x - x), Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.y - y));

                    if (distToGateway === 0) {
                        ostatniaAkcja = teraz + 1500;
                        const range = 2;
                        const randomX = Engine.hero.d.x + (Math.floor(Math.random() * (range * 2 + 1)) - range);
                        const randomY = Engine.hero.d.y + (Math.floor(Math.random() * (range * 2 + 1)) - range);
                        Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: randomX, y: randomY });
                    } else if (distToGateway < 3) {
                        if (typeof celBramka.onclick === 'function') {
                            celBramka.onclick({ stopPropagation: ()=>{}, preventDefault: ()=>{} });
                        }
                        ostatniaAkcja = teraz + 3500;
                    } else {
                        Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: x, y: y });
                        ostatniaAkcja = teraz + 1500;
                    }
                }
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error("[AUTO-HUNTER ERROR]", error);
        }
    }

    setTimeout(stworzMenu, 2000);
    setInterval(glownaLogikaAPI, 350);
})();

    // Inicjalizacja domyślnych wartości w localStorage
    const defaults = {
        'dom_min_lvl': '16', 'dom_max_lvl': '25', 'dom_maps': expowiska["Nieumarli Torneg (16-25)"].maps,
        'dom_blacklist': expowiska["Nieumarli Torneg (16-25)"].blacklist, 'dom_dojscie_maps': expowiska["Nieumarli Torneg (16-25)"].dojscie,
        'dom_dojscie_enabled': 'false', 'dom_dojscie_finished': 'false', 'dom_active': 'false', 'dom_step': '0'
    };
    Object.keys(defaults).forEach(k => { if (!localStorage.getItem(k)) localStorage.setItem(k, defaults[k]); });

    let ostatniaAkcja = 0;
    let lastMapId = 0;
    let lastHeroX = 0;
    let lastHeroY = 0;
    let stuckCounter = 0;
    let ostatniBerserk = 0;

    document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
        if (e.key === 'F9') {
            const menu = document.getElementById('bot-menu');
            if (menu) menu.style.display = (menu.style.display === 'none' ? 'block' : 'none');
        }
    });

    function czyDostepny(targetX, targetY) {
        if (typeof Engine !== 'undefined' && Engine.map && Engine.map.pathfinder) {
            const path = Engine.map.pathfinder.findPath(Engine.hero.d.x, Engine.hero.d.y, targetX, targetY);
            return path !== null && path.length > 0;
        }
        return true;
    }

    function stworzMenu() {
        const istniejaceMenu = document.getElementById('bot-menu');
        if (istniejaceMenu) istniejaceMenu.remove();

        const savedY = localStorage.getItem('dom_menu_y') || '20';

        const menuHTML = `

                    <label style="display:block; margin-bottom: 4px;">Blacklista mobów (ID):</label>
                    <textarea id="dom-blacklist" style="width: 100%; height: 40px; background: #333; color: #fff; border: 1px solid #555; font-size: 11px; resize: vertical; box-sizing: border-box; padding: 4px;">${localStorage.getItem('dom_blacklist')}</textarea>
                </div>

                <button id="dom-toggle" style="width: 100%; padding: 6px; border: none; border-radius: 4px; cursor: pointer; font-weight: bold; background: ${localStorage.getItem('dom_active') === 'true' ? '#27ae60' : '#c0392b'}; color: #fff; margin-bottom: 5px;">${localStorage.getItem('dom_active') === 'true' ? 'WŁĄCZONY' : 'WYŁĄCZONY'}</button>
                <button id="dom-reset" style="width: 100%; padding: 4px; border: none; border-radius: 4px; cursor: pointer; font-weight: bold; background: #f39c12; color: #000;">RESET TRASY</button>
            </div>
        `;
        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.innerHTML = menuHTML;
        document.body.appendChild(div);

        document.getElementById('exp-select').addEventListener('change', function() {
            const exp = expowiska[this.value];
            if(exp) {
                document.getElementById('dom-maps').value = exp.maps;
                localStorage.setItem('dom_maps', exp.maps);
                document.getElementById('dom-blacklist').value = exp.blacklist;
                localStorage.setItem('dom_blacklist', exp.blacklist);
                const dojscieValue = exp.dojscie || "";
                document.getElementById('dom-dojscie-maps').value = dojscieValue;
                localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_maps', dojscieValue);
                const minLvl = exp.minLvl !== undefined ? exp.minLvl : 1;
                const maxLvl = exp.maxLvl !== undefined ? exp.maxLvl : 300;
                document.getElementById('dom-min').value = minLvl;
                localStorage.setItem('dom_min_lvl', minLvl);
                document.getElementById('dom-max').value = maxLvl;
                localStorage.setItem('dom_max_lvl', maxLvl);
            }
        });

        document.getElementById('dom-min').addEventListener('input', (e) => localStorage.setItem('dom_min_lvl', e.target.value));
        document.getElementById('dom-max').addEventListener('input', (e) => localStorage.setItem('dom_max_lvl', e.target.value));
        document.getElementById('dom-maps').addEventListener('input', (e) => localStorage.setItem('dom_maps', e.target.value));
        document.getElementById('dom-blacklist').addEventListener('input', (e) => localStorage.setItem('dom_blacklist', e.target.value));
        document.getElementById('dom-dojscie-maps').addEventListener('input', (e) => localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_maps', e.target.value));
        document.getElementById('dom-dojscie-toggle').addEventListener('change', (e) => localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_enabled', e.target.checked));

        document.getElementById('dom-toggle').addEventListener('click', function() {
            const stan = localStorage.getItem('dom_active') === 'true';
            localStorage.setItem('dom_active', (!stan).toString());
            this.innerText = !stan ? 'WŁĄCZONY' : 'WYŁĄCZONY';
            this.style.background = !stan ? '#27ae60' : '#c0392b';
        });

        document.getElementById('dom-reset').addEventListener('click', function() {
            if (typeof Engine !== 'undefined' && Engine.map && Engine.map.d) {
                const aktualnaMapaId = parseInt(Engine.map.d.id, 10);
                const isDojscieActive = localStorage.getItem('dom_dojscie_enabled') === 'true';
                const dojscieTrasa = (localStorage.getItem('dom_dojscie_maps') || "").split(/[\s,]+/).map(id => parseInt(id.trim(), 10)).filter(id => !isNaN(id));
                const mainTrasa = (localStorage.getItem('dom_maps') || "").split(/[\s,]+/).map(id => parseInt(id.trim(), 10)).filter(id => !isNaN(id));

                let indexDojscie = dojscieTrasa.indexOf(aktualnaMapaId);
                let indexMain = mainTrasa.indexOf(aktualnaMapaId);

                if (isDojscieActive && indexDojscie !== -1) {
                    localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_finished', 'false');
                    localStorage.setItem('dom_step', indexDojscie.toString());
                } else if (indexMain !== -1) {
                    if (isDojscieActive) localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_finished', 'true');
                    localStorage.setItem('dom_step', indexMain.toString());
                } else {
                    localStorage.setItem('dom_step', '0');
                    localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_finished', 'false');
                    alert(`Brak obecnej mapy (${aktualnaMapaId}) w Dojściu oraz Głównej Trasie.\nZresetowano wszystko do początku.`);
                }
            } else {
                localStorage.setItem('dom_step', '0');
                localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_finished', 'false');
                alert("Zresetowano krok trasy do zera.");
            }
        });

        const menuEl = document.getElementById('bot-menu');
        const headerEl = document.getElementById('bot-menu-header');
        let isDragging = false;
        let offsetX = 0; let offsetY = 0;
        headerEl.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => { isDragging = true; offsetX = e.clientX - menuEl.getBoundingClientRect().left; offsetY = e.clientY - menuEl.getBoundingClientRect().top; });
        document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => { if (isDragging) { menuEl.style.left = (e.clientX - offsetX) + 'px'; menuEl.style.top = (e.clientY - offsetY) + 'px'; } });
        document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => { if (isDragging) { isDragging = false; localStorage.setItem('dom_menu_x', parseInt(menuEl.style.left, 10)); localStorage.setItem('dom_menu_y', parseInt(menuEl.style.top, 10)); } });
    }

    function glownaLogikaAPI() {
        try {
            if (typeof Engine === 'undefined' || !Engine.hero || !Engine.npcs || !Engine.map) return;

            const teraz = Date.now();
            if (teraz < ostatniaAkcja) return;

            if (Engine.hero.opt && Engine.hero.opt.go) {
                if (Engine.hero.d.x === lastHeroX && Engine.hero.d.y === lastHeroY) {
                    stuckCounter++;
                } else {
                    stuckCounter = 0;
                }
                lastHeroX = Engine.hero.d.x;
                lastHeroY = Engine.hero.d.y;

                if (stuckCounter > 8) {
                    Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: Engine.hero.d.x + (Math.random() > 0.5 ? 3 : -3), y: Engine.hero.d.y + (Math.random() > 0.5 ? 3 : -3) });
                    stuckCounter = 0;
                    ostatniaAkcja = teraz + 1200;
                }
                return;
            }

            if (Engine.battle && Engine.battle.show) {
                const fastFightBtn = document.querySelector('.auto-fight-btn');
                if (fastFightBtn && fastFightBtn.offsetParent !== null) {
                    fastFightBtn.click();
                    ostatniaAkcja = teraz + 600;
                }
                return;
            }

            const isBotActive = localStorage.getItem('dom_active') === 'true';
            const aktualnaMapaId = parseInt(Engine.map.d.id, 10);

            if (aktualnaMapaId !== lastMapId) {
                const mapInfoEl = document.getElementById('bot-map-info');
                if (mapInfoEl) mapInfoEl.innerText = `Mapa: ${aktualnaMapaId}`;
            }

            const isDojscieActive = localStorage.getItem('dom_dojscie_enabled') === 'true';
            let isDojscieFinished = localStorage.getItem('dom_dojscie_finished') === 'true';

            let dojscieTrasa = (localStorage.getItem('dom_dojscie_maps') || "").split(/[\s,]+/).map(id => parseInt(id.trim(), 10)).filter(id => !isNaN(id));
            let mainTrasa = (localStorage.getItem('dom_maps') || "").split(/[\s,]+/).map(id => parseInt(id.trim(), 10)).filter(id => !isNaN(id));

            if (isDojscieActive && !isDojscieFinished && mainTrasa.includes(aktualnaMapaId)) {
                localStorage.setItem('dom_dojscie_finished', 'true');
                isDojscieFinished = true;
                localStorage.setItem('dom_step', mainTrasa.indexOf(aktualnaMapaId).toString());
            }

            const moznaBic = !(isDojscieActive && !isDojscieFinished);

            if (teraz - ostatniBerserk > 4000) {
                ostatniBerserk = teraz;
                if (isBotActive && moznaBic) {
                    const berserkIconDisabled = document.querySelector('div.gargonem-pocket-berserk-icon.disabled[tip-id="562"]');
                    if (berserkIconDisabled) berserkIconDisabled.click();
                } else {
                    const berserkIconEnabled = document.querySelector('div.gargonem-pocket-berserk-icon:not(.disabled)[tip-id="562"]');
                    if (berserkIconEnabled) berserkIconEnabled.click();
                }
            }

            if (!isBotActive) return;

            let trasa;
            if (isDojscieActive && !isDojscieFinished) {
                trasa = [...dojscieTrasa];
                if (mainTrasa.length > 0) trasa.push(mainTrasa[0]);
            } else {
                trasa = mainTrasa;
            }

            if (aktualnaMapaId !== lastMapId) {
                let currentStep = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('dom_step') || "0");
                if (currentStep >= trasa.length) currentStep = 0;
                let expectedNextMap = trasa[(currentStep + 1) % trasa.length];

                if (aktualnaMapaId === expectedNextMap) {
                    localStorage.setItem('dom_step', ((currentStep + 1) % trasa.length).toString());
                } else {
                    let idx = trasa.indexOf(aktualnaMapaId);
                    if (idx !== -1) localStorage.setItem('dom_step', idx.toString());
                }
                lastMapId = aktualnaMapaId;
            }

            let najblizszyMob = null;
            let minDystans = Infinity;

            if (moznaBic) {
                const minLvl = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('dom_min_lvl'), 10);
                const maxLvl = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('dom_max_lvl'), 10);
                const blacklist = localStorage.getItem('dom_blacklist').split(/[\s,]+/).filter(Boolean);

                for (const [idString, npc] of Object.entries(Engine.npcs.check())) {
                    if (blacklist.includes(idString)) continue;

                    if (npc.d && (npc.d.type === 2 || npc.d.type === 3) && npc.d.lvl >= minLvl && npc.d.lvl <= maxLvl) {
                        if (czyDostepny(npc.d.x, npc.d.y)) {
                            let dist = Math.max(Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.x - npc.d.x), Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.y - npc.d.y));
                            if (dist < minDystans) {
                                minDystans = dist;
                                najblizszyMob = { id: idString, name: npc.d.nick || npc.d.name || "Nieznany", x: npc.d.x, y: npc.d.y };
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            if (najblizszyMob) {
                Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: najblizszyMob.x, y: najblizszyMob.y });
                ostatniaAkcja = teraz + 700;
            } else {
                let currentStep = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('dom_step') || "0");
                if (currentStep >= trasa.length) currentStep = 0;
                let nextStep = (currentStep + 1) % trasa.length;
                let nastepnaMapaId = trasa[nextStep];
                let celBramka = Engine.map.gateways.getList().find(b => b.d && parseInt(b.d.id) === nastepnaMapaId);

                if (celBramka) {
                    let x = parseInt(celBramka.d.x);
                    let y = parseInt(celBramka.d.y);
                    let distToGateway = Math.max(Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.x - x), Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.y - y));

                    if (distToGateway === 0) {
                        ostatniaAkcja = teraz + 1500;
                        const range = 2;
                        const randomX = Engine.hero.d.x + (Math.floor(Math.random() * (range * 2 + 1)) - range);
                        const randomY = Engine.hero.d.y + (Math.floor(Math.random() * (range * 2 + 1)) - range);
                        Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: randomX, y: randomY });
                    } else if (distToGateway < 3) {
                        if (typeof celBramka.onclick === 'function') {
                            celBramka.onclick({ stopPropagation: ()=>{}, preventDefault: ()=>{} });
                        }
                        ostatniaAkcja = teraz + 3500;
                    } else {
                        Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: x, y: y });
                        ostatniaAkcja = teraz + 1500;
                    }
                }
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error("[AUTO-HUNTER ERROR]", error);
        }
    }

    setTimeout(stworzMenu, 2000);
    setInterval(glownaLogikaAPI, 350);
})();

// ==UserScript==
// @name         Margonem Bot (Nowy Interfejs - Poprawiony)
// @namespace    http://tampermonkey.net/
// @version      1.3
// @description  Bot do Margonem.pl działający na nowym interfejsie (WebGL/Canvas) - poprawiona wersja
// @author       TwójNick
// @match        https://*.margonem.pl/
// @match        https://*.margonem.com/
// @grant        none
// @run-at       document-end
// ==/UserScript==

(function() {
    'use strict';

    // ====== KONFIGURACJA ======
    const config = {
        debugMode: true,
        decisionInterval: 1500,
        safeMode: true,
        minHpToFight: 0.5,
        minMpToUseSkill: 0.3,
        maxMonsterDistance: 3,
        maxItemDistance: 2,
        fleeThreshold: 0.2,
        avoidNpcs: ['Strażnik', 'Mistrz Gildii'],
        questRefreshInterval: 30000,
        pathfinding: {
            maxSteps: 20,
            avoidObstacles: true
        }
    };

    // ====== STAN GRY ======
    const gameState = {
        player: {
            hp: 0,
            maxHp: 0,
            mp: 0,
            maxMp: 0,
            level: 0,
            position: { x: 0, y: 0 },
            target: null,
            skills: [],
            buffs: []
        },
        map: {
            name: '',
            size: { width: 100, height: 100 },
            monsters: [],
            players: [],
            npcs: [],
            items: [],
            obstacles: []
        },
        quests: {
            active: [],
            completed: [],
            available: []
        },
        killedMonsters: {},
        lastAction: null,
        lastActionTime: 0,
        isFighting: false,
        isMoving: false,
        mode: 'exp'
    };

    // ====== INICJALIZACJA ======
    function init() {
        console.log('[Margonem Bot] Inicjalizacja bota...');

        // Czekaj na załadowanie gry
        const checkGameLoaded = setInterval(() => {
            if (typeof window.Engine !== 'undefined' && window.Engine.game) {
                clearInterval(checkGameLoaded);
                console.log('[Margonem Bot] Gra załadowana, tworzenie interfejsu...');
                createUI();
                startGameMonitoring();
                startDecisionLoop();
                startQuestMonitoring();
                console.log('[Margonem Bot] Bot gotowy!');
            } else {
                console.log('[Margonem Bot] Czekam na załadowanie gry...');
            }
        }, 1000);
    }

    // ====== TWORZENIE INTERFEJSU ======
    function createUI() {
        // Sprawdź, czy interfejs już istnieje
        if (document.getElementById('margo-bot-ui')) {
            return;
        }

        const ui = document.createElement('div');
        ui.id = 'margo-bot-ui';
        ui.style.position = 'fixed';
        ui.style.bottom = '10px';
        ui.style.right = '10px';
        ui.style.zIndex = '99999';
        ui.style.backgroundColor = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.8)';
        ui.style.color = 'white';
        ui.style.padding = '10px';
        ui.style.borderRadius = '5px';
        ui.style.fontFamily = 'Arial, sans-serif';
        ui.style.fontSize = '12px';
        ui.style.width = '300px';
        ui.style.boxShadow = '0 0 10px rgba(0,0,0,0.5)';

        ui.innerHTML = `
            <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; margin-bottom: 10px;">
                <h3 style="margin: 0;">Margonem Bot</h3>
                <span id="margo-bot-status" style="color: lime;">Status: Gotowy</span>
            </div>
            <div style="margin-bottom: 10px;">
                <strong>Tryb:</strong>
                <select id="margo-bot-mode" style="margin-left: 5px; background: #333; color: white; border: 1px solid #555; border-radius: 3px;">
                    <option value="exp">Expienie</option>
                    <option value="quest">Robienie questów</option>
                    <option value="heros">Szukanie herosów</option>
                    <option value="e2">Stanie na E2</option>
                </select>
            </div>
            <div style="margin-bottom: 10px;">
                <button id="margo-toggle-bot" style="background: #4CAF50; color: white; border: none; padding: 5px 10px; border-radius: 3px; margin-right: 5px;">Włącz</button>
                <button id="margo-debug-info" style="background: #2196F3; color: white; border: none; padding: 5px 10px; border-radius: 3px; margin-right: 5px;">Debug</button>
                <button id="margo-clear-killed" style="background: #f44336; color: white; border: none; padding: 5px 10px; border-radius: 3px;">Wyczyść zabite</button>
            </div>
            <div style="margin-bottom: 10px;">
                <strong>Opcje:</strong><br>
                <label style="display: block; margin: 5px 0;"><input type="checkbox" id="margo-auto-use-skills" checked> Automatyczne używanie umiejętności</label>
                <label style="display: block; margin: 5px 0;"><input type="checkbox" id="margo-auto-pick-items" checked> Automatyczne podnoszenie przedmiotów</label>
                <label style="display: block; margin: 5px 0;"><input type="checkbox" id="margo-avoid-npcs" checked> Unikaj określonych NPC</label>
            </div>
            <div id="margo-bot-log" style="height: 200px; overflow-y: auto; border: 1px solid #333; padding: 5px; background: rgba(0,0,0,0.5); font-family: monospace;"></div>
        `;

        document.body.appendChild(ui);

        // Dodaj event listenery
        document.getElementById('margo-toggle-bot').addEventListener('click', toggleBot);
        document.getElementById('margo-debug-info').addEventListener('click', showDebugInfo);
        document.getElementById('margo-clear-killed').addEventListener('click', clearKilledMonsters);
        document.getElementById('margo-bot-mode').addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            gameState.mode = e.target.value;
            log(`Zmieniono tryb na: ${gameState.mode}`);
        });

        // Ustaw początkowy status
        document.getElementById('margo-bot-status').textContent = 'Status: Wyłączony';
        document.getElementById('margo-bot-status').style.color = 'red';
    }

    // ====== FUNKCJE POMOCNICZE ======
    function log(message) {
        if (!config.debugMode) return;

        const logElement = document.getElementById('margo-bot-log');
        if (logElement) {
            const time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
            const logEntry = document.createElement('div');
            logEntry.textContent = `[${time}] ${message}`;
            logElement.appendChild(logEntry);
            logElement.scrollTop = logElement.scrollHeight;
        }

        console.log(`[Margonem Bot] ${message}`);
    }

    function calculateDistance(pos1, pos2) {
        return Math.sqrt(Math.pow(pos1.x - pos2.x, 2) + Math.pow(pos1.y - pos2.y, 2));
    }

    function isPositionWalkable(position) {
        if (!window.Engine.game.map.collision) return true;

        const collision = window.Engine.game.map.collision;
        const x = Math.floor(position.x);
        const y = Math.floor(position.y);

        if (x < 0 || x >= collision[0].length || y < 0 || y >= collision.length) {
            return false;
        }

        return !collision[y][x];
    }

    // ====== STEROWANIE BOTEM ======
    function toggleBot() {
        const statusElement = document.getElementById('margo-bot-status');
        const button = document.getElementById('margo-toggle-bot');

        if (statusElement.textContent.includes('Aktywny')) {
            statusElement.textContent = 'Status: Wyłączony';
            statusElement.style.color = 'red';
            button.textContent = 'Włącz';
            button.style.background = '#4CAF50';
            log('Bot wyłączony');
        } else {
            statusElement.textContent = 'Status: Aktywny';
            statusElement.style.color = 'lime';
            button.textContent = 'Wyłącz';
            button.style.background = '#f44336';
            log('Bot włączony');
        }
    }

    function showDebugInfo() {
        log('=== DEBUG INFO ===');
        log(`Tryb: ${gameState.mode}`);
        log(`Pozycja: ${gameState.player.position.x}, ${gameState.player.position.y}`);
        log(`HP: ${gameState.player.hp}/${gameState.player.maxHp} (${Math.round((gameState.player.hp / gameState.player.maxHp) * 100)}%)`);
        log(`MP: ${gameState.player.mp}/${gameState.player.maxMp} (${Math.round((gameState.player.mp / gameState.player.maxMp) * 100)}%)`);
        log(`Poziom: ${gameState.player.level}`);
        log(`Mapa: ${gameState.map.name}`);
        log(`Potwory w pobliżu: ${gameState.map.monsters.length}`);
        log(`Gracze w pobliżu: ${gameState.map.players.length}`);
        log(`Przedmioty na ziemi: ${gameState.map.items.length}`);
        log(`Aktywne questy: ${gameState.quests.active.length}`);
        log('==================');
    }

    function clearKilledMonsters() {
        gameState.killedMonsters = {};
        log('Wyczyszczono listę zabitych potworów');
    }

    // ====== MONITOROWANIE GRY ======
    function startGameMonitoring() {
        setInterval(updateGameState, 1000);
    }

    function updateGameState() {
        if (!window.Engine || !window.Engine.game) return;

        try {
            updatePlayerInfo();
            updateMapInfo();
            updateUIStatus();
        } catch (e) {
            log(`Błąd aktualizacji stanu gry: ${e.message}`);
        }
    }

    function updatePlayerInfo() {
        const player = window.Engine.game.player;

        if (!player) return;

        gameState.player.hp = player.hp;
        gameState.player.maxHp = player.max_hp;
        gameState.player.mp = player.mp;
        gameState.player.maxMp = player.max_mp;
        gameState.player.level = player.level;
        gameState.player.position = { x: player.x, y: player.y };
        gameState.player.target = player.target ? player.target.nick : null;

        gameState.player.skills = [];
        if (player.skills) {
            for (const skillId in player.skills) {
                const skill = player.skills[skillId];
                gameState.player.skills.push({
                    name: skill.name,
                    cooldown: skill.cooldown > 0,
                    lastUsed: 0
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.player.buffs = [];
        if (player.buffs) {
            for (const buffId in player.buffs) {
                const buff = player.buffs[buffId];
                gameState.player.buffs.push(buff.name);
            }
        }

        gameState.isFighting = player.inFight;
    }

    function updateMapInfo() {
        const game = window.Engine.game;

        if (!game || !game.map) return;

        gameState.map.name = game.map.name || 'Nieznana';
        gameState.map.size = {
            width: game.map.width || 100,
            height: game.map.height || 100
        };

        gameState.map.monsters = [];
        if (game.map.monsters) {
            for (const monsterId in game.map.monsters) {
                const monster = game.map.monsters[monsterId];
                gameState.map.monsters.push({
                    id: monsterId,
                    name: monster.name,
                    position: { x: monster.x, y: monster.y },
                    hp: monster.hp,
                    maxHp: monster.max_hp,
                    level: monster.level,
                    distance: calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, { x: monster.x, y: monster.y }),
                    isBoss: monster.boss
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.map.monsters.sort((a, b) => {
            if (a.isBoss && !b.isBoss) return -1;
            if (!a.isBoss && b.isBoss) return 1;

            const aHpPercent = a.hp / a.maxHp;
            const bHpPercent = b.hp / b.maxHp;
            if (aHpPercent < 0.3 && bHpPercent >= 0.3) return -1;
            if (bHpPercent < 0.3 && aHpPercent >= 0.3) return 1;

            return b.level - a.level;
        });

        gameState.map.players = [];
        if (game.map.players) {
            for (const playerId in game.map.players) {
                const player = game.map.players[playerId];
                if (player.nick === game.player.nick) continue;

                gameState.map.players.push({
                    name: player.nick,
                    position: { x: player.x, y: player.y },
                    distance: calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, { x: player.x, y: player.y }),
                    isHeros: player.nick.includes('[Heros]') || player.nick.includes('Heros')
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.map.npcs = [];
        if (game.map.npcs) {
            for (const npcId in game.map.npcs) {
                const npc = game.map.npcs[npcId];
                gameState.map.npcs.push({
                    id: npcId,
                    name: npc.name,
                    position: { x: npc.x, y: npc.y },
                    distance: calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, { x: npc.x, y: npc.y }),
                    isQuestNpc: npc.quest
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.map.items = [];
        if (game.map.items) {
            for (const itemId in game.map.items) {
                const item = game.map.items[itemId];
                gameState.map.items.push({
                    id: itemId,
                    name: item.name,
                    position: { x: item.x, y: item.y },
                    distance: calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, { x: item.x, y: item.y }),
                    isGold: item.name.includes('Złoto'),
                    isQuestItem: item.quest
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.map.obstacles = [];
        if (game.map.collision) {
            const collision = game.map.collision;
            for (let y = 0; y < collision.length; y++) {
                for (let x = 0; x < collision[y].length; x++) {
                    if (collision[y][x]) {
                        gameState.map.obstacles.push({ x, y });
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function updateUIStatus() {
        const statusElement = document.getElementById('margo-bot-status');
        if (statusElement) {
            const modeText = {
                'exp': 'Expienie',
                'quest': 'Robienie questów',
                'heros': 'Szukanie herosów',
                'e2': 'Stanie na E2'
            }[gameState.mode] || gameState.mode;

            statusElement.textContent = `Status: ${gameState.isFighting ? 'Walka' : 'Spokój'} | Tryb: ${modeText}`;
        }
    }

    // ====== MONITOROWANIE QUESTÓW ======
    function startQuestMonitoring() {
        setInterval(updateQuests, config.questRefreshInterval);
    }

    function updateQuests() {
        if (!window.Engine || !window.Engine.game || !window.Engine.game.quests) return;

        try {
            const quests = window.Engine.game.quests;

            gameState.quests.active = [];
            if (quests.active) {
                for (const questId in quests.active) {
                    const quest = quests.active[questId];
                    gameState.quests.active.push({
                        id: questId,
                        name: quest.name,
                        progress: quest.progress,
                        isCompleted: quest.progress.current >= quest.progress.total
                    });
                }
            }

            gameState.quests.available = [];
            if (quests.available) {
                for (const questId in quests.available) {
                    const quest = quests.available[questId];
                    gameState.quests.available.push({
                        id: questId,
                        name: quest.name,
                        giver: quest.giver
                    });
                }
            }

            gameState.quests.completed = [];
            if (quests.completed) {
                for (const questId in quests.completed) {
                    const quest = quests.completed[questId];
                    gameState.quests.completed.push({
                        id: questId,
                        name: quest.name,
                        receiver: quest.receiver
                    });
                }
            }

            log(`Zaktualizowano questy. Aktywne: ${gameState.quests.active.length}, Dostępne: ${gameState.quests.available.length}, Ukończone: ${gameState.quests.completed.length}`);
        } catch (e) {
            log(`Błąd aktualizacji questów: ${e.message}`);
        }
    }

    // ====== CYKL DECYZYJNY ======
    function startDecisionLoop() {
        setInterval(makeDecision, config.decisionInterval);
    }

    function makeDecision() {
        if (!window.Engine || !window.Engine.game || !document.getElementById('margo-bot-status').textContent.includes('Aktywny')) {
            return;
        }

        try {
            if (gameState.isFighting) {
                handleCombat();
                return;
            }

            switch (gameState.mode) {
                case 'exp':
                    handleExpMode();
                    break;
                case 'quest':
                    handleQuestMode();
                    break;
                case 'heros':
                    handleHerosMode();
                    break;
                case 'e2':
                    handleE2Mode();
                    break;
                default:
                    handleExpMode();
            }
        } catch (e) {
            log(`Błąd podejmowania decyzji: ${e.message}`);
        }
    }

    // ====== TRYBY DZIAŁANIA ======
    function handleExpMode() {
        const decisions = [
            checkFleeCondition(),
            checkLowHp(),
            checkLowMp(),
            checkAttackableMonster(),
            checkPickableItem(),
            checkRandomMovement()
        ];

        const bestDecision = getBestDecision(decisions);
        executeDecision(bestDecision);
    }

    function handleQuestMode() {
        if (gameState.quests.completed.length > 0) {
            const quest = gameState.quests.completed[0];
            const npc = gameState.map.npcs.find(n => n.name === quest.receiver);

            if (npc) {
                if (npc.distance <= 1) {
                    return executeDecision({
                        action: 'turn_in_quest',
                        target: quest.id,
                        reason: `Oddaję quest: ${quest.name}`,
                        priority: 10
                    });
                } else {
                    return executeDecision({
                        action: 'move_to',
                        target: npc.position,
                        reason: `Idę oddać quest: ${quest.name}`,
                        priority: 10
                    });
                }
            }
        }

        if (gameState.quests.available.length > 0) {
            const quest = gameState.quests.available[0];
            const npc = gameState.map.npcs.find(n => n.name === quest.giver);

            if (npc) {
                if (npc.distance <= 1) {
                    return executeDecision({
                        action: 'accept_quest',
                        target: quest.id,
                        reason: `Przyjmuję quest: ${quest.name}`,
                        priority: 9
                    });
                } else {
                    return executeDecision({
                        action: 'move_to',
                        target: npc.position,
                        reason: `Idę przyjąć quest: ${quest.name}`,
                        priority: 9
                    });
                }
            }
        }

        handleExpMode();
    }

    function handleHerosMode() {
        const herosPlayers = gameState.map.players.filter(p => p.isHeros);

        if (herosPlayers.length > 0) {
            const closestHeros = herosPlayers[0];

            if (closestHeros.distance <= 1) {
                return executeDecision({
                    action: 'follow_player',
                    target: closestHeros.name,
                    reason: `Podążam za herosem: ${closestHeros.name}`,
                    priority: 8
                });
            } else {
                return executeDecision({
                    action: 'move_to',
                    target: closestHeros.position,
                    reason: `Idę do herosa: ${closestHeros.name}`,
                    priority: 8
                });
            }
        }

        handleExpMode();
    }

    function handleE2Mode() {
        const e2Position = { x: 50, y: 50 };

        if (calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, e2Position) <= 1) {
            return executeDecision({
                action: 'wait',
                reason: 'Stoję na E2',
                priority: 1
            });
        } else {
            return executeDecision({
                action: 'move_to',
                target: e2Position,
                reason: 'Idę na E2',
                priority: 10
            });
        }
    }

    // ====== DECYZJE ======
    function checkFleeCondition() {
        const hpPercentage = gameState.player.hp / gameState.player.maxHp;
        if (hpPercentage < config.fleeThreshold) {
            return { action: 'flee', reason: 'Niskie HP - ucieczka', priority: 10 };
        }
        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkLowHp() {
        const hpPercentage = gameState.player.hp / gameState.player.maxHp;
        if (hpPercentage < config.minHpToFight) {
            return { action: 'use_potion', target: 'hp', reason: 'Niskie HP', priority: 9 };
        }
        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkLowMp() {
        const mpPercentage = gameState.player.mp / gameState.player.maxMp;
        if (mpPercentage < config.minMpToUseSkill) {
            return { action: 'use_potion', target: 'mp', reason: 'Niskie MP', priority: 8 };
        }
        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkAttackableMonster() {
        if (gameState.map.monsters.length === 0) {
            return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
        }

        const closestMonster = gameState.map.monsters[0];

        if (gameState.killedMonsters[closestMonster.name] &&
            gameState.killedMonsters[closestMonster.name] >= 5) {
            log(`Potwór ${closestMonster.name} został już zabity wystarczająco razy, pomijam`);
            return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
        }

        if (closestMonster.distance <= config.maxMonsterDistance) {
            return {
                action: 'attack',
                target: closestMonster.id,
                reason: `Potwór ${closestMonster.name} (Lvl ${closestMonster.level}) w zasięgu`,
                priority: 7
            };
        }

        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkPickableItem() {
        if (!document.getElementById('margo-auto-pick-items')?.checked) {
            return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
        }

        if (gameState.map.items.length === 0) {
            return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
        }

        const closestItem = gameState.map.items[0];
        if (closestItem.distance <= config.maxItemDistance) {
            return {
                action: 'pick_up',
                target: closestItem.id,
                reason: `Przedmiot ${closestItem.name} w zasięgu`,
                priority: 6
            };
        }

        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkRandomMovement() {
        return { action: 'move_random', reason: 'Brak innych akcji', priority: 1 };
    }

    function getBestDecision(decisions) {
        return decisions.reduce((best, current) =>
            (current.priority > best.priority) ? current : best,
            { action: 'wait', priority: 0 }
        );
    }

    // ====== WYKONYWANIE DECYZJI ======
    function executeDecision(decision) {
        if (!decision || !decision.action || decision.priority === 0) {
            return;
        }

        gameState.lastAction = `${decision.action} ${decision.target ? `(${decision.target})` : ''}`;
        gameState.lastActionTime = Date.now();

        log(`Wykonuję: ${decision.action} (${decision.reason})`);

        switch (decision.action) {
            case 'attack':
                attackMonster(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'move_to':
                moveToPosition(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'pick_up':
                pickUpItem(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'use_potion':
                usePotion(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'use_skill':
                useSkill(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'flee':
                fleeFromCombat();
                break;
            case 'talk_to_npc':
                talkToNPC(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'accept_quest':
                acceptQuest(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'turn_in_quest':
                turnInQuest(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'follow_player':
                followPlayer(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'move_random':
                moveRandomly();
                break;
            case 'wait':
            default:
                log('Czekam...');
                break;
        }
    }

    // ====== AKCJE ======
    function attackMonster(monsterId) {
        const monster = gameState.map.monsters.find(m => m.id === monsterId);
        if (!monster) {
            log(`Nie znaleziono potwora o ID: ${monsterId}`);
            return;
        }

        if (monster.distance > 1) {
            log(`Potwór ${monster.name} jest za daleko (${monster.distance.toFixed(1)})`);
            moveToPosition(monster.position);
            return;
        }

        log(`Atakuję ${monster.name} (Lvl ${monster.level}, HP: ${monster.hp}/${monster.maxHp})`);

        if (!gameState.killedMonsters[monster.name]) {
            gameState.killedMonsters[monster.name] = 0;
        }
        gameState.killedMonsters[monster.name]++;

        window.Engine.game.attack(monsterId);

        if (document.getElementById('margo-auto-use-skills')?.checked) {
            useCombatSkills();
        }
    }

    function moveToPosition(position) {
        if (gameState.isMoving) return;

        const distance = calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, position);
        if (distance <= 1) {
            log(`Już jesteśmy przy celu (${position.x}, ${position.y})`);
            return;
        }

        log(`Poruszam się do (${position.x}, ${position.y})`);

        const path = findPath(gameState.player.position, position);
        if (path.length > 0) {
            const nextStep = path[0];
            window.Engine.game.move(nextStep.x, nextStep.y);
            gameState.isMoving = true;

            setTimeout(() => {
                gameState.isMoving = false;
            }, 1000);
        } else {
            log('Nie znaleziono ścieżki!');
            window.Engine.game.move(position.x, position.y);
        }
    }

    function findPath(start, end) {
        const openSet = [start];
        const cameFrom = {};
        const gScore = {};
        const fScore = {};

        gScore[start.x + ',' + start.y] = 0;
        fScore[start.x + ',' + start.y] = calculateDistance(start, end);

        while (openSet.length > 0) {
            let current = openSet[0];
            for (const node of openSet) {
                if (fScore[node.x + ',' + node.y] < fScore[current.x + ',' + current.y]) {
                    current = node;
                }
            }

            if (current.x === end.x && current.y === end.y) {
                const path = [];
                let temp = current;
                while (temp.x !== start.x || temp.y !== start.y) {
                    path.push(temp);
                    temp = cameFrom[temp.x + ',' + temp.y];
                }
                return path.reverse();
            }

            openSet.splice(openSet.indexOf(current), 1);

            const neighbors = [
                { x: current.x + 1, y: current.y },
                { x: current.x - 1, y: current.y },
                { x: current.x, y: current.y + 1 },
                { x: current.x, y: current.y - 1 }
            ];

            for (const neighbor of neighbors) {
                if (neighbor.x < 0 || neighbor.x >= gameState.map.size.width ||
                    neighbor.y < 0 || neighbor.y >= gameState.map.size.height) {
                    continue;
                }

                if (config.pathfinding.avoidObstacles && !isPositionWalkable(neighbor)) {
                    continue;
                }

                const tentativeGScore = gScore[current.x + ',' + current.y] + 1;

                if (!gScore[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y] ||
                    tentativeGScore < gScore[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y]) {
                    cameFrom[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y] = current;
                    gScore[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y] = tentativeGScore;
                    fScore[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y] = tentativeGScore + calculateDistance(neighbor, end);

                    if (!openSet.some(node => node.x === neighbor.x && node.y === neighbor.y)) {
                        openSet.push(neighbor);
                    }
                }
            }

            if (Object.keys(cameFrom).length > config.pathfinding.maxSteps) {
                log('Przekroczono maksymalną liczbę kroków w szukaniu ścieżki');
                return [];
            }
        }

        log('Nie znaleziono ścieżki!');
        return [];
    }

    function pickUpItem(itemId) {
        const item = gameState.map.items.find(i => i.id === itemId);
        if (!item) {
            log(`Nie znaleziono przedmiotu o ID: ${itemId}`);
            return;
        }

        if (item.distance > 1) {
            log(`Przedmiot ${item.name} jest za daleko (${item.distance.toFixed(1)})`);
            moveToPosition(item.position);
            return;
        }

        log(`Podnoszę ${item.name}`);
        window.Engine.game.pickUpItem(itemId);
    }

    function usePotion(type) {
        log(`Używam mikstury: ${type}`);
        window.Engine.game.usePotion(type);
    }

    function useSkill(skillName) {
        if (!document.getElementById('margo-auto-use-skills')?.checked) {
            return;
        }

        const skill = gameState.player.skills.find(s => s.name === skillName);
        if (!skill) {
            log(`Nie znaleziono umiejętności: ${skillName}`);
            return;
        }

        log(`Używam umiejętności: ${skillName}`);
        window.Engine.game.useSkill(skillName);
    }

    function useCombatSkills() {
        if (gameState.player.hp / gameState.player.maxHp < 0.5) {
            const healSkill = gameState.player.skills.find(s =>
                s.name.includes('Leczenie') || s.name.includes('Heal')
            );
            if (healSkill) {
                useSkill(healSkill.name);
                return;
            }
        }

        const offensiveSkills = gameState.player.skills.filter(s =>
            !s.cooldown &&
            (s.name.includes('Atak') || s.name.includes('Fireball') || s.name.includes('Błyskawica'))
        );

        if (offensiveSkills.length > 0) {
            useSkill(offensiveSkills[0].name);
        }
    }

    function fleeFromCombat() {
        log('Uciekam z walki!');
        window.Engine.game.flee();
    }

    function talkToNPC(npcId) {
        log(`Rozmawiam z NPC o ID: ${npcId}`);
        window.Engine.game.talkToNPC(npcId);
    }

    function acceptQuest(questId) {
        log(`Przyjmuję quest o ID: ${questId}`);
        window.Engine.game.acceptQuest(questId);
    }

    function turnInQuest(questId) {
        log(`Oddaję quest o ID: ${questId}`);
        window.Engine.game.turnInQuest(questId);
    }

    function followPlayer(playerName) {
        const player = gameState.map.players.find(p => p.name === playerName);
        if (!player) {
            log(`Nie znaleziono gracza: ${playerName}`);
            return;
        }

        if (player.distance <= 1) {
            log(`Podążam za graczem: ${playerName}`);
        } else {
            moveToPosition(player.position);
        }
    }

    function moveRandomly() {
        if (gameState.isMoving) return;

        const directions = [
            { x: 0, y: -1 },
            { x: 1, y: 0 },
            { x: 0, y: 1 },
            { x: -1, y: 0 }
        ];

        const randomDir = directions[Math.floor(Math.random() * directions.length)];
        const newPos = {
            x: gameState.player.position.x + randomDir.x,
            y: gameState.player.position.y + randomDir.y
        };

        if (newPos.x >= 0 && newPos.x < gameState.map.size.width &&
            newPos.y >= 0 && newPos.y < gameState.map.size.height &&
            isPositionWalkable(newPos)) {
            window.Engine.game.move(newPos.x, newPos.y);
        }
    }

    function handleCombat() {
        if (gameState.player.hp / gameState.player.maxHp < config.fleeThreshold) {
            fleeFromCombat();
            return;
        }

        if (gameState.player.hp / gameState.player.maxHp < config.minHpToFight) {
            usePotion('hp');
            return;
        }

        if (gameState.player.mp / gameState.player.maxMp < config.minMpToUseSkill) {
            usePotion('mp');
            return;
        }

        if (document.getElementById('margo-auto-use-skills')?.checked) {
            useCombatSkills();
        }
    }

    // ====== ROZWIĄZYWANIE PROBLEMÓW ======
    function checkForProblems() {
        // Sprawdź, czy interfejs się wyświetla
        if (!document.getElementById('margo-bot-ui')) {
            log('❌ Interfejs bota nie został utworzony!');
            console.error('[Margonem Bot] Interfejs nie został utworzony. Sprawdź, czy skrypt działa na właściwej stronie.');
            return false;
        }

        // Sprawdź, czy Engine.game istnieje
        if (!window.Engine || !window.Engine.game) {
            log('❌ Nie znaleziono obiektu Engine.game!');
            console.error('[Margonem Bot] Nie znaleziono obiektu Engine.game. Upewnij się, że jesteś w grze na nowym interfejsie.');
            return false;
        }

        // Sprawdź, czy metody gry są dostępne
        const requiredMethods = ['attack', 'move', 'pickUpItem', 'usePotion', 'useSkill'];
        for (const method of requiredMethods) {
            if (typeof window.Engine.game[method] !== 'function') {
                log(`❌ Metoda ${method} nie jest dostępna w Engine.game!`);
                console.error(`[Margonem Bot] Metoda ${method} nie jest dostępna. Gra mogła zaktualizować API.`);
                return false;
            }
        }

        log('✅ Wszystkie sprawdzenia przeszły pomyślnie!');
        return true;
    }

    // ====== INICJALIZACJA ======
    // Sprawdź, czy jesteśmy na właściwej stronie
    if (window.location.hostname.includes('margonem.pl') || window.location.hostname.includes('margonem.com')) {
        // Uruchom diagnostykę po 5 sekundach
        setTimeout(() => {
            if (!checkForProblems()) {
                console.log('[Margonem Bot] Wykryto problemy. Spróbuj ponownie uruchomić skrypt.');
            }
        }, 5000);

        init();
    } else {
        console.log('[Margonem Bot] Nie jesteś na stronie Margonem. Skrypt nie zostanie uruchomiony.');
    }
})();

// ==UserScript==
// @name         Follow The Leader
// @namespace    https://bettermargo.pl/private/
// @version      1.0.0
// @author       Sziki
// @description  Prywatny dodatek: wykrywa lidera grupy (party) i automatycznie podąża za nim po mapie.
// @match        http*://*.margonem.pl/
// @match        http*://*.margonem.com/
// @exclude      http*://forum.margonem.*/*
// @exclude      http*://commons.margonem.*/*
// @exclude      http*://dev-commons.margonem.*/*
// @run-at       document-idle
// ==/UserScript==

(function () {
  "use strict";

  const STORAGE_KEY = "ftl-enabled";
  const POLL_MS = 900;
  const WAIT_TIMEOUT_MS = 30000;
  const WAIT_STEP_MS = 250;

  const state = {
    enabled: localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY) === "1",
    statusText: "Nieaktywny",
    lastLeaderPos: null,
    ui: null,
  };

  function wait(ms) {
    return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
  }

  async function waitForGameContext() {
    const startedAt = Date.now();
    while (Date.now() - startedAt < WAIT_TIMEOUT_MS) {
      if (globalThis.Engine?.hero?.d?.id != null) return true;
      await wait(WAIT_STEP_MS);
    }
    throw new Error("Timeout podczas oczekiwania na Engine.hero.d.id");
  }

  function isInBattle() {
    const battle = globalThis.Engine?.battle;
    if (!battle) return false;
    if (battle.getShow && battle.getShow()) return true;
    return !!document.querySelector(".battle-window, .battle-area");
  }

  function getLeaderId() {
    const party = globalThis.Engine?.party;
    if (!party || typeof party.getLeaderId !== "function") return null;
    try {
      return party.getLeaderId();
    } catch (_) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  function getLeaderObj(leaderId) {
    const others = globalThis.Engine?.others;
    if (!others || typeof others.getById !== "function") return null;
    try {
      return others.getById(leaderId);
    } catch (_) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  function setStatus(text) {
    if (state.statusText === text) return;
    state.statusText = text;
    if (state.ui) state.ui.status.textContent = text;
  }

  function tick() {
    if (!state.enabled) return;
    if (globalThis.Engine?.dead || isInBattle()) {
      setStatus("Wstrzymano (walka/martwy)");
      return;
    }

    const heroD = globalThis.Engine?.hero?.d;
    if (!heroD) {
      setStatus("Brak danych bohatera");
      return;
    }

    const leaderId = getLeaderId();
    if (leaderId == null) {
      setStatus("Brak grupy");
      state.lastLeaderPos = null;
      return;
    }
    if (String(leaderId) === String(heroD.id)) {
      setStatus("Jesteś liderem");
      state.lastLeaderPos = null;
      return;
    }

    const leaderObj = getLeaderObj(leaderId);
    if (!leaderObj?.d) {
      setStatus("Lider poza zasięgiem");
      state.lastLeaderPos = null;
      return;
    }

    const leaderD = leaderObj.d;
    const dx = Math.abs(leaderD.x - heroD.x);
    const dy = Math.abs(leaderD.y - heroD.y);

    if (dx <= 1 && dy <= 1) {
      setStatus(`Przy liderze: ${leaderD.nick}`);
      state.lastLeaderPos = { x: leaderD.x, y: leaderD.y };
      return;
    }

    const moved = !state.lastLeaderPos || state.lastLeaderPos.x !== leaderD.x || state.lastLeaderPos.y !== leaderD.y;
    if (moved) {
      state.lastLeaderPos = { x: leaderD.x, y: leaderD.y };
      try {
        globalThis.Engine.hero.addAfterFollowAction(leaderObj);
      } catch (_) {}
    }
    setStatus(`Podążam za: ${leaderD.nick} (${Math.max(dx, dy)}p)`);
  }

  function setEnabled(next) {
    state.enabled = next;
    localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, next ? "1" : "0");
    if (state.ui) {
      state.ui.button.classList.toggle("ftl-on", next);
      state.ui.button.textContent = next ? "FTL: ON" : "FTL: OFF";
    }
    setStatus(next ? "Szukam lidera..." : "Nieaktywny");
  }

  function injectUi() {
    const style = document.createElement("style");
    style.textContent = `
      #ftl-panel {
        position: fixed;
        right: 12px;
        bottom: 90px;
        z-index: 99999;
        display: flex;
        flex-direction: column;
        align-items: stretch;
        gap: 4px;
        font-family: Arial, sans-serif;
        user-select: none;
      }
      #ftl-panel button {
        cursor: pointer;
        border: 1px solid #333;
        border-radius: 4px;
        background: #444;
        color: #eee;
        font-size: 11px;
        font-weight: bold;
        padding: 6px 10px;
      }
      #ftl-panel button.ftl-on {
        background: #2e7d32;
        border-color: #1b5e20;
      }
      #ftl-panel .ftl-status {
        font-size: 10px;
        color: #ddd;
        background: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.6);
        border-radius: 3px;
        padding: 3px 6px;
        text-align: center;
        max-width: 160px;
      }
    `;
    document.head.appendChild(style);

    const panel = document.createElement("div");
    panel.id = "ftl-panel";

    const button = document.createElement("button");
    button.type = "button";
    button.textContent = state.enabled ? "FTL: ON" : "FTL: OFF";
    button.classList.toggle("ftl-on", state.enabled);
    button.addEventListener("click", () => setEnabled(!state.enabled));

    const status = document.createElement("div");
    status.className = "ftl-status";
    status.textContent = state.statusText;

    panel.appendChild(button);
    panel.appendChild(status);
    document.body.appendChild(panel);

    state.ui = { panel, button, status };
  }

  async function init() {
    await waitForGameContext();
    injectUi();
    setInterval(tick, POLL_MS);
  }

  init().catch((err) => console.error("[FollowTheLeader]", err));
})();

        { action: "hunt", mobs: ["Brązowa mrówka żołnierz", "Brązowa mrówka robotnica", "Brązowa mrówka tragarz"], targetCount: 10, maps: [2528], desc: "Zabij 10 Mrówek"},
        { action: "move", x: 7, y: 4, desc: "Podejdź (7, 4)" },
        { action: "bramka", targetMapId: 2522, desc: "Idź do mapy Mrowisko" },
        { action: "bramka", targetMapId: 2029, desc: "Idź do mapy Łany Zboża" },
        { action: "move", x: 9, y: 2, desc: "Podejdź (9, 2)" },
        { action: "talk", nick: "Młynarzowa Trenia", desc: "Zagadaj z npc Młynarzowa Trenia" },
        { action: "dialog", option: 1, desc: "Wybierz Dialog 1 (Zejdź do podziemi)" },
        { action: "dialog", option: 1, desc: "Wybierz Dialog 1 (Zejdź do podziemi)" },
        { action: "dialog", option: 1, desc: "Wybierz Dialog 1 (Zejdź do podziemi)" },
        { action: "dialog", option: 1, desc: "Wybierz Dialog 1 (Zejdź do podziemi)" },
        { action: "dialog", option: 1, desc: "Wybierz Dialog 1 (Zejdź do podziemi)" }, // Awiatka kontynuacja
    ];

    // ==========================================
    // ZMIENNE SILNIKA
    // ==========================================
    let isRunning = false;
    let currentStepIndex = 0;
    let lastActionTime = 0;
    let sequenceInterval = null;

    function updateDisplay() {
        let stepEl = document.getElementById('quest-bot-step');
        let statusEl = document.getElementById('quest-bot-status');
        let selectEl = document.getElementById('quest-step-select');

        if (currentStepIndex >= QUEST_SEQUENCE.length) {
            stepEl.innerText = "Wszystkie kroki wykonane!";
            statusEl.innerText = "ZAKOŃCZONO!";
            statusEl.style.color = "#2ecc71";
            isRunning = false;
            let btn = document.getElementById('quest-toggle-btn');
            if (btn) {
                btn.innerHTML = "▶ START";
                btn.style.background = "#27ae60";
            }
            clearInterval(sequenceInterval);
        } else {
            let step = QUEST_SEQUENCE[currentStepIndex];
            stepEl.innerText = `Aktualnie: ${step.desc}`;

            // Synchronizacja listy rozwijanej z aktualnym krokiem
            if (selectEl && parseInt(selectEl.value, 10) !== currentStepIndex) {
                selectEl.value = currentStepIndex;
            }
        }
    }

    function forceInteract(target) {
        if (typeof target.onclick === 'function') {
            target.onclick({ preventDefault: ()=>{}, stopPropagation: ()=>{}, button: 2 });
        } else if (target.d && target.d.isGw) {
            let gwObj = Engine.map.gateways.getList().find(g => g.d && g.d.id === target.d.id);
            if (gwObj && typeof gwObj.onclick === 'function') gwObj.onclick({stopPropagation:()=>{}, preventDefault:()=>{}});
        } else {
            console.warn("[Bot] Obiekt nie posiada funkcji onclick!");
        }
    }

    // ==========================================
    // GŁÓWNA LOGIKA WYKONAWCZA
    // ==========================================
    function processSequence() {
        if (!isRunning) return;

        let now = Date.now();
        if (now < lastActionTime) return;
        const currentMap = Engine.map.d ? parseInt(Engine.map.d.id, 10) : 0; // W razie czego do usunięcia
        if (typeof Engine !== 'undefined' && Engine.battle && Engine.battle.show) {
            let fastFightBtn = document.querySelector('.auto-fight-btn');
            if (!Engine.battle._botAutoFought) {
                if (fastFightBtn) {
                    fastFightBtn.click();
                    Engine.battle._botAutoFought = true;
                    lastActionTime = now + 1500;
                } else {
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                }
            } else {
                lastActionTime = now + 500;
            }
            return;
        } else if (typeof Engine !== 'undefined' && Engine.battle) {
            Engine.battle._botAutoFought = false;
        }

        let step = QUEST_SEQUENCE[currentStepIndex];
        if (!step) {
            updateDisplay();
            return;
        }
        updateDisplay();

        switch (step.action) {
                // ==================================================
            // CASE: TRASA (Podążanie po wyznaczonej ścieżce map)
            // ==================================================
            case 'path':
                let nowTimePath = Date.now();

                // Sprawdzamy czy poprawnie wpisano trasę
                if (!step.maps || step.maps.length === 0) {
                    console.error("[Bot] Błąd: Brak tablicy maps w akcji 'path'.");
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    break;
                }

                let mapIndex = step.maps.indexOf(currentMap);
                let finalMap = step.maps[step.maps.length - 1];

                // Aktualizacja interfejsu
                let pathStatusEl = document.getElementById('quest-bot-status');
                if (pathStatusEl) {
                    pathStatusEl.innerText = `Trasa: Cel -> ${finalMap}`;
                    pathStatusEl.style.color = "#3498db";
                }

                // 1. Sukces - Jesteśmy na ostatniej mapie z trasy
                if (currentMap === finalMap) {
                    console.log(`[Bot] Dotarto do celu trasy: ${finalMap}`);
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = nowTimePath + 500;
                    break;
                }

                // 2. Jesteśmy na trasie - Szukamy przejścia do następnej mapy
                if (mapIndex !== -1) {
                    let nextMapId = step.maps[mapIndex + 1];
                    let gates = Engine.map.gateways.getList();
