                    // Szukamy bramki prowadzącej do 'nextMapId'
                    let celBramka = gates.find(g => g.d && (parseInt(g.d.target) === nextMapId || parseInt(g.d.id) === nextMapId));

                    if (celBramka) {
                        let dX = Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.x - celBramka.d.x);
                        let dY = Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.y - celBramka.d.y);

                        // Podchodzenie do bramki
                        if (dX > 1 || dY > 1) {
                            Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: celBramka.d.x, y: celBramka.d.y });
                            lastActionTime = nowTimePath + 800;
                        }
                        // Kliknięcie w bramkę
                        else {
                            forceInteract(celBramka);
                            console.log(`[Bot] Podążam trasą. Przechodzę na mapę: ${nextMapId}`);
                            lastActionTime = nowTimePath + 2500; // Dajemy czas na wczytanie nowej mapy
                        }
                    } else {
                        console.warn(`[Bot] Na trasie, ale nie widzę bramki na mapę ${nextMapId}!`);
                        if (pathStatusEl) pathStatusEl.innerText = `Brak przejścia do ${nextMapId}`;
                        lastActionTime = nowTimePath + 1000;
                    }
                }
                // 3. Zgubiliśmy się - obecna mapa nie istnieje w tablicy trasy
                else {
                    console.warn(`[Bot] Zgubiłem się! Obecna mapa (${currentMap}) nie należy do trasy: [${step.maps.join(', ')}]`);
                    if (pathStatusEl) {
                        pathStatusEl.innerText = `Zgubiono trasę!`;
                        pathStatusEl.style.color = "#e74c3c";
                    }
                    lastActionTime = nowTimePath + 2000;
                }
                break;
            // ==================================================
                // ==================================================
            // CASE: POLOWANIE WYZNACZONĄ TRASĄ (Synchronizacja z listą Questów)
            // ==================================================
            case 'hunt':
                let nowTime = Date.now();

                // Inicjalizacja wewnętrznych zmiennych bota
                if (step.killedCount === undefined) step.killedCount = 0;
                if (step.currentRouteIndex === undefined) step.currentRouteIndex = 0;

                // 1. ODCZYT STANU Z INTERFEJSU GRY (Śledzone questy)
                let uiKills = -1;
                let uiTarget = step.targetCount || 0;
                let uiDone = false;

                // Szukamy elementów z misjami typu "Zabij"
                let missionElements = document.querySelectorAll('.one-quest-mission.mission-type-2 .one-name');
                for (let el of missionElements) {
                    let text = el.innerText.trim(); // np. "Czarny wilk (5/5)"

                    // Sprawdzamy, czy ten punkt questa dotyczy któregoś z naszych mobów z tablicy step.mobs
                    let matchesMob = step.mobs.some(m => text.toLowerCase().includes(m.toLowerCase()));

                    if (matchesMob) {
                        // Sprawdzamy czy całe zadanie ma już klasę 'quest-done'
                        let missionWrapper = el.closest('.one-quest-mission');
                        if (missionWrapper && missionWrapper.classList.contains('quest-done')) {
                            uiDone = true;
                        }

                        // Wyciąganie postępu z tekstu np. "(3/5)" za pomocą Regexa
                        let match = text.match(/\((\d+)\/(\d+)\)/);
                        if (match) {
                            uiKills = parseInt(match[1], 10);
                            uiTarget = parseInt(match[2], 10);
                        }
                        break; // Znaleźliśmy właściwy tracker questa, przerywamy pętle
                    }
                }

                // Synchronizacja: Priorytet ma UI gry. Jeśli quest nie jest śledzony - zostaje licznik wewnętrzny bota
                if (uiKills !== -1) {
                    step.killedCount = uiKills;
                    step.targetCount = uiTarget; // Bot sam wie ile ma zabić z interfejsu, nawet jeśli w JSON podasz błędną liczbę!
                }

                // Aktualizacja UI bota
                let questStatusEl = document.getElementById('quest-bot-status');
                if (questStatusEl) {
                    questStatusEl.innerText = `Polowanie: ${step.killedCount} / ${step.targetCount || '?'}`;
                    questStatusEl.style.color = "#f1c40f";
                }

                // 2. CZY OSIĄGNIĘTO CEL?
                if (uiDone || (step.targetCount > 0 && step.killedCount >= step.targetCount)) {
                    console.log(`[Bot] Zakończono polowanie! Osiągnięto cel questa.`);
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = nowTime + 500;
                    break;
                }

                // 3. LOGIKA TRASY I SZUKANIA MOBÓW
                let expectedMap = step.maps[step.currentRouteIndex];

                if (currentMap !== expectedMap && step.maps.includes(currentMap)) {
                    step.currentRouteIndex = step.maps.indexOf(currentMap);
                    expectedMap = currentMap;
                }

                if (currentMap === expectedMap) {
                    let npcs = Object.values(Engine.npcs.check());
                    let tMob = null;
                    let minDist = Infinity;

                    npcs.forEach(n => {
                        if (!n.d || !(n.d.type === 2 || n.d.type === 3)) return;

                        let isMatch = step.mobs.some(m => n.d.nick.toLowerCase().includes(m.toLowerCase()));

                        if (isMatch) {
                            let dist = Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.x - n.d.x) + Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.y - n.d.y);
                            if (dist < minDist) {
                                minDist = dist;
                                tMob = n;
                            }
                        }
                    });

                    // 4A. Mamy Moba na mapie
                    if (tMob) {
                        let dX = Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.x - tMob.d.x);
                        let dY = Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.y - tMob.d.y);

                        if (dX > 1 || dY > 1) {
                            Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: tMob.d.x, y: tMob.d.y });
                            lastActionTime = nowTime + 800;
                        } else {
                            forceInteract(tMob);
                            console.log(`[Bot] Atakuję: ${tMob.d.nick}`);

                            // Jeśli gra nie jest śledzona (uiKills === -1), bot dodaje zabójstwo w ciemno.
                            // Jeśli jest śledzona, bot po prostu czeka aż UI samo zaktualizuje ułamek np. (1/5) na (2/5).
                            if (uiKills === -1) step.killedCount++;

                            lastActionTime = nowTime + 2000;
                        }
                    }
                    // 4B. Brak mobów - idziemy do następnej mapy
                    else {
                        if (step.currentRouteIndex + 1 < step.maps.length) {
                            let nextMapId = step.maps[step.currentRouteIndex + 1];
                            let gates = Engine.map.gateways.getList();
                            let celBramka = gates.find(g => g.d && (parseInt(g.d.target) === nextMapId || parseInt(g.d.id) === nextMapId));

                            if (celBramka) {
                                let dX = Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.x - celBramka.d.x);
                                let dY = Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.y - celBramka.d.y);
                                if (dX > 1 || dY > 1) {
                                    Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: celBramka.d.x, y: celBramka.d.y });
                                    lastActionTime = nowTime + 800;
                                } else {
                                    forceInteract(celBramka);
                                    console.log(`[Bot] Czysto! Idę dalej ścieżką na mapę: ${nextMapId}`);
                                    step.currentRouteIndex++;
                                    lastActionTime = nowTime + 3000;
                                }
                            } else {
                                console.warn(`[Bot] Ścieżka przerwana. Nie widzę bramki do: ${nextMapId}`);
                                if (questStatusEl) questStatusEl.innerText = `Błąd przejścia do ${nextMapId}`;
                                lastActionTime = nowTime + 1000;
                            }
                        } else {
                            console.log("[Bot] Dotarto do końca trasy. Zapętlam ścieżkę...");
                            step.currentRouteIndex = 0;
                            lastActionTime = nowTime + 1000;
                        }
                    }
                }
                // 5. Zgubiliśmy się (jesteśmy poza wyznaczoną trasą)
                else {
                    console.warn(`[Bot] Zgubiłem się! Szukam powrotu na trasę (cel: ${expectedMap})...`);
                    let gates = Engine.map.gateways.getList();
                    let celBramka = gates.find(g => g.d && (parseInt(g.d.target) === expectedMap || parseInt(g.d.id) === expectedMap));

                    if (celBramka) {
                        forceInteract(celBramka);
                        lastActionTime = nowTime + 2500;
                    } else {
                        lastActionTime = nowTime + 1500;
                    }
                }
                break;
            // ==================================================
            // ==================================================
                // ===============================================================================
                case 'bramka':
                // 1. Sprawdzamy czy jesteśmy na mapie docelowej (czytamy step.targetMapId)
                if (currentMap === step.targetMapId) {
                    console.log(`[Bot] Jesteśmy na mapie: ${step.targetMapId}. Przechodzę dalej.`);
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                    break;
                }

                // 2. Szukamy bramki (sprawdzamy zarówno ID bramki, jak i jej target)
                let gates = Engine.map.gateways.getList();
                let celBramka = gates.find(b =>
                    b.d &&
                    (parseInt(b.d.id) === step.targetMapId || parseInt(b.d.target) === step.targetMapId)
                );

                if (celBramka) {
                    let distX = Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.x - celBramka.d.x);
                    let distY = Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.y - celBramka.d.y);

                    if (distX > 1 || distY > 1) {
                        Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: celBramka.d.x, y: celBramka.d.y });
                        lastActionTime = now + 800;
                    } else {
                        // Używamy funkcji forceInteract do kliknięcia w bramkę
                        forceInteract(celBramka);
                        console.log(`[Bot] Kliknięto bramkę prowadzącą do ID: ${step.targetMapId}`);
                        lastActionTime = now + 2500; // Czas na zmianę mapy
                    }
                } else if (step.x !== undefined && step.y !== undefined) {
                    // Jeśli bot nie widzi bramki, idzie w jej koordynaty (metoda awaryjna)
                    Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: step.x, y: step.y });
                    lastActionTime = now + 800;
                } else {
                    console.warn(`[Bot] Nie widzę bramki o ID: ${step.targetMapId}`);
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                }
                break;
                // ==================================================
            // CASE: CZEKANIE (SLEEP)
            // ==================================================
            case 'sleep':
                let sleepTime = step.time || 1000; // domyślnie 1 sekunda, jeśli nie podasz czasu
                console.log(`[Bot] Śpię przez ${sleepTime}ms`);
                lastActionTime = now + sleepTime;
                currentStepIndex++;
                break;
            // ==================================================
                // ==================================================
            // CASE: ZAMYKANIE OKNA RZEMIOSŁA (Wersja Precyzyjna)
            // ==================================================
            case 'craft_close':
                // Szukamy przycisku zamknięcia tylko w oknie z klasą .barter-window
                // .window-on-peak gwarantuje, że dotyczy to aktywnego okna
                let craftCloseBtn = document.querySelector('.barter-window.window-on-peak .close-button');

                if (craftCloseBtn) {
                    craftCloseBtn.click();
                    console.log("[Bot] Zamknięto okno Rzemiosła.");
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000; // Czas na zamknięcie
                } else {
                    console.log("[Bot] Nie znaleziono aktywnego okna Rzemiosła, pomijam.");
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                }
                break;
            // ==================================================

                // ==================================================
            // CASE: KLIKANIE PRZYCISKU "UŻYJ" W RZEMIOŚLE
            // ==================================================
            case 'craft_use':
                // Szukamy wszystkich przycisków na ekranie
                let allButtons = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.button'));
                // Znajdujemy ten, który ma tekst "Użyj"
                let useBtn = allButtons.find(b => b.innerText.trim() === "Użyj");

                if (useBtn) {
                    useBtn.click();
                    console.log("[Bot] Kliknięto: Użyj");
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000; // Czas na przetworzenie
                } else {
                    console.warn("[Bot] Nie znaleziono przycisku 'Użyj'.");
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                }
                break;
            // ==================================================
                // ==================================================
            // CASE: RZEMIOSŁO (Wybór przepisu i wykonanie)
            // ==================================================
            case 'craft_item':
                // Szukamy wszystkich przepisów na liście
                let recipes = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.crafting-recipe-in-list'));

                // Znajdujemy ten, który zawiera naszą nazwę przedmiotu
                let targetRecipe = recipes.find(el => {
                    let nameEl = el.querySelector('.name');
                    return nameEl && nameEl.innerText.includes(step.itemName);
                });

                if (targetRecipe) {
                    // Sprawdzamy czy przepis jest już zaznaczony (ma klasę 'active')
                    if (targetRecipe.classList.contains('active')) {
                        // Jest zaznaczony, więc klikamy przycisk "Wykonaj"
                        let craftBtn = document.querySelector('.do-recipe');
                        if (craftBtn) {
                            craftBtn.click();
                            console.log(`[Bot] Rzemiosło: Wykonano ${step.itemName}`);
                            currentStepIndex++;
                            lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                        } else {
                            lastActionTime = now + 500;
                        }
                    } else {
                        // Nie jest zaznaczony, klikamy w przepis
                        targetRecipe.click();
                        console.log(`[Bot] Rzemiosło: Wybrano ${step.itemName}`);
                        lastActionTime = now + 500;
                    }
                } else {
                    console.warn(`[Bot] Nie znaleziono przepisu: ${step.itemName}`);
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                }
                break;
            // ==================================================
                // ==================================================
            // CASE: PRZENOSZENIE TORBY (Pełna kontrola)
            // ==================================================
            // ==================================================
            // CASE: PRZENOSZENIE PRZEDMIOTU (DRAG & DROP)
            // ==================================================
            case 'move_bag':
                // Szukamy przedmiotu po TPL i slotu docelowego po klasie (np. 'bag-2-slot')
                let sourceItem = document.querySelector(`.item-tpl-${step.tpl}`);
                let targetSlot = document.querySelector(`.${step.target}`);

                if (sourceItem && targetSlot) {
                    let sRect = sourceItem.getBoundingClientRect();
                    let tRect = targetSlot.getBoundingClientRect();

                    // 1. Chwycenie przedmiotu (mousedown)
                    sourceItem.dispatchEvent(new MouseEvent('mousedown', { bubbles: true, clientX: sRect.left + 16, clientY: sRect.top + 16 }));

                    // 2. "Ruch" myszką do slotu (mousemove - to jest kluczowe dla jQuery UI)
                    document.dispatchEvent(new MouseEvent('mousemove', { bubbles: true, clientX: tRect.left + 16, clientY: tRect.top + 16 }));

                    // 3. Upuszczenie (mouseup)
                    targetSlot.dispatchEvent(new MouseEvent('mouseup', { bubbles: true, clientX: tRect.left + 16, clientY: tRect.top + 16 }));

                    console.log(`[Bot] Przeniesiono przedmiot tpl-${step.tpl} do ${step.target}.`);
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                } else {
                    console.warn(`[Bot] Nie znaleziono przedmiotu (tpl: ${step.tpl}) lub slotu docelowego (.${step.target}).`);
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                }
                break;
                // ==================================================
            // CASE: ZAMYKANIE OKNA SKLEPU
            // ==================================================
            // ==================================================
            // CASE: ZAMYKANIE OKNA SKLEPU (Poprawka)
            // ==================================================
            // ==================================================
            // CASE: ZAMYKANIE OKNA SKLEPU (Wersja Precyzyjna)
            // ==================================================
            case 'shop_close':
                // 1. Znajdujemy wszystkie okna
                let allWindows = document.querySelectorAll('.c-window');
                let shopWindow = Array.from(allWindows).find(win => {
                    let header = win.querySelector('.header-label .text');
                    return header && header.innerText.includes("Sklep");
                });

                // 2. Jeśli znaleźliśmy okno sklepu, szukamy w nim przycisku zamykania
                if (shopWindow) {
                    let closeBtn = shopWindow.querySelector('.close-button-corner-decor .close-button');
                    if (closeBtn) {
                        closeBtn.click();
                        console.log("[Bot] Zamknięto okno Sklepu.");
                        currentStepIndex++;
                        lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                    } else {
                        console.warn("[Bot] Znaleziono okno Sklepu, ale nie ma w nim przycisku zamknięcia!");
                        currentStepIndex++;
                        lastActionTime = now + 500;
                    }
                } else {
                    // Jeśli okna z napisem "Sklep" nie ma, to znaczy że już jest zamknięte
                    console.log("[Bot] Okno sklepu już zamknięte.");
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                }
                break;

                // ==================================================
            // CASE: KLIKANIE PRZEDMIOTU W SKLEPIE
            // ==================================================
            case 'shop_buy':
                // Szukamy przedmiotu po jego ID (np. item-id-65)
                let itemToBuy = document.querySelector(`.shop-items .item-id-${step.itemId}`);
                if (itemToBuy) {
                    itemToBuy.click();
                    console.log(`[Bot] Kliknięto przedmiot o ID: ${step.itemId}`);
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                } else {
                    console.warn(`[Bot] Nie widzę przedmiotu o ID: ${step.itemId} w sklepie.`);
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                }
                break;

            // ==================================================
            // CASE: AKCEPTACJA ZAKUPU
            // ==================================================
            case 'shop_accept':
                // Szukamy przycisku "Akceptuj" wewnątrz kontenera finalize-button
                let acceptBtn = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.finalize-button .button'))
                                     .find(el => el.innerText.includes("Akceptuj"));

                if (acceptBtn) {
                    acceptBtn.click();
                    console.log("[Bot] Akceptowano zakup/sprzedaż.");
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                } else {
                    // Czekamy, aż przycisk się pojawi
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                }
                break;

            case 'alert_confirm':
                let btnClass = (step.option === 'no') ? '.alert-cancel-hotkey' : '.alert-accept-hotkey';
                let alertBtn = document.querySelector(btnClass);

                if (alertBtn) {
                    alertBtn.click();
                    console.log(`[Bot] Kliknięto '${step.option === 'no' ? 'Nie' : 'Tak'}' w oknie potwierdzenia.`);
                    //                   { action: "alert_confirm", desc: "Kliknij TAK" }
                    //                   { action: "alert_confirm", option: "no", desc: "Kliknij NIE" }
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                } else {
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                }
                break;

            case 'choose_prof':
                let outfitCards = document.querySelectorAll('.outfit-card');

                if (outfitCards.length > 0) {
                    let targetCard = Array.from(outfitCards).find(card => {
                        let textEl = card.querySelector('.text');
                        return textEl && textEl.innerText.trim().toLowerCase() === step.profName.toLowerCase();
                    });

                    if (targetCard) {
                        let borderEl = targetCard.querySelector('.outfit-border');

                        if (borderEl && borderEl.classList.contains('active')) {
                            let confirmBtn = document.querySelector('.button.confirmButton');

                            if (confirmBtn && !confirmBtn.classList.contains('disable')) {
                                confirmBtn.click();
                                console.log(`[Bot] Wybrano profesję: ${step.profName} i zatwierdzono.`);
                                currentStepIndex++;
                                lastActionTime = now + 1500;
                            } else {
                                lastActionTime = now + 300;
                            }
                        } else {
                            targetCard.click();
                            console.log(`[Bot] Klikam w profesję: ${step.profName}`);
                            lastActionTime = now + 500;
                        }
                    } else {
                        console.warn(`[Bot] Nie znaleziono karty profesji: ${step.profName}`);
                        lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                    }
                } else {
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                }
                break;

            case 'follow_arrow':
                if (!window._celQuesta && typeof Engine.targets.getTargets === 'function') {
                    let tgts = Engine.targets.getTargets();
                    let k = Object.keys(tgts)[0];
                    if (k && tgts[k]) window._celQuesta = { x: tgts[k].x, y: tgts[k].y };
                }

                if (window._celQuesta) {
                    let cel = window._celQuesta;
                    let distX = Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.x - cel.x);
                    let distY = Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.y - cel.y);

                    let isCollision = false;
                    if (typeof Engine.map.col.check === 'function') {
                        isCollision = Engine.map.col.check(cel.x, cel.y);
                    }
                    let targetDist = isCollision ? 1 : 0;

                    if (distX <= targetDist && distY <= targetDist) {
                        currentStepIndex++;
                        lastActionTime = now + 500;
                    } else {
                        Engine.hero.autoGoTo(cel);
                        lastActionTime = now + 800;
                    }
                } else {
                    console.warn("[Bot] Szukam strzałki questa...");
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                }
                break;

            case 'move':
                if (Engine.hero.d.x === step.x && Engine.hero.d.y === step.y) {
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 200;
                } else {
                    Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: step.x, y: step.y });
                    lastActionTime = now + 800;
                }
                break;

            case 'talk':
                let npcsTalk = Object.values(Engine.npcs.check()).filter(n => n.d && n.d.nick.toLowerCase().includes(step.nick.toLowerCase()));
                let gws = Engine.map.gateways.getList().filter(g => g.d && g.tip && g.tip[0].toLowerCase().includes(step.nick.toLowerCase()));

                // Łączymy wszystko w jedną listę kandydatów
                let candidates = [
                    ...npcsTalk.map(n => ({ d: n.d, obj: n, type: 'npc' })),
                    ...gws.map(g => ({ d: g.d, obj: g, type: 'gateway' }))
                ];

                // Jeśli podano konkretne X i Y w zadaniu, zawężamy listę tylko do tego punktu
                if (step.x !== undefined && step.y !== undefined) {
                    candidates = candidates.filter(c => c.d.x === step.x && c.d.y === step.y);
                }

                // Znajdujemy najbliższego
                let tTarget = null;
                let minDist = Infinity;

                candidates.forEach(c => {
                    let dist = Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.x - c.d.x) + Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.y - c.d.y);
                    if (dist < minDist) {
                        minDist = dist;
                        tTarget = c;
                    }
                });

                if (tTarget) {
                    let distX = Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.x - tTarget.d.x);
                    let distY = Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.y - tTarget.d.y);

                    if (distX > 1 || distY > 1) {
                        Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: tTarget.d.x, y: tTarget.d.y });
                        lastActionTime = now + 800;
                    } else {
                        // forceInteract wymaga obiektu z funkcją onclick
                        // Dostosowujemy obiekt w zależności czy to NPC czy Gateway
                        let interactObj = (tTarget.type === 'npc') ? tTarget.obj : { d: tTarget.d, onclick: tTarget.obj.onclick };
                        forceInteract(interactObj);
                        currentStepIndex++;
                        lastActionTime = now + 1500;
                    }
                } else {
                    console.warn(`[Bot] Nie widzę obiektu: ${step.nick}`);
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                }
                break;

            case 'attack':
                let npcsAttack = Object.values(Engine.npcs.check());
                let aTarget = null;

                if (step.targetId) {
                    aTarget = npcsAttack.find(n => n.d && n.d.id === step.targetId);
                } else {
                    aTarget = npcsAttack.find(n => {
                        if (!n.d || !(n.d.type === 2 || n.d.type === 3) || !n.d.nick.toLowerCase().includes(step.nick.toLowerCase())) return false;
                        if (step.x !== undefined && step.y !== undefined) {
                            return n.d.x === step.x && n.d.y === step.y;
                        }
                        return true;
                    });
                    if (aTarget) step.targetId = aTarget.d.id;
                }

                if (aTarget) {
                    let distX = Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.x - aTarget.d.x);
                    let distY = Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.y - aTarget.d.y);

                    if (distX > 1 || distY > 1) {
                        Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: aTarget.d.x, y: aTarget.d.y });
                        lastActionTime = now + 800;
                    } else {
                        forceInteract(aTarget);
                        lastActionTime = now + 2000;
                    }
                } else {
                    if (step.targetId) {
                        console.log(`[Bot] Cel pokonany! Przechodzę dalej.`);
                        currentStepIndex++;
                        delete step.targetId;
                        lastActionTime = now + 500;
                    } else {
                        document.getElementById('quest-bot-status').innerText = "Czekam na potwora...";
                        lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                    }
                }
                break;

            case 'equip':
                let itemElement = document.querySelector(`.item-tpl-${step.tpl}.inventory-item`);
                if (itemElement) {
                    let event = new MouseEvent('dblclick', { bubbles: true, cancelable: true, view: window });
                    itemElement.dispatchEvent(event);
                    console.log("[Bot] Założono przedmiot.");
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                } else {
                    console.warn("[Bot] Przedmiot założony.");
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                }
                break;

            case 'dialog':
                let opcje = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.dialogue-window-answer, .dialog-answer, .answer'))
                                 .filter(el => el.offsetParent !== null);

                if (opcje.length > 0) {
                    if (typeof Engine !== 'undefined' && Engine.dialogue && typeof Engine.dialogue.choose === 'function') {
                        try {
                            Engine.dialogue.choose(step.option - 1);
                            currentStepIndex++;
                            lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                            break;
                        } catch(e) {}
                    }

                    if (opcje.length >= step.option) {
                        opcje[step.option - 1].click();
                        currentStepIndex++;
                        lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                    } else {
                        console.warn(`[Bot] Za mało opcji dialogowych. Oczekiwano ${step.option}, znaleziono ${opcje.length}`);
                        lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                    }
                } else {
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                }
                break;

            case 'wait_map':
                if (Engine.map && Engine.map.d && Engine.map.d.name.includes(step.mapName)) {
                    currentStepIndex++;
                    lastActionTime = now + 500;
                } else {
                    lastActionTime = now + 1000;
                }
                break;
        }
    }

    // ==========================================
    // INICJALIZACJA Z PRZECHWYTYWANIEM STRZAŁEK
    // ==========================================
    function initBot() {
        let initTimer = setInterval(() => {
            if (typeof Engine !== 'undefined' && Engine.targets) {
                clearInterval(initTimer);

                const origAdd = Engine.targets.addArrow;
                const origDel = Engine.targets.deleteArrow;

                Engine.targets.addArrow = function(...args) {
                    if (args[2] && args[2].x !== undefined) {
                        window._celQuesta = { x: args[2].x, y: args[2].y };
                    }
                    return origAdd.apply(this, args);
                };

                Engine.targets.deleteArrow = function(id) {
                    window._celQuesta = null;
                    return origDel.apply(this, arguments);
                };

                createUI();
            }
        }, 1000);
    }

    // ==========================================
    // INTERFEJS (Z LISTĄ ROZWIJANĄ)
    // ==========================================
    function createUI() {
        let savedX = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('margo_quest_x'), 10) || 20;
        let savedY = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('margo_quest_y'), 10) || 350;

        const menuHTML = `
            <div id="quest-bot-menu" style="position: fixed; top: ${savedY}px; left: ${savedX}px; z-index: 999999; background: rgba(20, 20, 20, 0.95); border: 2px solid #f39c12; color: #fff; font-family: Tahoma, sans-serif; font-size: 11px; padding: 12px; border-radius: 6px; width: 180px; box-shadow: 0 0 10px rgba(0,0,0,0.8);">
                <div id="quest-bot-header" style="cursor: move; user-select: none; font-weight: bold; text-align: center; margin-bottom: 8px; border-bottom: 1px solid #444; padding-bottom: 5px; color: #f39c12;">Quest Bot 📜</div>
                <div id="quest-bot-status" style="text-align: center; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: #7f8c8d;">Wstrzymano</div>
                <div id="quest-bot-step" style="text-align: center; color: #3498db; font-size: 10px; margin-bottom: 8px; min-height: 15px; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center;">Gotowy do rozpoczęcia</div>

                <div style="margin-bottom: 10px;">
                    <select id="quest-step-select" style="width: 100%; padding: 4px; background: #2c3e50; color: #ecf0f1; border: 1px solid #34495e; border-radius: 4px; font-size: 10px; cursor: pointer;">
                        </select>
                </div>

                <div style="display: flex; gap: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px;">
                    <button id="quest-prev-btn" title="Cofnij o jeden krok" style="flex: 1; padding: 6px; border: none; border-radius: 4px; cursor: pointer; background: #34495e; color: #fff;">⏪</button>
                    <button id="quest-toggle-btn" style="flex: 2; padding: 6px; border: none; border-radius: 4px; cursor: pointer; font-weight: bold; background: #27ae60; color: #fff;">▶ START</button>
                    <button id="quest-next-btn" title="Pomiń krok" style="flex: 1; padding: 6px; border: none; border-radius: 4px; cursor: pointer; background: #34495e; color: #fff;">⏩</button>
                </div>

                <div style="display: flex; gap: 5px;">
                    <button id="quest-reset-btn" style="width: 100%; padding: 4px; border: none; border-radius: 4px; cursor: pointer; font-weight: bold; background: #c0392b; color: #fff;">↺ RESET OD NOWA</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;

        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.innerHTML = menuHTML;
        document.body.appendChild(div);

        // --- WYPEŁNIENIE LISTY ROZWIJANEJ KROKAMI ---
        const selectEl = document.getElementById('quest-step-select');
        QUEST_SEQUENCE.forEach((step, index) => {
            let opt = document.createElement('option');
            opt.value = index;
            opt.innerText = `[Krok ${index + 1}] ${step.desc}`;
            selectEl.appendChild(opt);
        });

        // Nasłuchiwanie zmiany na liście rozwijanej
        selectEl.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            currentStepIndex = parseInt(e.target.value, 10);
            updateDisplay();
            console.log(`[Bot] Przeskoczono do kroku ${currentStepIndex + 1}.`);
        });
        // ------------------------------------------

        document.getElementById('quest-toggle-btn').addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (currentStepIndex >= QUEST_SEQUENCE.length) return;

            isRunning = !isRunning;
            if (isRunning) {
                e.target.innerHTML = "⏸ PAUZA";
                e.target.style.background = "#e67e22";
                document.getElementById('quest-bot-status').innerText = "W Trakcie...";
                document.getElementById('quest-bot-status').style.color = "#f39c12";
                sequenceInterval = setInterval(processSequence, 300);
            } else {
                e.target.innerHTML = "▶ START";
                e.target.style.background = "#27ae60";
                document.getElementById('quest-bot-status').innerText = "Wstrzymano";
                document.getElementById('quest-bot-status').style.color = "#7f8c8d";
                clearInterval(sequenceInterval);
            }
        });

        document.getElementById('quest-prev-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {
            if (currentStepIndex > 0) { currentStepIndex--; updateDisplay(); }
        });

        document.getElementById('quest-next-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {
            if (currentStepIndex < QUEST_SEQUENCE.length - 1) { currentStepIndex++; updateDisplay(); }
        });

        document.getElementById('quest-reset-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {
            isRunning = false;
            clearInterval(sequenceInterval);
            currentStepIndex = 0;
            QUEST_SEQUENCE.forEach(s => { if(s.targetId) delete s.targetId; });
            document.getElementById('quest-toggle-btn').innerHTML = "▶ START";
            document.getElementById('quest-toggle-btn').style.background = "#27ae60";
            document.getElementById('quest-bot-status').innerText = "Zresetowano";
            document.getElementById('quest-bot-status').style.color = "#7f8c8d";
            updateDisplay();
        });

        updateDisplay();

        const menuEl = document.getElementById('quest-bot-menu');
        const headerEl = document.getElementById('quest-bot-header');
        let isDragging = false, offsetX = 0, offsetY = 0;

        headerEl.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
            // Zablokowanie przeciągania na przyciskach i listach
            if(['BUTTON', 'SELECT', 'OPTION'].includes(e.target.tagName)) return;
            isDragging = true;
            offsetX = e.clientX - menuEl.getBoundingClientRect().left;
            offsetY = e.clientY - menuEl.getBoundingClientRect().top;
        });
        document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => { if (isDragging) { menuEl.style.left = (e.clientX - offsetX) + 'px'; menuEl.style.top = (e.clientY - offsetY) + 'px'; } });
        document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => { if (isDragging) { isDragging = false; localStorage.setItem('margo_quest_x', parseInt(menuEl.style.left, 10)); localStorage.setItem('margo_quest_y', parseInt(menuEl.style.top, 10)); } });
    }

    initBot();

})();
// ==UserScript==
// @name         Margonem Bot (Nowy Interfejs)
// @namespace    http://tampermonkey.net/
// @version      1.2
// @description  Bot do Margonem.pl działający na nowym interfejsie (WebGL/Canvas)
// @author       TwójNick
// @match        https://*.margonem.pl/
// @match        https://*.margonem.com/
// @grant        none
// @run-at       document-idle
// ==/UserScript==

(function() {
    'use strict';

    // ====== KONFIGURACJA ======
    const config = {
        debugMode: true,          // Tryb debugowania (logi w konsoli)
        decisionInterval: 1500,   // Co ile ms podejmować decyzje
        safeMode: true,           // Tryb bezpieczny - nie atakuje graczy
        minHpToFight: 0.5,        // Minimalny % HP, aby atakować (0.5 = 50%)
        minMpToUseSkill: 0.3,     // Minimalny % MP, aby używać umiejętności
        maxMonsterDistance: 3,    // Maksymalna odległość ataku
        maxItemDistance: 2,       // Maksymalna odległość podnoszenia przedmiotów
        fleeThreshold: 0.2,       // Uciekaj, jeśli HP < 20%
        avoidNpcs: ['Strażnik', 'Mistrz Gildii'], // NPC do unikania
        questRefreshInterval: 30000, // Co ile ms odświeżać questy
        pathfinding: {
            maxSteps: 20,         // Maksymalna liczba kroków w szukaniu ścieżki
            avoidObstacles: true  // Unikaj przeszkód
        }
    };

    // ====== STAN GRY ======
    const gameState = {
        player: {
            hp: 0,
            maxHp: 0,
            mp: 0,
            maxMp: 0,
            level: 0,
            position: { x: 0, y: 0 },
            target: null,
            skills: [],
            buffs: []
        },
        map: {
            name: '',
            size: { width: 100, height: 100 },
            monsters: [],
            players: [],
            npcs: [],
            items: [],
            obstacles: []
        },
        quests: {
            active: [],
            completed: [],
            available: []
        },
        killedMonsters: {},
        lastAction: null,
        lastActionTime: 0,
        isFighting: false,
        isMoving: false,
        mode: 'exp' // exp, quest, heros, e2
    };

    // ====== INICJALIZACJA ======
    function init() {
        log('[Margonem Bot] Inicjalizacja bota dla nowego interfejsu...');

        // Czekaj, aż gra się załaduje
        const checkGameLoaded = setInterval(() => {
            if (typeof window.Engine !== 'undefined' && window.Engine.game) {
                clearInterval(checkGameLoaded);
                log('[Margonem Bot] Gra załadowana, inicjalizacja bota...');
                addUI();
                startGameMonitoring();
                startDecisionLoop();
                startQuestMonitoring();
                log('[Margonem Bot] Bot zainicjalizowany. Tryb: ' + gameState.mode);
            }
        }, 1000);
    }

    // ====== FUNKCJE POMOCNICZE ======
    function log(message) {
        if (!config.debugMode) return;

        const logElement = document.getElementById('margo-bot-log');
        if (logElement) {
            const time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
            const logEntry = document.createElement('div');
            logEntry.textContent = `[${time}] ${message}`;
            logElement.appendChild(logEntry);
            logElement.scrollTop = logElement.scrollHeight;
        }

        console.log(`[Margonem Bot] ${message}`);
    }

    function calculateDistance(pos1, pos2) {
        return Math.sqrt(Math.pow(pos1.x - pos2.x, 2) + Math.pow(pos1.y - pos2.y, 2));
    }

    function isPositionWalkable(position) {
        if (!window.Engine.game.map.collision) return true;

        const collision = window.Engine.game.map.collision;
        const x = Math.floor(position.x);
        const y = Math.floor(position.y);

        if (x < 0 || x >= collision[0].length || y < 0 || y >= collision.length) {
            return false;
        }

        return !collision[y][x];
    }

    // ====== INTERFEJS UŻYTKOWNIKA ======
    function addUI() {
        const ui = document.createElement('div');
        ui.id = 'margo-bot-ui';
        ui.style.position = 'fixed';
        ui.style.bottom = '10px';
        ui.style.right = '10px';
        ui.style.zIndex = '99999';
        ui.style.backgroundColor = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.8)';
        ui.style.color = 'white';
        ui.style.padding = '10px';
        ui.style.borderRadius = '5px';
        ui.style.fontFamily = 'Arial, sans-serif';
        ui.style.fontSize = '12px';
        ui.style.width = '300px';

        ui.innerHTML = `
            <h3 style="margin: 0 0 10px 0;">Margonem Bot (Nowy Interfejs)</h3>
            <div id="margo-bot-status">Status: Inicjalizacja...</div>
            <div style="margin: 10px 0;">
                <strong>Tryb:</strong>
                <select id="margo-bot-mode" style="margin-left: 5px;">
                    <option value="exp">Expienie</option>
                    <option value="quest">Robienie questów</option>
                    <option value="heros">Szukanie herosów</option>
                    <option value="e2">Stanie na E2</option>
                </select>
            </div>
            <div id="margo-bot-actions" style="margin: 10px 0;">
                <button id="margo-toggle-bot" style="margin-right: 5px;">Włącz/Wyłącz</button>
                <button id="margo-debug-info" style="margin-right: 5px;">Debug</button>
                <button id="margo-clear-killed">Wyczyść zabite</button>
            </div>
            <div style="margin: 10px 0;">
                <strong>Opcje:</strong><br>
                <label><input type="checkbox" id="margo-auto-use-skills" checked> Automatyczne używanie umiejętności</label><br>
                <label><input type="checkbox" id="margo-auto-pick-items" checked> Automatyczne podnoszenie przedmiotów</label><br>
                <label><input type="checkbox" id="margo-avoid-npcs" checked> Unikaj określonych NPC</label>
            </div>
            <div id="margo-bot-log" style="margin-top: 10px; max-height: 200px; overflow-y: auto; border: 1px solid #333; padding: 5px; background: rgba(0,0,0,0.5);"></div>
        `;

        document.body.appendChild(ui);

        document.getElementById('margo-toggle-bot').addEventListener('click', toggleBot);
        document.getElementById('margo-debug-info').addEventListener('click', showDebugInfo);
        document.getElementById('margo-clear-killed').addEventListener('click', clearKilledMonsters);
        document.getElementById('margo-bot-mode').addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            gameState.mode = e.target.value;
            log(`Zmieniono tryb na: ${gameState.mode}`);
        });
    }

    function toggleBot() {
        const statusElement = document.getElementById('margo-bot-status');
        if (statusElement.textContent.includes('Aktywny')) {
            statusElement.textContent = 'Status: Wyłączony';
            statusElement.style.color = 'red';
            log('Bot wyłączony');
        } else {
            statusElement.textContent = 'Status: Aktywny';
            statusElement.style.color = 'lime';
            log('Bot włączony');
        }
    }

    function showDebugInfo() {
        log('=== DEBUG INFO ===');
        log(`Tryb: ${gameState.mode}`);
        log(`Pozycja: ${gameState.player.position.x}, ${gameState.player.position.y}`);
        log(`HP: ${gameState.player.hp}/${gameState.player.maxHp} (${Math.round((gameState.player.hp / gameState.player.maxHp) * 100)}%)`);
        log(`MP: ${gameState.player.mp}/${gameState.player.maxMp} (${Math.round((gameState.player.mp / gameState.player.maxMp) * 100)}%)`);
        log(`Poziom: ${gameState.player.level}`);
        log(`Mapa: ${gameState.map.name}`);
        log(`Potwory w pobliżu: ${gameState.map.monsters.length}`);
        log(`Gracze w pobliżu: ${gameState.map.players.length}`);
        log(`Przedmioty na ziemi: ${gameState.map.items.length}`);
        log(`Aktywne questy: ${gameState.quests.active.length}`);
        log('==================');
    }

    function clearKilledMonsters() {
        gameState.killedMonsters = {};
        log('Wyczyszczono listę zabitych potworów');
    }

    // ====== MONITOROWANIE GRY ======
    function startGameMonitoring() {
        setInterval(updateGameState, 1000);
    }

    function updateGameState() {
        if (!window.Engine || !window.Engine.game) return;

        try {
            updatePlayerInfo();
            updateMapInfo();
            updateUIStatus();
        } catch (e) {
            log(`Błąd aktualizacji stanu gry: ${e.message}`);
        }
    }

    function updatePlayerInfo() {
        const player = window.Engine.game.player;

        if (!player) return;

        gameState.player.hp = player.hp;
        gameState.player.maxHp = player.max_hp;
        gameState.player.mp = player.mp;
        gameState.player.maxMp = player.max_mp;
        gameState.player.level = player.level;
        gameState.player.position = { x: player.x, y: player.y };
        gameState.player.target = player.target ? player.target.nick : null;

        gameState.player.skills = [];
        if (player.skills) {
            for (const skillId in player.skills) {
                const skill = player.skills[skillId];
                gameState.player.skills.push({
                    name: skill.name,
                    cooldown: skill.cooldown > 0,
                    lastUsed: 0
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.player.buffs = [];
        if (player.buffs) {
            for (const buffId in player.buffs) {
                const buff = player.buffs[buffId];
                gameState.player.buffs.push(buff.name);
            }
        }

        gameState.isFighting = player.inFight;
    }

    function updateMapInfo() {
        const game = window.Engine.game;

        if (!game || !game.map) return;

        gameState.map.name = game.map.name || 'Nieznana';
        gameState.map.size = {
            width: game.map.width || 100,
            height: game.map.height || 100
        };

        gameState.map.monsters = [];
        if (game.map.monsters) {
            for (const monsterId in game.map.monsters) {
                const monster = game.map.monsters[monsterId];
                gameState.map.monsters.push({
                    id: monsterId,
                    name: monster.name,
                    position: { x: monster.x, y: monster.y },
                    hp: monster.hp,
                    maxHp: monster.max_hp,
                    level: monster.level,
                    distance: calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, { x: monster.x, y: monster.y }),
                    isBoss: monster.boss
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.map.monsters.sort((a, b) => {
            if (a.isBoss && !b.isBoss) return -1;
            if (!a.isBoss && b.isBoss) return 1;

            const aHpPercent = a.hp / a.maxHp;
            const bHpPercent = b.hp / b.maxHp;
            if (aHpPercent < 0.3 && bHpPercent >= 0.3) return -1;
            if (bHpPercent < 0.3 && aHpPercent >= 0.3) return 1;

            return b.level - a.level;
        });

        gameState.map.players = [];
        if (game.map.players) {
            for (const playerId in game.map.players) {
                const player = game.map.players[playerId];
                if (player.nick === game.player.nick) continue;

                gameState.map.players.push({
                    name: player.nick,
                    position: { x: player.x, y: player.y },
                    distance: calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, { x: player.x, y: player.y }),
                    isHeros: player.nick.includes('[Heros]') || player.nick.includes('Heros')
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.map.npcs = [];
        if (game.map.npcs) {
            for (const npcId in game.map.npcs) {
                const npc = game.map.npcs[npcId];
                gameState.map.npcs.push({
                    id: npcId,
                    name: npc.name,
                    position: { x: npc.x, y: npc.y },
                    distance: calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, { x: npc.x, y: npc.y }),
                    isQuestNpc: npc.quest
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.map.items = [];
        if (game.map.items) {
            for (const itemId in game.map.items) {
                const item = game.map.items[itemId];
                gameState.map.items.push({
                    id: itemId,
                    name: item.name,
                    position: { x: item.x, y: item.y },
                    distance: calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, { x: item.x, y: item.y }),
                    isGold: item.name.includes('Złoto'),
                    isQuestItem: item.quest
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.map.obstacles = [];
        if (game.map.collision) {
            const collision = game.map.collision;
            for (let y = 0; y < collision.length; y++) {
                for (let x = 0; x < collision[y].length; x++) {
                    if (collision[y][x]) {
                        gameState.map.obstacles.push({ x, y });
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function updateUIStatus() {
        const statusElement = document.getElementById('margo-bot-status');
        if (statusElement) {
            const modeText = {
                'exp': 'Expienie',
                'quest': 'Robienie questów',
                'heros': 'Szukanie herosów',
                'e2': 'Stanie na E2'
            }[gameState.mode] || gameState.mode;

            statusElement.textContent = `Status: ${gameState.isFighting ? 'Walka' : 'Spokój'} | Tryb: ${modeText} | Poziom: ${gameState.player.level}`;
        }
    }

    // ====== MONITOROWANIE QUESTÓW ======
    function startQuestMonitoring() {
        setInterval(updateQuests, config.questRefreshInterval);
    }

    function updateQuests() {
        if (!window.Engine || !window.Engine.game || !window.Engine.game.quests) return;

        try {
            const quests = window.Engine.game.quests;

            gameState.quests.active = [];
            if (quests.active) {
                for (const questId in quests.active) {
                    const quest = quests.active[questId];
                    gameState.quests.active.push({
                        id: questId,
                        name: quest.name,
                        progress: quest.progress,
                        isCompleted: quest.progress.current >= quest.progress.total
                    });
                }
            }

            gameState.quests.available = [];
            if (quests.available) {
                for (const questId in quests.available) {
                    const quest = quests.available[questId];
                    gameState.quests.available.push({
                        id: questId,
                        name: quest.name,
                        giver: quest.giver
                    });
                }
            }

            gameState.quests.completed = [];
            if (quests.completed) {
                for (const questId in quests.completed) {
                    const quest = quests.completed[questId];
                    gameState.quests.completed.push({
                        id: questId,
                        name: quest.name,
                        receiver: quest.receiver
                    });
                }
            }

            log(`Zaktualizowano questy. Aktywne: ${gameState.quests.active.length}, Dostępne: ${gameState.quests.available.length}, Ukończone: ${gameState.quests.completed.length}`);
        } catch (e) {
            log(`Błąd aktualizacji questów: ${e.message}`);
        }
    }

    // ====== CYKL DECYZYJNY ======
    function startDecisionLoop() {
        setInterval(makeDecision, config.decisionInterval);
    }

    function makeDecision() {
        if (!window.Engine || !window.Engine.game || !document.getElementById('margo-bot-status').textContent.includes('Aktywny')) {
            return;
        }

        try {
            if (gameState.isFighting) {
                handleCombat();
                return;
            }

            switch (gameState.mode) {
                case 'exp':
                    handleExpMode();
                    break;
                case 'quest':
                    handleQuestMode();
                    break;
                case 'heros':
                    handleHerosMode();
                    break;
                case 'e2':
                    handleE2Mode();
                    break;
                default:
                    handleExpMode();
            }
        } catch (e) {
            log(`Błąd podejmowania decyzji: ${e.message}`);
        }
    }

    // ====== TRYBY DZIAŁANIA ======
    function handleExpMode() {
        const decisions = [
            checkFleeCondition(),
            checkLowHp(),
            checkLowMp(),
            checkAttackableMonster(),
            checkPickableItem(),
            checkRandomMovement()
        ];

        const bestDecision = getBestDecision(decisions);
        executeDecision(bestDecision);
    }

    function handleQuestMode() {
        if (gameState.quests.completed.length > 0) {
            const quest = gameState.quests.completed[0];
            const npc = gameState.map.npcs.find(n => n.name === quest.receiver);

            if (npc) {
                if (npc.distance <= 1) {
                    return executeDecision({
                        action: 'turn_in_quest',
                        target: quest.id,
                        reason: `Oddaję quest: ${quest.name}`,
                        priority: 10
                    });
                } else {
                    return executeDecision({
                        action: 'move_to',
                        target: npc.position,
                        reason: `Idę oddać quest: ${quest.name}`,
                        priority: 10
                    });
                }
            }
        }

        if (gameState.quests.available.length > 0) {
            const quest = gameState.quests.available[0];
            const npc = gameState.map.npcs.find(n => n.name === quest.giver);

            if (npc) {
                if (npc.distance <= 1) {
                    return executeDecision({
                        action: 'accept_quest',
                        target: quest.id,
                        reason: `Przyjmuję quest: ${quest.name}`,
                        priority: 9
                    });
                } else {
                    return executeDecision({
                        action: 'move_to',
                        target: npc.position,
                        reason: `Idę przyjąć quest: ${quest.name}`,
                        priority: 9
                    });
                }
            }
        }

        handleExpMode();
    }

    function handleHerosMode() {
        const herosPlayers = gameState.map.players.filter(p => p.isHeros);

        if (herosPlayers.length > 0) {
            const closestHeros = herosPlayers[0];

            if (closestHeros.distance <= 1) {
                return executeDecision({
                    action: 'follow_player',
                    target: closestHeros.name,
                    reason: `Podążam za herosem: ${closestHeros.name}`,
                    priority: 8
                });
            } else {
                return executeDecision({
                    action: 'move_to',
                    target: closestHeros.position,
                    reason: `Idę do herosa: ${closestHeros.name}`,
                    priority: 8
                });
            }
        }

        handleExpMode();
    }

    function handleE2Mode() {
        const e2Position = { x: 50, y: 50 };

        if (calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, e2Position) <= 1) {
            return executeDecision({
                action: 'wait',
                reason: 'Stoję na E2',
                priority: 1
            });
        } else {
            return executeDecision({
                action: 'move_to',
                target: e2Position,
                reason: 'Idę na E2',
                priority: 10
            });
        }
    }

    // ====== DECYZJE ======
    function checkFleeCondition() {
        const hpPercentage = gameState.player.hp / gameState.player.maxHp;
        if (hpPercentage < config.fleeThreshold) {
            return { action: 'flee', reason: 'Niskie HP - ucieczka', priority: 10 };
        }
        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkLowHp() {
        const hpPercentage = gameState.player.hp / gameState.player.maxHp;
        if (hpPercentage < config.minHpToFight) {
            return { action: 'use_potion', target: 'hp', reason: 'Niskie HP', priority: 9 };
        }
        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkLowMp() {
        const mpPercentage = gameState.player.mp / gameState.player.maxMp;
        if (mpPercentage < config.minMpToUseSkill) {
            return { action: 'use_potion', target: 'mp', reason: 'Niskie MP', priority: 8 };
        }
        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkAttackableMonster() {
        if (gameState.map.monsters.length === 0) {
            return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
        }

        const closestMonster = gameState.map.monsters[0];

        if (gameState.killedMonsters[closestMonster.name] &&
            gameState.killedMonsters[closestMonster.name] >= 5) {
            log(`Potwór ${closestMonster.name} został już zabity wystarczająco razy, pomijam`);
            return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
        }

        if (closestMonster.distance <= config.maxMonsterDistance) {
            return {
                action: 'attack',
                target: closestMonster.id,
                reason: `Potwór ${closestMonster.name} (Lvl ${closestMonster.level}) w zasięgu`,
                priority: 7
            };
        }

        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkPickableItem() {
        if (!document.getElementById('margo-auto-pick-items')?.checked) {
            return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
        }

        if (gameState.map.items.length === 0) {
            return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
        }

        const closestItem = gameState.map.items[0];
        if (closestItem.distance <= config.maxItemDistance) {
            return {
                action: 'pick_up',
                target: closestItem.id,
                reason: `Przedmiot ${closestItem.name} w zasięgu`,
                priority: 6
            };
        }

        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkRandomMovement() {
        return { action: 'move_random', reason: 'Brak innych akcji', priority: 1 };
    }

    function getBestDecision(decisions) {
        return decisions.reduce((best, current) =>
            (current.priority > best.priority) ? current : best,
            { action: 'wait', priority: 0 }
        );
    }

    // ====== WYKONYWANIE DECYZJI ======
    function executeDecision(decision) {
        if (!decision || !decision.action || decision.priority === 0) {
            return;
        }

        gameState.lastAction = `${decision.action} ${decision.target ? `(${decision.target})` : ''}`;
        gameState.lastActionTime = Date.now();

        log(`Wykonuję: ${decision.action} (${decision.reason})`);

        switch (decision.action) {
            case 'attack':
                attackMonster(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'move_to':
                moveToPosition(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'pick_up':
                pickUpItem(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'use_potion':
                usePotion(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'use_skill':
                useSkill(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'flee':
                fleeFromCombat();
                break;
            case 'talk_to_npc':
                talkToNPC(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'accept_quest':
                acceptQuest(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'turn_in_quest':
                turnInQuest(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'follow_player':
                followPlayer(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'move_random':
                moveRandomly();
                break;
            case 'wait':
            default:
                log('Czekam...');
                break;
        }
    }

    // ====== AKCJE ======
    function attackMonster(monsterId) {
        const monster = gameState.map.monsters.find(m => m.id === monsterId);
        if (!monster) {
            log(`Nie znaleziono potwora o ID: ${monsterId}`);
            return;
        }

        if (monster.distance > 1) {
            log(`Potwór ${monster.name} jest za daleko (${monster.distance.toFixed(1)})`);
            moveToPosition(monster.position);
            return;
        }

        log(`Atakuję ${monster.name} (Lvl ${monster.level}, HP: ${monster.hp}/${monster.maxHp})`);

        if (!gameState.killedMonsters[monster.name]) {
            gameState.killedMonsters[monster.name] = 0;
        }
        gameState.killedMonsters[monster.name]++;

        window.Engine.game.attack(monsterId);

        if (document.getElementById('margo-auto-use-skills')?.checked) {
            useCombatSkills();
        }
    }

    function moveToPosition(position) {
        if (gameState.isMoving) return;

        const distance = calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, position);
        if (distance <= 1) {
            log(`Już jesteśmy przy celu (${position.x}, ${position.y})`);
            return;
        }

        log(`Poruszam się do (${position.x}, ${position.y})`);

        const path = findPath(gameState.player.position, position);
        if (path.length > 0) {
            const nextStep = path[0];
            window.Engine.game.move(nextStep.x, nextStep.y);
            gameState.isMoving = true;

            setTimeout(() => {
                gameState.isMoving = false;
            }, 1000);
        } else {
            log('Nie znaleziono ścieżki!');
            window.Engine.game.move(position.x, position.y);
        }
    }

    function findPath(start, end) {
        const openSet = [start];
        const cameFrom = {};
        const gScore = {};
        const fScore = {};

        gScore[start.x + ',' + start.y] = 0;
        fScore[start.x + ',' + start.y] = calculateDistance(start, end);

        while (openSet.length > 0) {
            let current = openSet[0];
            for (const node of openSet) {
                if (fScore[node.x + ',' + node.y] < fScore[current.x + ',' + current.y]) {
                    current = node;
                }
            }

            if (current.x === end.x && current.y === end.y) {
                const path = [];
                let temp = current;
                while (temp.x !== start.x || temp.y !== start.y) {
                    path.push(temp);
                    temp = cameFrom[temp.x + ',' + temp.y];
                }
                return path.reverse();
            }

            openSet.splice(openSet.indexOf(current), 1);

            const neighbors = [
                { x: current.x + 1, y: current.y },
                { x: current.x - 1, y: current.y },
                { x: current.x, y: current.y + 1 },
                { x: current.x, y: current.y - 1 }
            ];

            for (const neighbor of neighbors) {
                if (neighbor.x < 0 || neighbor.x >= gameState.map.size.width ||
                    neighbor.y < 0 || neighbor.y >= gameState.map.size.height) {
                    continue;
                }

                if (config.pathfinding.avoidObstacles && !isPositionWalkable(neighbor)) {
                    continue;
                }

                const tentativeGScore = gScore[current.x + ',' + current.y] + 1;

                if (!gScore[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y] ||
                    tentativeGScore < gScore[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y]) {
                    cameFrom[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y] = current;
                    gScore[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y] = tentativeGScore;
                    fScore[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y] = tentativeGScore + calculateDistance(neighbor, end);

                    if (!openSet.some(node => node.x === neighbor.x && node.y === neighbor.y)) {
                        openSet.push(neighbor);
                    }
                }
            }

            if (Object.keys(cameFrom).length > config.pathfinding.maxSteps) {
                log('Przekroczono maksymalną liczbę kroków w szukaniu ścieżki');
                return [];
            }
        }

        log('Nie znaleziono ścieżki!');
        return [];
    }

    function pickUpItem(itemId) {
        const item = gameState.map.items.find(i => i.id === itemId);
        if (!item) {
            log(`Nie znaleziono przedmiotu o ID: ${itemId}`);
            return;
        }

        if (item.distance > 1) {
            log(`Przedmiot ${item.name} jest za daleko (${item.distance.toFixed(1)})`);
            moveToPosition(item.position);
            return;
        }

        log(`Podnoszę ${item.name}`);
        window.Engine.game.pickUpItem(itemId);
    }

    function usePotion(type) {
        log(`Używam mikstury: ${type}`);
        window.Engine.game.usePotion(type);
    }

    function useSkill(skillName) {
        if (!document.getElementById('margo-auto-use-skills')?.checked) {
            return;
        }

        const skill = gameState.player.skills.find(s => s.name === skillName);
        if (!skill) {
            log(`Nie znaleziono umiejętności: ${skillName}`);
            return;
        }

        log(`Używam umiejętności: ${skillName}`);
        window.Engine.game.useSkill(skillName);
    }

    function useCombatSkills() {
        if (gameState.player.hp / gameState.player.maxHp < 0.5) {
            const healSkill = gameState.player.skills.find(s =>
                s.name.includes('Leczenie') || s.name.includes('Heal')
            );
            if (healSkill) {
                useSkill(healSkill.name);
                return;
            }
        }

        const offensiveSkills = gameState.player.skills.filter(s =>
            !s.cooldown &&
            (s.name.includes('Atak') || s.name.includes('Fireball') || s.name.includes('Błyskawica'))
        );

        if (offensiveSkills.length > 0) {
            useSkill(offensiveSkills[0].name);
        }
    }

    function fleeFromCombat() {
        log('Uciekam z walki!');
        window.Engine.game.flee();
    }

    function talkToNPC(npcId) {
        log(`Rozmawiam z NPC o ID: ${npcId}`);
        window.Engine.game.talkToNPC(npcId);
    }

    function acceptQuest(questId) {
        log(`Przyjmuję quest o ID: ${questId}`);
        window.Engine.game.acceptQuest(questId);
    }

    function turnInQuest(questId) {
        log(`Oddaję quest o ID: ${questId}`);
        window.Engine.game.turnInQuest(questId);
    }

    function followPlayer(playerName) {
        const player = gameState.map.players.find(p => p.name === playerName);
        if (!player) {
            log(`Nie znaleziono gracza: ${playerName}`);
            return;
        }

        if (player.distance <= 1) {
            log(`Podążam za graczem: ${playerName}`);
        } else {
            moveToPosition(player.position);
        }
    }

    function moveRandomly() {
        if (gameState.isMoving) return;

        const directions = [
            { x: 0, y: -1 },
            { x: 1, y: 0 },
            { x: 0, y: 1 },
            { x: -1, y: 0 }
        ];

        const randomDir = directions[Math.floor(Math.random() * directions.length)];
        const newPos = {
            x: gameState.player.position.x + randomDir.x,
            y: gameState.player.position.y + randomDir.y
        };

        if (newPos.x >= 0 && newPos.x < gameState.map.size.width &&
            newPos.y >= 0 && newPos.y < gameState.map.size.height &&
            isPositionWalkable(newPos)) {
            window.Engine.game.move(newPos.x, newPos.y);
        }
    }

    // ====== INICJALIZACJA ======
    init();
})();

// ==UserScript==
// @name         Follow The Leader
// @namespace    https://bettermargo.pl/private/
// @version      1.0.0
// @author       Sziki
// @description  Prywatny dodatek: wykrywa lidera grupy (party) i automatycznie podąża za nim po mapie.
// @match        http*://*.margonem.pl/
// @match        http*://*.margonem.com/
// @exclude      http*://forum.margonem.*/*
// @exclude      http*://commons.margonem.*/*
// @exclude      http*://dev-commons.margonem.*/*
// @run-at       document-idle
// ==/UserScript==

(function () {
  "use strict";

  // Tampermonkey (i inne) odpalają userscript w izolowanym świecie JS — DOM jest wspólny
  // ze stroną, ale zmienne globalne strony (jak `Engine`, ustawiane przez var/window.Engine=
  // w kodzie gry) NIE są widoczne przez zwykłe `window`/`globalThis` z tego świata.
  // `unsafeWindow` wskazuje na prawdziwe okno strony i to jedyny pewny sposób, by dobrać się
  // do żywego obiektu Engine. Bez tego heroD/party zawsze wychodzi undefined mimo że gra działa.
  const page = typeof unsafeWindow !== "undefined" ? unsafeWindow : window;

  const STORAGE_KEY = "ftl-enabled";
  const MINIMIZED_KEY = "ftl-minimized";
  const POS_KEY = "ftl-pos";
  const POLL_MS = 400;

  function loadPos() {
    try {
      const raw = localStorage.getItem(POS_KEY);
      if (!raw) return null;
      const parsed = JSON.parse(raw);
      if (Number.isFinite(parsed?.left) && Number.isFinite(parsed?.top)) return parsed;
    } catch (_) {}
    return null;
  }

  const state = {
    enabled: localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY) === "1",
    minimized: localStorage.getItem(MINIMIZED_KEY) === "1",
    pos: loadPos(),
    statusText: "Nieaktywny",
    leaderText: "Brak lidera",
    lastKnownLeaderId: null,
    blinkOn: false,
    ui: null,
  };

  function isInBattle() {
    const battle = page.Engine?.battle;
    if (battle && typeof battle.getShow === "function") {
      try {
        return !!battle.getShow();
      } catch (_) {}
    }
    // .battle-window jest tworzone raz przy starcie gry i tylko chowane/pokazywane —
    // istnieje w DOM zawsze, więc samo querySelector daje fałszywy pozytyw non-stop.
    // offsetParent === null gdy element (lub przodek) ma display:none.
    const el = document.querySelector(".battle-window, .battle-area");
    return !!el && el.offsetParent !== null;
  }

  // Engine.party.getLeaderId() w tym buildzie gry zawsze zwraca undefined (zweryfikowane
  // logami) — nie da się na tym polegać w ogóle. Jedyne wiarygodne źródło to korona w DOM
  // (.party__crown, inline style="display: block;" u lidera) wewnątrz WIDOCZNEGO okna party
  // (.party-window). Filtr widoczności (offsetParent) jest kluczowy — bez niego łapiemy też
  // osierocone/ukryte kopie okna z poprzednich grup, co dawało losowe/migające wyniki.
  function getVisiblePartyRows() {
    try {
      return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(".party-window .party-member[class*='other-party-id-']")).filter(
        (row) => row.offsetParent !== null,
      );
    } catch (_) {
      return [];
    }
  }

  function getLeaderIdFromCrownDom() {
    for (const row of getVisiblePartyRows()) {
      const crown = row.querySelector(".party__crown");
      if (crown && crown.style.display === "block") {
        const match = row.className.match(/other-party-id-(\d+)/);
        if (match) return match[1];
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  // Gdy okno party jest zwinięte/zamknięte, nie widać żadnych wierszy — wtedy trzymamy
  // ostatnio potwierdzonego lidera zamiast migać na "Brak lidera". Roster (nawet ukryty,
  // bez filtra widoczności) mówi nam czy w ogóle jesteśmy dalej w grupie.
  function getValidatedLeaderId() {
    const crownLeader = getLeaderIdFromCrownDom();
    if (crownLeader != null) {
      state.lastKnownLeaderId = crownLeader;
      return crownLeader;
    }
    const hasAnyRoster = document.querySelector(".party-window .party-member[class*='other-party-id-']") != null;
    if (!hasAnyRoster) {
      state.lastKnownLeaderId = null;
      return null;
    }
    return state.lastKnownLeaderId;
  }

  function getLeaderObj(leaderId) {
    const others = page.Engine?.others;
    if (!others || typeof others.getById !== "function") return null;
    try {
      return others.getById(leaderId);
    } catch (_) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  // Nick lidera z widgetu grupy w DOM — działa nawet gdy lider jest poza zasięgiem
  // renderowania mapy (Engine.others go wtedy nie widzi).
  function getLeaderNickFromDom(leaderId) {
    try {
      const row = document.querySelector(`.party-member.other-party-id-${leaderId}`);
      const nick = row?.querySelector(".nickname .nickname-text")?.textContent?.trim();
      return nick || null;
    } catch (_) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  function setStatus(text) {
    if (state.statusText === text) return;
    state.statusText = text;
    if (state.ui) state.ui.status.textContent = text;
  }

  function setLeaderLine(text) {
    if (state.leaderText === text) return;
    state.leaderText = text;
    if (state.ui) state.ui.leader.textContent = text;
  }

  function heartbeat() {
    if (!state.ui) return;
    state.blinkOn = !state.blinkOn;
    state.ui.dot.classList.toggle("ftl-blink", state.enabled && state.blinkOn);
  }

  function tick() {
    heartbeat();
    if (!state.enabled) return;

    const heroD = page.Engine?.hero?.d;

    if (heroD?.id == null) {
      setStatus("Czekam na grę...");
      return;
    }
    if (page.Engine?.dead || isInBattle()) {
      setStatus("Wstrzymano (walka/martwy)");
      return;
    }

    const leaderId = getValidatedLeaderId();
    if (leaderId == null) {
      setStatus("Brak grupy");
      setLeaderLine("Brak lidera");
      return;
    }
    if (String(leaderId) === String(heroD.id)) {
      setStatus("Jesteś liderem");
      setLeaderLine(`Lider: ${heroD.nick} (Ty)`);
      return;
    }

    const leaderNick = getLeaderNickFromDom(leaderId) || `#${leaderId}`;
    setLeaderLine(`Lider: ${leaderNick}`);

    const leaderObj = getLeaderObj(leaderId);
    if (!leaderObj?.d) {
      setStatus("Lider poza zasięgiem");
      return;
    }

    const leaderD = leaderObj.d;
    const dx = Math.abs(leaderD.x - heroD.x);
    const dy = Math.abs(leaderD.y - heroD.y);

    if (dx <= 1 && dy <= 1) {
      setStatus("Przy liderze");
      return;
    }

    // addAfterFollowAction liczy trasę JEDNORAZOWO do pozycji lidera w momencie wywołania —
    // nie doszlusowuje w locie. Żeby realnie "podążać" za ruszającym się liderem, trzeba to
    // wołać na każdym ticku (jak dobijara robi to na każdym heartbeacie "t=_"), nie tylko
    // gdy wykryjemy zmianę pola — inaczej hero robi jeden krok i czeka na kolejny ruch lidera.
    try {
      page.Engine.hero.addAfterFollowAction(leaderObj);
    } catch (_) {}
