    setStatus(`Podążam (${Math.max(dx, dy)}p)`);
  }

  function setEnabled(next) {
    state.enabled = next;
    localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, next ? "1" : "0");
    if (state.ui) {
      state.ui.button.classList.toggle("ftl-on", next);
      state.ui.button.textContent = next ? "FTL: ON" : "FTL: OFF";
      if (!next) state.ui.dot.classList.remove("ftl-blink");
    }
    setStatus(next ? "Szukam lidera..." : "Nieaktywny");
    if (!next) setLeaderLine("Brak lidera");
  }

  function clamp(val, min, max) {
    return Math.min(Math.max(val, min), max);
  }

  function savePos(left, top) {
    state.pos = { left, top };
    try {
      localStorage.setItem(POS_KEY, JSON.stringify(state.pos));
    } catch (_) {}
  }

  function makeDraggable(panel, handle) {
    let offsetX = 0;
    let offsetY = 0;

    function onMove(e) {
      const left = clamp(e.clientX - offsetX, 0, window.innerWidth - panel.offsetWidth);
      const top = clamp(e.clientY - offsetY, 0, window.innerHeight - panel.offsetHeight);
      panel.style.left = `${left}px`;
      panel.style.top = `${top}px`;
      panel.style.right = "auto";
      panel.style.bottom = "auto";
    }

    function onUp() {
      document.removeEventListener("mousemove", onMove);
      document.removeEventListener("mouseup", onUp);
      savePos(parseInt(panel.style.left, 10), parseInt(panel.style.top, 10));
    }

    handle.addEventListener("mousedown", (e) => {
      const rect = panel.getBoundingClientRect();
      offsetX = e.clientX - rect.left;
      offsetY = e.clientY - rect.top;
      document.addEventListener("mousemove", onMove);
      document.addEventListener("mouseup", onUp);
      e.preventDefault();
    });
  }

  function setMinimized(next) {
    state.minimized = next;
    localStorage.setItem(MINIMIZED_KEY, next ? "1" : "0");
    if (state.ui) {
      state.ui.panel.classList.toggle("ftl-minimized", next);
      state.ui.minBtn.textContent = next ? "▢" : "▁";
      state.ui.minBtn.title = next ? "Rozwiń" : "Zwiń";
    }
  }

  function injectUi() {
    const style = document.createElement("style");
    style.textContent = `
      #ftl-panel {
        position: fixed;
        right: 12px;
        bottom: 90px;
        z-index: 99999;
        width: 168px;
        font-family: Arial, sans-serif;
        user-select: none;
      }
      #ftl-panel .ftl-header {
        display: flex;
        align-items: center;
        justify-content: space-between;
        gap: 6px;
        background: #222;
        border: 1px solid #333;
        border-radius: 4px 4px 0 0;
        padding: 4px 6px;
        cursor: move; 
      }
      #ftl-panel.ftl-minimized .ftl-header {
        border-radius: 4px;
      }
      #ftl-panel .ftl-title {
        display: flex;
        align-items: center;
        gap: 6px;
        font-size: 11px;
        font-weight: bold;
        color: #ccc;
      }
      #ftl-panel .ftl-min-btn {
        cursor: pointer;
        border: none;
        background: transparent;
        color: #ccc;
        font-size: 11px;
        line-height: 1;
        padding: 2px 4px;
      }
      #ftl-panel .ftl-min-btn:hover {
        color: #fff;
      }
      #ftl-panel .ftl-body {
        display: flex;
        flex-direction: column;
        align-items: stretch;
        gap: 4px;
        padding-top: 4px;
      }
      #ftl-panel.ftl-minimized .ftl-body {
        display: none;
      }
      #ftl-panel button.ftl-toggle {
        cursor: pointer;
        border: 1px solid #333;
        border-radius: 4px;
        background: #444;
        color: #eee;
        font-size: 11px;
        font-weight: bold;
        padding: 6px 10px;
        width: 100%;
      }
      #ftl-panel button.ftl-toggle.ftl-on {
        background: #2e7d32;
        border-color: #1b5e20;
      }
      #ftl-panel .ftl-dot {
        width: 8px;
        height: 8px;
        border-radius: 50%;
        background: #777;
        transition: background 0.15s, box-shadow 0.15s;
        flex-shrink: 0;
      }
      #ftl-panel .ftl-dot.ftl-blink {
        background: #7cfc00;
        box-shadow: 0 0 5px #7cfc00;
      }
      #ftl-panel .ftl-leader {
        font-size: 10px;
        color: #ffd54f;
        background: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.6);
        border-radius: 3px;
        padding: 3px 6px;
        text-align: center;
        font-weight: bold;
      }
      #ftl-panel .ftl-status {
        font-size: 10px;
        color: #ddd;
        background: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.6);
        border-radius: 3px;
        padding: 3px 6px;
        text-align: center;
      }
    `;
    document.head.appendChild(style);

    const panel = document.createElement("div");
    panel.id = "ftl-panel";
    if (state.pos) {
      panel.style.left = `${state.pos.left}px`;
      panel.style.top = `${state.pos.top}px`;
      panel.style.right = "auto";
      panel.style.bottom = "auto";
    }

    const header = document.createElement("div");
    header.className = "ftl-header";

    const title = document.createElement("div");
    title.className = "ftl-title";

    const dot = document.createElement("span");
    dot.className = "ftl-dot";

    const titleText = document.createElement("span");
    titleText.textContent = "FTL";

    title.appendChild(dot);
    title.appendChild(titleText);

    const minBtn = document.createElement("button");
    minBtn.type = "button";
    minBtn.className = "ftl-min-btn";
    minBtn.textContent = state.minimized ? "▢" : "▁";
    minBtn.title = state.minimized ? "Rozwiń" : "Zwiń";
    minBtn.addEventListener("click", () => setMinimized(!state.minimized));

    header.appendChild(title);
    header.appendChild(minBtn);

    const body = document.createElement("div");
    body.className = "ftl-body";

    const button = document.createElement("button");
    button.type = "button";
    button.className = "ftl-toggle";
    button.classList.toggle("ftl-on", state.enabled);
    button.textContent = state.enabled ? "FTL: ON" : "FTL: OFF";
    button.addEventListener("click", () => setEnabled(!state.enabled));

    const leader = document.createElement("div");
    leader.className = "ftl-leader";
    leader.textContent = state.leaderText;

    const status = document.createElement("div");
    status.className = "ftl-status";
    status.textContent = state.statusText;

    body.appendChild(button);
    body.appendChild(leader);
    body.appendChild(status);

    panel.appendChild(header);
    panel.appendChild(body);
    panel.classList.toggle("ftl-minimized", state.minimized);
    document.body.appendChild(panel);

    makeDraggable(panel, header);

    state.ui = { panel, header, button, dot, minBtn, leader, status };
  }

  function init() {
    injectUi();
    setInterval(tick, POLL_MS);
  }

  if (document.body) {
    init();
  } else {
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", init, { once: true });
  }
})();


// ==UserScript==
// @name         Margonem Advanced Bot (Gargonem Integration)
// @namespace    http://tampermonkey.net/
// @version      1.0
// @description  Zaawansowany bot do Margonem.pl zintegrowany z Gargonem (Priw8)
// @author       TwójNick
// @match        https://*.margonem.pl/
// @exclude      https://www.margonem.pl/
// @match        https://*.margonem.com/
// @exclude      https://www.margonem.com/
// @icon         https://www.google.com/s2/favicons?sz=64&domain=margonem.pl
// @grant        GM_setValue
// @grant        GM_getValue
// @grant        GM_deleteValue
// @grant        GM_listValues
// @grant        unsafeWindow
// @require      https://priw8.com/margo/gargonem/dist/main.js
// ==/UserScript==

(function() {
    'use strict';

    // ====== KONFIGURACJA ======
    const config = {
        debugMode: true,          // Tryb debugowania
        decisionInterval: 1500,   // Co ile ms podejmować decyzje
        safeMode: true,           // Tryb bezpieczny - nie atakuje graczy
        minHpToFight: 0.5,        // Minimalny % HP, aby atakować
        minMpToUseSkill: 0.3,     // Minimalny % MP, aby używać umiejętności
        maxMonsterDistance: 3,    // Maksymalna odległość ataku
        maxItemDistance: 2,       // Maksymalna odległość podnoszenia przedmiotów
        fleeThreshold: 0.2,       // Uciekaj, jeśli HP < 20%
        avoidNpcs: ['Strażnik', 'Mistrz Gildii'], // NPC do unikania
        questRefreshInterval: 30000, // Co ile ms odświeżać questy
        pathfinding: {
            maxSteps: 20,         // Maksymalna liczba kroków w szukaniu ścieżki
            avoidObstacles: true  // Unikaj przeszkód
        }
    };

    // ====== STAN GRY ======
    const gameState = {
        player: {
            hp: 0,
            maxHp: 0,
            mp: 0,
            maxMp: 0,
            level: 0,
            position: { x: 0, y: 0 },
            target: null,
            skills: [],
            buffs: []
        },
        map: {
            name: '',
            size: { width: 100, height: 100 },
            monsters: [],
            players: [],
            npcs: [],
            items: [],
            obstacles: []
        },
        quests: {
            active: [],
            completed: [],
            available: []
        },
        killedMonsters: GM_getValue('killedMonsters', {}),
        lastAction: null,
        lastActionTime: 0,
        isFighting: false,
        isMoving: false,
        mode: 'exp' // exp, quest, heros, e2
    };

    // ====== INICJALIZACJA ======
    function init() {
        log('[Gargonem Bot] Inicjalizacja bota...');

        // Czekaj, aż Gargonem się załaduje
        const checkGargonemLoaded = setInterval(() => {
            if (typeof unsafeWindow.g !== 'undefined' && unsafeWindow.g.game) {
                clearInterval(checkGargonemLoaded);
                log('[Gargonem Bot] Gargonem załadowany, inicjalizacja bota...');
                addUI();
                loadSavedState();
                startGameMonitoring();
                startDecisionLoop();
                startQuestMonitoring();
                log('[Gargonem Bot] Bot zainicjalizowany. Tryb: ' + gameState.mode);
            }
        }, 1000);
    }

    // ====== FUNKCJE POMOCNICZE ======
    function log(message) {
        if (!config.debugMode) return;

        const logElement = document.getElementById('gargonem-bot-log');
        if (logElement) {
            const time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
            const logEntry = document.createElement('div');
            logEntry.textContent = `[${time}] ${message}`;
            logElement.appendChild(logEntry);
            logElement.scrollTop = logElement.scrollHeight;
        }

        console.log(`[Gargonem Bot] ${message}`);
    }

    function calculateDistance(pos1, pos2) {
        return Math.sqrt(Math.pow(pos1.x - pos2.x, 2) + Math.pow(pos1.y - pos2.y, 2));
    }

    function isPositionWalkable(position) {
        if (!unsafeWindow.g.game.map.collision) return true;

        const collision = unsafeWindow.g.game.map.collision;
        const x = Math.floor(position.x);
        const y = Math.floor(position.y);

        if (x < 0 || x >= collision[0].length || y < 0 || y >= collision.length) {
            return false;
        }

        return !collision[y][x];
    }

    // ====== ZAPISYWANIE STANU ======
    function saveState() {
        GM_setValue('killedMonsters', gameState.killedMonsters);
    }

    function loadSavedState() {
        gameState.killedMonsters = GM_getValue('killedMonsters', {});
    }

    // ====== INTERFEJS UŻYTKOWNIKA ======
    function addUI() {
        const ui = document.createElement('div');
        ui.id = 'gargonem-bot-ui';
        ui.style.position = 'fixed';
        ui.style.bottom = '10px';
        ui.style.right = '10px';
        ui.style.zIndex = '99999';
        ui.style.backgroundColor = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.8)';
        ui.style.color = 'white';
        ui.style.padding = '10px';
        ui.style.borderRadius = '5px';
        ui.style.fontFamily = 'Arial, sans-serif';
        ui.style.fontSize = '12px';
        ui.style.width = '300px';

        ui.innerHTML = `
            <h3 style="margin: 0 0 10px 0;">Margonem Advanced Bot</h3>
            <div id="gargonem-bot-status">Status: Inicjalizacja...</div>
            <div style="margin: 10px 0;">
                <strong>Tryb:</strong>
                <select id="gargonem-bot-mode" style="margin-left: 5px;">
                    <option value="exp">Expienie</option>
                    <option value="quest">Robienie questów</option>
                    <option value="heros">Szukanie herosów</option>
                    <option value="e2">Stanie na E2</option>
                </select>
            </div>
            <div id="gargonem-bot-actions" style="margin: 10px 0;">
                <button id="gargonem-toggle-bot" style="margin-right: 5px;">Włącz/Wyłącz</button>
                <button id="gargonem-debug-info" style="margin-right: 5px;">Debug</button>
                <button id="gargonem-clear-killed">Wyczyść zabite</button>
            </div>
            <div style="margin: 10px 0;">
                <strong>Opcje:</strong><br>
                <label><input type="checkbox" id="gargonem-auto-use-skills" checked> Automatyczne używanie umiejętności</label><br>
                <label><input type="checkbox" id="gargonem-auto-pick-items" checked> Automatyczne podnoszenie przedmiotów</label><br>
                <label><input type="checkbox" id="gargonem-avoid-npcs" checked> Unikaj określonych NPC</label>
            </div>
            <div id="gargonem-bot-log" style="margin-top: 10px; max-height: 200px; overflow-y: auto; border: 1px solid #333; padding: 5px; background: rgba(0,0,0,0.5);"></div>
        `;

        document.body.appendChild(ui);

        document.getElementById('gargonem-toggle-bot').addEventListener('click', toggleBot);
        document.getElementById('gargonem-debug-info').addEventListener('click', showDebugInfo);
        document.getElementById('gargonem-clear-killed').addEventListener('click', clearKilledMonsters);
        document.getElementById('gargonem-bot-mode').addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            gameState.mode = e.target.value;
            log(`Zmieniono tryb na: ${gameState.mode}`);
        });
    }

    function toggleBot() {
        const statusElement = document.getElementById('gargonem-bot-status');
        if (statusElement.textContent.includes('Aktywny')) {
            statusElement.textContent = 'Status: Wyłączony';
            statusElement.style.color = 'red';
            log('Bot wyłączony');
        } else {
            statusElement.textContent = 'Status: Aktywny';
            statusElement.style.color = 'lime';
            log('Bot włączony');
        }
    }

    function showDebugInfo() {
        log('=== DEBUG INFO ===');
        log(`Tryb: ${gameState.mode}`);
        log(`Pozycja: ${gameState.player.position.x}, ${gameState.player.position.y}`);
        log(`HP: ${gameState.player.hp}/${gameState.player.maxHp} (${Math.round((gameState.player.hp / gameState.player.maxHp) * 100)}%)`);
        log(`MP: ${gameState.player.mp}/${gameState.player.maxMp} (${Math.round((gameState.player.mp / gameState.player.maxMp) * 100)}%)`);
        log(`Poziom: ${gameState.player.level}`);
        log(`Mapa: ${gameState.map.name}`);
        log(`Potwory w pobliżu: ${gameState.map.monsters.length}`);
        log(`Gracze w pobliżu: ${gameState.map.players.length}`);
        log(`Przedmioty na ziemi: ${gameState.map.items.length}`);
        log(`Aktywne questy: ${gameState.quests.active.length}`);
        log(`Zabite potwory: ${Object.keys(gameState.killedMonsters).length}`);
        log('==================');
    }

    function clearKilledMonsters() {
        gameState.killedMonsters = {};
        saveState();
        log('Wyczyszczono listę zabitych potworów');
    }

    // ====== MONITOROWANIE GRY ======
    function startGameMonitoring() {
        setInterval(updateGameState, 1000);
    }

    function updateGameState() {
        if (!unsafeWindow.g || !unsafeWindow.g.game) return;

        try {
            updatePlayerInfo();
            updateMapInfo();
            updateUIStatus();
        } catch (e) {
            log(`Błąd aktualizacji stanu gry: ${e.message}`);
        }
    }

    function updatePlayerInfo() {
        const player = unsafeWindow.g.game.player;

        if (!player) return;

        gameState.player.hp = player.hp;
        gameState.player.maxHp = player.max_hp;
        gameState.player.mp = player.mp;
        gameState.player.maxMp = player.max_mp;
        gameState.player.level = player.level;
        gameState.player.position = { x: player.x, y: player.y };
        gameState.player.target = player.target ? player.target.nick : null;

        gameState.player.skills = [];
        if (player.skills) {
            for (const skillId in player.skills) {
                const skill = player.skills[skillId];
                gameState.player.skills.push({
                    name: skill.name,
                    cooldown: skill.cooldown > 0,
                    lastUsed: 0
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.player.buffs = [];
        if (player.buffs) {
            for (const buffId in player.buffs) {
                const buff = player.buffs[buffId];
                gameState.player.buffs.push(buff.name);
            }
        }

        gameState.isFighting = player.inFight;
    }

    function updateMapInfo() {
        const game = unsafeWindow.g.game;

        if (!game || !game.map) return;

        gameState.map.name = game.map.name || 'Nieznana';
        gameState.map.size = {
            width: game.map.width || 100,
            height: game.map.height || 100
        };

        gameState.map.monsters = [];
        if (game.map.monsters) {
            for (const monsterId in game.map.monsters) {
                const monster = game.map.monsters[monsterId];
                gameState.map.monsters.push({
                    id: monsterId,
                    name: monster.name,
                    position: { x: monster.x, y: monster.y },
                    hp: monster.hp,
                    maxHp: monster.max_hp,
                    level: monster.level,
                    distance: calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, { x: monster.x, y: monster.y }),
                    isBoss: monster.boss
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.map.monsters.sort((a, b) => {
            if (a.isBoss && !b.isBoss) return -1;
            if (!a.isBoss && b.isBoss) return 1;

            const aHpPercent = a.hp / a.maxHp;
            const bHpPercent = b.hp / b.maxHp;
            if (aHpPercent < 0.3 && bHpPercent >= 0.3) return -1;
            if (bHpPercent < 0.3 && aHpPercent >= 0.3) return 1;

            return b.level - a.level;
        });

        gameState.map.players = [];
        if (game.map.players) {
            for (const playerId in game.map.players) {
                const player = game.map.players[playerId];
                if (player.nick === game.player.nick) continue;

                gameState.map.players.push({
                    name: player.nick,
                    position: { x: player.x, y: player.y },
                    distance: calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, { x: player.x, y: player.y }),
                    isHeros: player.nick.includes('[Heros]') || player.nick.includes('Heros')
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.map.npcs = [];
        if (game.map.npcs) {
            for (const npcId in game.map.npcs) {
                const npc = game.map.npcs[npcId];
                gameState.map.npcs.push({
                    id: npcId,
                    name: npc.name,
                    position: { x: npc.x, y: npc.y },
                    distance: calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, { x: npc.x, y: npc.y }),
                    isQuestNpc: npc.quest
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.map.items = [];
        if (game.map.items) {
            for (const itemId in game.map.items) {
                const item = game.map.items[itemId];
                gameState.map.items.push({
                    id: itemId,
                    name: item.name,
                    position: { x: item.x, y: item.y },
                    distance: calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, { x: item.x, y: item.y }),
                    isGold: item.name.includes('Złoto'),
                    isQuestItem: item.quest
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.map.obstacles = [];
        if (game.map.collision) {
            const collision = game.map.collision;
            for (let y = 0; y < collision.length; y++) {
                for (let x = 0; x < collision[y].length; x++) {
                    if (collision[y][x]) {
                        gameState.map.obstacles.push({ x, y });
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function updateUIStatus() {
        const statusElement = document.getElementById('gargonem-bot-status');
        if (statusElement) {
            const modeText = {
                'exp': 'Expienie',
                'quest': 'Robienie questów',
                'heros': 'Szukanie herosów',
                'e2': 'Stanie na E2'
            }[gameState.mode] || gameState.mode;

            statusElement.textContent = `Status: ${gameState.isFighting ? 'Walka' : 'Spokój'} | Tryb: ${modeText} | Poziom: ${gameState.player.level}`;
        }
    }

    // ====== MONITOROWANIE QUESTÓW ======
    function startQuestMonitoring() {
        setInterval(updateQuests, config.questRefreshInterval);
    }

    function updateQuests() {
        if (!unsafeWindow.g || !unsafeWindow.g.game || !unsafeWindow.g.game.quests) return;

        try {
            const quests = unsafeWindow.g.game.quests;

            gameState.quests.active = [];
            if (quests.active) {
                for (const questId in quests.active) {
                    const quest = quests.active[questId];
                    gameState.quests.active.push({
                        id: questId,
                        name: quest.name,
                        progress: quest.progress,
                        isCompleted: quest.progress.current >= quest.progress.total
                    });
                }
            }

            gameState.quests.available = [];
            if (quests.available) {
                for (const questId in quests.available) {
                    const quest = quests.available[questId];
                    gameState.quests.available.push({
                        id: questId,
                        name: quest.name,
                        giver: quest.giver
                    });
                }
            }

            gameState.quests.completed = [];
            if (quests.completed) {
                for (const questId in quests.completed) {
                    const quest = quests.completed[questId];
                    gameState.quests.completed.push({
                        id: questId,
                        name: quest.name,
                        receiver: quest.receiver
                    });
                }
            }

            log(`Zaktualizowano questy. Aktywne: ${gameState.quests.active.length}, Dostępne: ${gameState.quests.available.length}, Ukończone: ${gameState.quests.completed.length}`);
        } catch (e) {
            log(`Błąd aktualizacji questów: ${e.message}`);
        }
    }

    // ====== CYKL DECYZYJNY ======
    function startDecisionLoop() {
        setInterval(makeDecision, config.decisionInterval);
    }

    function makeDecision() {
        if (!unsafeWindow.g || !unsafeWindow.g.game || !document.getElementById('gargonem-bot-status').textContent.includes('Aktywny')) {
            return;
        }

        try {
            if (gameState.isFighting) {
                handleCombat();
                return;
            }

            switch (gameState.mode) {
                case 'exp':
                    handleExpMode();
                    break;
                case 'quest':
                    handleQuestMode();
                    break;
                case 'heros':
                    handleHerosMode();
                    break;
                case 'e2':
                    handleE2Mode();
                    break;
                default:
                    handleExpMode();
            }
        } catch (e) {
            log(`Błąd podejmowania decyzji: ${e.message}`);
        }
    }

    // ====== TRYBY DZIAŁANIA ======
    function handleExpMode() {
        const decisions = [
            checkFleeCondition(),
            checkLowHp(),
            checkLowMp(),
            checkAttackableMonster(),
            checkPickableItem(),
            checkRandomMovement()
        ];

        const bestDecision = getBestDecision(decisions);
        executeDecision(bestDecision);
    }

    function handleQuestMode() {
        if (gameState.quests.completed.length > 0) {
            const quest = gameState.quests.completed[0];
            const npc = gameState.map.npcs.find(n => n.name === quest.receiver);

            if (npc) {
                if (npc.distance <= 1) {
                    return executeDecision({
                        action: 'turn_in_quest',
                        target: quest.id,
                        reason: `Oddaję quest: ${quest.name}`,
                        priority: 10
                    });
                } else {
                    return executeDecision({
                        action: 'move_to',
                        target: npc.position,
                        reason: `Idę oddać quest: ${quest.name}`,
                        priority: 10
                    });
                }
            }
        }

        if (gameState.quests.available.length > 0) {
            const quest = gameState.quests.available[0];
            const npc = gameState.map.npcs.find(n => n.name === quest.giver);

            if (npc) {
                if (npc.distance <= 1) {
                    return executeDecision({
                        action: 'accept_quest',
                        target: quest.id,
                        reason: `Przyjmuję quest: ${quest.name}`,
                        priority: 9
                    });
                } else {
                    return executeDecision({
                        action: 'move_to',
                        target: npc.position,
                        reason: `Idę przyjąć quest: ${quest.name}`,
                        priority: 9
                    });
                }
            }
        }

        handleExpMode();
    }

    function handleHerosMode() {
        const herosPlayers = gameState.map.players.filter(p => p.isHeros);

        if (herosPlayers.length > 0) {
            const closestHeros = herosPlayers[0];

            if (closestHeros.distance <= 1) {
                return executeDecision({
                    action: 'follow_player',
                    target: closestHeros.name,
                    reason: `Podążam za herosem: ${closestHeros.name}`,
                    priority: 8
                });
            } else {
                return executeDecision({
                    action: 'move_to',
                    target: closestHeros.position,
                    reason: `Idę do herosa: ${closestHeros.name}`,
                    priority: 8
                });
            }
        }

        handleExpMode();
    }

    function handleE2Mode() {
        const e2Position = { x: 50, y: 50 };

        if (calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, e2Position) <= 1) {
            return executeDecision({
                action: 'wait',
                reason: 'Stoję na E2',
                priority: 1
            });
        } else {
            return executeDecision({
                action: 'move_to',
                target: e2Position,
                reason: 'Idę na E2',
                priority: 10
            });
        }
    }

    // ====== DECYZJE ======
    function checkFleeCondition() {
        const hpPercentage = gameState.player.hp / gameState.player.maxHp;
        if (hpPercentage < config.fleeThreshold) {
            return { action: 'flee', reason: 'Niskie HP - ucieczka', priority: 10 };
        }
        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkLowHp() {
        const hpPercentage = gameState.player.hp / gameState.player.maxHp;
        if (hpPercentage < config.minHpToFight) {
            return { action: 'use_potion', target: 'hp', reason: 'Niskie HP', priority: 9 };
        }
        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkLowMp() {
        const mpPercentage = gameState.player.mp / gameState.player.maxMp;
        if (mpPercentage < config.minMpToUseSkill) {
            return { action: 'use_potion', target: 'mp', reason: 'Niskie MP', priority: 8 };
        }
        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkAttackableMonster() {
        if (gameState.map.monsters.length === 0) {
            return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
        }

        const closestMonster = gameState.map.monsters[0];

        if (gameState.killedMonsters[closestMonster.name] &&
            gameState.killedMonsters[closestMonster.name] >= 5) {
            log(`Potwór ${closestMonster.name} został już zabity wystarczająco razy, pomijam`);
            return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
        }

        if (closestMonster.distance <= config.maxMonsterDistance) {
            return {
                action: 'attack',
                target: closestMonster.id,
                reason: `Potwór ${closestMonster.name} (Lvl ${closestMonster.level}) w zasięgu`,
                priority: 7
            };
        }

        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkPickableItem() {
        if (!document.getElementById('gargonem-auto-pick-items')?.checked) {
            return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
        }

        if (gameState.map.items.length === 0) {
            return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
        }

        const closestItem = gameState.map.items[0];
        if (closestItem.distance <= config.maxItemDistance) {
            return {
                action: 'pick_up',
                target: closestItem.id,
                reason: `Przedmiot ${closestItem.name} w zasięgu`,
                priority: 6
            };
        }

        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkRandomMovement() {
        return { action: 'move_random', reason: 'Brak innych akcji', priority: 1 };
    }

    function getBestDecision(decisions) {
        return decisions.reduce((best, current) =>
            (current.priority > best.priority) ? current : best,
            { action: 'wait', priority: 0 }
        );
    }

    // ====== WYKONYWANIE DECYZJI ======
    function executeDecision(decision) {
        if (!decision || !decision.action || decision.priority === 0) {
            return;
        }

        gameState.lastAction = `${decision.action} ${decision.target ? `(${decision.target})` : ''}`;
        gameState.lastActionTime = Date.now();

        log(`Wykonuję: ${decision.action} (${decision.reason})`);

        switch (decision.action) {
            case 'attack':
                attackMonster(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'move_to':
                moveToPosition(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'pick_up':
                pickUpItem(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'use_potion':
                usePotion(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'use_skill':
                useSkill(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'flee':
                fleeFromCombat();
                break;
            case 'talk_to_npc':
                talkToNPC(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'accept_quest':
                acceptQuest(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'turn_in_quest':
                turnInQuest(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'follow_player':
                followPlayer(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'move_random':
                moveRandomly();
                break;
            case 'wait':
            default:
                log('Czekam...');
                break;
        }
    }

    // ====== AKCJE ======
    function attackMonster(monsterId) {
        const monster = gameState.map.monsters.find(m => m.id === monsterId);
        if (!monster) {
            log(`Nie znaleziono potwora o ID: ${monsterId}`);
            return;
        }

        if (monster.distance > 1) {
            log(`Potwór ${monster.name} jest za daleko (${monster.distance.toFixed(1)})`);
            moveToPosition(monster.position);
            return;
        }

        log(`Atakuję ${monster.name} (Lvl ${monster.level}, HP: ${monster.hp}/${monster.maxHp})`);

        if (!gameState.killedMonsters[monster.name]) {
            gameState.killedMonsters[monster.name] = 0;
        }
        gameState.killedMonsters[monster.name]++;
        saveState();

        unsafeWindow.g.game.attack(monsterId);

        if (document.getElementById('gargonem-auto-use-skills')?.checked) {
            useCombatSkills();
        }
    }

    function moveToPosition(position) {
        if (gameState.isMoving) return;

        const distance = calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, position);
        if (distance <= 1) {
            log(`Już jesteśmy przy celu (${position.x}, ${position.y})`);
            return;
        }

        log(`Poruszam się do (${position.x}, ${position.y})`);

        const path = findPath(gameState.player.position, position);
        if (path.length > 0) {
            const nextStep = path[0];
            unsafeWindow.g.game.move(nextStep.x, nextStep.y);
            gameState.isMoving = true;

            setTimeout(() => {
                gameState.isMoving = false;
            }, 1000);
        } else {
            log('Nie znaleziono ścieżki!');
            unsafeWindow.g.game.move(position.x, position.y);
        }
    }

    function findPath(start, end) {
        const openSet = [start];
        const cameFrom = {};
        const gScore = {};
        const fScore = {};

        gScore[start.x + ',' + start.y] = 0;
        fScore[start.x + ',' + start.y] = calculateDistance(start, end);

        while (openSet.length > 0) {
            let current = openSet[0];
            for (const node of openSet) {
                if (fScore[node.x + ',' + node.y] < fScore[current.x + ',' + current.y]) {
                    current = node;
                }
            }

            if (current.x === end.x && current.y === end.y) {
                const path = [];
                let temp = current;
                while (temp.x !== start.x || temp.y !== start.y) {
                    path.push(temp);
                    temp = cameFrom[temp.x + ',' + temp.y];
                }
                return path.reverse();
            }

            openSet.splice(openSet.indexOf(current), 1);

            const neighbors = [
                { x: current.x + 1, y: current.y },
                { x: current.x - 1, y: current.y },
                { x: current.x, y: current.y + 1 },
                { x: current.x, y: current.y - 1 }
            ];

            for (const neighbor of neighbors) {
                if (neighbor.x < 0 || neighbor.x >= gameState.map.size.width ||
                    neighbor.y < 0 || neighbor.y >= gameState.map.size.height) {
                    continue;
                }

                if (config.pathfinding.avoidObstacles && !isPositionWalkable(neighbor)) {
                    continue;
                }

                const tentativeGScore = gScore[current.x + ',' + current.y] + 1;

                if (!gScore[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y] ||
                    tentativeGScore < gScore[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y]) {
                    cameFrom[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y] = current;
                    gScore[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y] = tentativeGScore;
                    fScore[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y] = tentativeGScore + calculateDistance(neighbor, end);

                    if (!openSet.some(node => node.x === neighbor.x && node.y === neighbor.y)) {
                        openSet.push(neighbor);
                    }
                }
            }

            if (Object.keys(cameFrom).length > config.pathfinding.maxSteps) {
                log('Przekroczono maksymalną liczbę kroków w szukaniu ścieżki');
                return [];
            }
        }

        log('Nie znaleziono ścieżki!');
        return [];
    }

    function pickUpItem(itemId) {
        const item = gameState.map.items.find(i => i.id === itemId);
        if (!item) {
            log(`Nie znaleziono przedmiotu o ID: ${itemId}`);
            return;
        }

        if (item.distance > 1) {
            log(`Przedmiot ${item.name} jest za daleko (${item.distance.toFixed(1)})`);
            moveToPosition(item.position);
            return;
        }

        log(`Podnoszę ${item.name}`);
        unsafeWindow.g.game.pickUpItem(itemId);
    }

    function usePotion(type) {
        log(`Używam mikstury: ${type}`);
        unsafeWindow.g.game.usePotion(type);
    }

    function useSkill(skillName) {
        if (!document.getElementById('gargonem-auto-use-skills')?.checked) {
            return;
        }

        const skill = gameState.player.skills.find(s => s.name === skillName);
        if (!skill) {
            log(`Nie znaleziono umiejętności: ${skillName}`);
            return;
        }

        log(`Używam umiejętności: ${skillName}`);
        unsafeWindow.g.game.useSkill(skillName);
    }

    function useCombatSkills() {
        if (gameState.player.hp / gameState.player.maxHp < 0.5) {
            const healSkill = gameState.player.skills.find(s =>
                s.name.includes('Leczenie') || s.name.includes('Heal')
            );
            if (healSkill) {
                useSkill(healSkill.name);
                return;
            }
        }

        const offensiveSkills = gameState.player.skills.filter(s =>
            !s.cooldown &&
            (s.name.includes('Atak') || s.name.includes('Fireball') || s.name.includes('Błyskawica'))
        );

        if (offensiveSkills.length > 0) {
            useSkill(offensiveSkills[0].name);
        }
    }

    function fleeFromCombat() {
        log('Uciekam z walki!');
        unsafeWindow.g.game.flee();
    }

    function talkToNPC(npcId) {
        log(`Rozmawiam z NPC o ID: ${npcId}`);
        unsafeWindow.g.game.talkToNPC(npcId);
    }

    function acceptQuest(questId) {
        log(`Przyjmuję quest o ID: ${questId}`);
        unsafeWindow.g.game.acceptQuest(questId);
    }

    function turnInQuest(questId) {
        log(`Oddaję quest o ID: ${questId}`);
        unsafeWindow.g.game.turnInQuest(questId);
    }

    function followPlayer(playerName) {
        const player = gameState.map.players.find(p => p.name === playerName);
        if (!player) {
            log(`Nie znaleziono gracza: ${playerName}`);
            return;
        }

        if (player.distance <= 1) {
            log(`Podążam za graczem: ${playerName}`);
        } else {
            moveToPosition(player.position);
        }
    }

    function moveRandomly() {
        if (gameState.isMoving) return;

        const directions = [
            { x: 0, y: -1 },
            { x: 1, y: 0 },
            { x: 0, y: 1 },
            { x: -1, y: 0 }
        ];

        const randomDir = directions[Math.floor(Math.random() * directions.length)];
        const newPos = {
            x: gameState.player.position.x + randomDir.x,
            y: gameState.player.position.y + randomDir.y
        };

        if (newPos.x >= 0 && newPos.x < gameState.map.size.width &&
            newPos.y >= 0 && newPos.y < gameState.map.size.height &&
            isPositionWalkable(newPos)) {
            unsafeWindow.g.game.move(newPos.x, newPos.y);
        }
    }

    // ====== INICJALIZACJA ======
    init();
})();

// ==UserScript==
// @name         Margonem Advanced Bot (Gargonem Integration)
// @namespace    http://tampermonkey.net/
// @version      1.0
// @description  Zaawansowany bot do Margonem.pl zintegrowany z Gargonem (Priw8)
// @author       TwójNick
// @match        https://*.margonem.pl/
// @exclude      https://www.margonem.pl/
// @match        https://*.margonem.com/
// @exclude      https://www.margonem.com/
// @icon         https://www.google.com/s2/favicons?sz=64&domain=margonem.pl
// @grant        GM_setValue
// @grant        GM_getValue
// @grant        GM_deleteValue
// @grant        GM_listValues
// @grant        unsafeWindow
// @require      https://priw8.com/margo/gargonem/dist/main.js
// ==/UserScript==

(function() {
    'use strict';

    // ====== KONFIGURACJA ======
    const config = {
        debugMode: true,          // Tryb debugowania
        decisionInterval: 1500,   // Co ile ms podejmować decyzje
        safeMode: true,           // Tryb bezpieczny - nie atakuje graczy
        minHpToFight: 0.5,        // Minimalny % HP, aby atakować
        minMpToUseSkill: 0.3,     // Minimalny % MP, aby używać umiejętności
        maxMonsterDistance: 3,    // Maksymalna odległość ataku
        maxItemDistance: 2,       // Maksymalna odległość podnoszenia przedmiotów
        fleeThreshold: 0.2,       // Uciekaj, jeśli HP < 20%
        avoidNpcs: ['Strażnik', 'Mistrz Gildii'], // NPC do unikania
        questRefreshInterval: 30000, // Co ile ms odświeżać questy
        pathfinding: {
            maxSteps: 20,         // Maksymalna liczba kroków w szukaniu ścieżki
            avoidObstacles: true  // Unikaj przeszkód
        }
    };

    // ====== STAN GRY ======
    const gameState = {
        player: {
            hp: 0,
            maxHp: 0,
            mp: 0,
            maxMp: 0,
            level: 0,
            position: { x: 0, y: 0 },
            target: null,
            skills: [],
            buffs: []
        },
        map: {
            name: '',
            size: { width: 100, height: 100 },
            monsters: [],
            players: [],
            npcs: [],
            items: [],
            obstacles: []
        },
        quests: {
            active: [],
            completed: [],
            available: []
        },
        killedMonsters: GM_getValue('killedMonsters', {}),
        lastAction: null,
        lastActionTime: 0,
        isFighting: false,
        isMoving: false,
        mode: 'exp' // exp, quest, heros, e2
    };

    // ====== INICJALIZACJA ======
    function init() {
        log('[Gargonem Bot] Inicjalizacja bota...');

        // Czekaj, aż Gargonem się załaduje
        const checkGargonemLoaded = setInterval(() => {
            if (typeof unsafeWindow.g !== 'undefined' && unsafeWindow.g.game) {
                clearInterval(checkGargonemLoaded);
                log('[Gargonem Bot] Gargonem załadowany, inicjalizacja bota...');
                addUI();
                loadSavedState();
                startGameMonitoring();
                startDecisionLoop();
                startQuestMonitoring();
                log('[Gargonem Bot] Bot zainicjalizowany. Tryb: ' + gameState.mode);
            }
        }, 1000);
    }

    // ====== FUNKCJE POMOCNICZE ======
    function log(message) {
        if (!config.debugMode) return;

        const logElement = document.getElementById('gargonem-bot-log');
        if (logElement) {
            const time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
            const logEntry = document.createElement('div');
            logEntry.textContent = `[${time}] ${message}`;
            logElement.appendChild(logEntry);
            logElement.scrollTop = logElement.scrollHeight;
        }

        console.log(`[Gargonem Bot] ${message}`);
    }

    function calculateDistance(pos1, pos2) {
        return Math.sqrt(Math.pow(pos1.x - pos2.x, 2) + Math.pow(pos1.y - pos2.y, 2));
    }

    function isPositionWalkable(position) {
        if (!unsafeWindow.g.game.map.collision) return true;

        const collision = unsafeWindow.g.game.map.collision;
        const x = Math.floor(position.x);
        const y = Math.floor(position.y);

        if (x < 0 || x >= collision[0].length || y < 0 || y >= collision.length) {
            return false;
        }

        return !collision[y][x];
    }

    // ====== ZAPISYWANIE STANU ======
    function saveState() {
        GM_setValue('killedMonsters', gameState.killedMonsters);
    }

    function loadSavedState() {
        gameState.killedMonsters = GM_getValue('killedMonsters', {});
    }

    // ====== INTERFEJS UŻYTKOWNIKA ======
    function addUI() {
        const ui = document.createElement('div');
        ui.id = 'gargonem-bot-ui';
        ui.style.position = 'fixed';
        ui.style.bottom = '10px';
        ui.style.right = '10px';
        ui.style.zIndex = '99999';
        ui.style.backgroundColor = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.8)';
        ui.style.color = 'white';
        ui.style.padding = '10px';
        ui.style.borderRadius = '5px';
        ui.style.fontFamily = 'Arial, sans-serif';
        ui.style.fontSize = '12px';
        ui.style.width = '300px';

        ui.innerHTML = `
            <h3 style="margin: 0 0 10px 0;">Margonem Advanced Bot</h3>
            <div id="gargonem-bot-status">Status: Inicjalizacja...</div>
            <div style="margin: 10px 0;">
                <strong>Tryb:</strong>
                <select id="gargonem-bot-mode" style="margin-left: 5px;">
                    <option value="exp">Expienie</option>
                    <option value="quest">Robienie questów</option>
                    <option value="heros">Szukanie herosów</option>
                    <option value="e2">Stanie na E2</option>
                </select>
            </div>
            <div id="gargonem-bot-actions" style="margin: 10px 0;">
                <button id="gargonem-toggle-bot" style="margin-right: 5px;">Włącz/Wyłącz</button>
                <button id="gargonem-debug-info" style="margin-right: 5px;">Debug</button>
                <button id="gargonem-clear-killed">Wyczyść zabite</button>
            </div>
            <div style="margin: 10px 0;">
                <strong>Opcje:</strong><br>
                <label><input type="checkbox" id="gargonem-auto-use-skills" checked> Automatyczne używanie umiejętności</label><br>
                <label><input type="checkbox" id="gargonem-auto-pick-items" checked> Automatyczne podnoszenie przedmiotów</label><br>
                <label><input type="checkbox" id="gargonem-avoid-npcs" checked> Unikaj określonych NPC</label>
            </div>
            <div id="gargonem-bot-log" style="margin-top: 10px; max-height: 200px; overflow-y: auto; border: 1px solid #333; padding: 5px; background: rgba(0,0,0,0.5);"></div>
        `;

        document.body.appendChild(ui);

        document.getElementById('gargonem-toggle-bot').addEventListener('click', toggleBot);
        document.getElementById('gargonem-debug-info').addEventListener('click', showDebugInfo);
        document.getElementById('gargonem-clear-killed').addEventListener('click', clearKilledMonsters);
        document.getElementById('gargonem-bot-mode').addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            gameState.mode = e.target.value;
            log(`Zmieniono tryb na: ${gameState.mode}`);
        });
    }

    function toggleBot() {
        const statusElement = document.getElementById('gargonem-bot-status');
        if (statusElement.textContent.includes('Aktywny')) {
            statusElement.textContent = 'Status: Wyłączony';
            statusElement.style.color = 'red';
            log('Bot wyłączony');
        } else {
            statusElement.textContent = 'Status: Aktywny';
            statusElement.style.color = 'lime';
            log('Bot włączony');
        }
    }

    function showDebugInfo() {
        log('=== DEBUG INFO ===');
        log(`Tryb: ${gameState.mode}`);
        log(`Pozycja: ${gameState.player.position.x}, ${gameState.player.position.y}`);
        log(`HP: ${gameState.player.hp}/${gameState.player.maxHp} (${Math.round((gameState.player.hp / gameState.player.maxHp) * 100)}%)`);
        log(`MP: ${gameState.player.mp}/${gameState.player.maxMp} (${Math.round((gameState.player.mp / gameState.player.maxMp) * 100)}%)`);
        log(`Poziom: ${gameState.player.level}`);
        log(`Mapa: ${gameState.map.name}`);
        log(`Potwory w pobliżu: ${gameState.map.monsters.length}`);
        log(`Gracze w pobliżu: ${gameState.map.players.length}`);
        log(`Przedmioty na ziemi: ${gameState.map.items.length}`);
        log(`Aktywne questy: ${gameState.quests.active.length}`);
        log(`Zabite potwory: ${Object.keys(gameState.killedMonsters).length}`);
        log('==================');
    }

    function clearKilledMonsters() {
        gameState.killedMonsters = {};
        saveState();
        log('Wyczyszczono listę zabitych potworów');
    }

    // ====== MONITOROWANIE GRY ======
    function startGameMonitoring() {
        setInterval(updateGameState, 1000);
    }

    function updateGameState() {
        if (!unsafeWindow.g || !unsafeWindow.g.game) return;

        try {
            updatePlayerInfo();
            updateMapInfo();
            updateUIStatus();
        } catch (e) {
            log(`Błąd aktualizacji stanu gry: ${e.message}`);
        }
    }

    function updatePlayerInfo() {
        const player = unsafeWindow.g.game.player;

        if (!player) return;

        gameState.player.hp = player.hp;
        gameState.player.maxHp = player.max_hp;
        gameState.player.mp = player.mp;
        gameState.player.maxMp = player.max_mp;
        gameState.player.level = player.level;
        gameState.player.position = { x: player.x, y: player.y };
        gameState.player.target = player.target ? player.target.nick : null;

        gameState.player.skills = [];
        if (player.skills) {
            for (const skillId in player.skills) {
                const skill = player.skills[skillId];
                gameState.player.skills.push({
                    name: skill.name,
                    cooldown: skill.cooldown > 0,
                    lastUsed: 0
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.player.buffs = [];
        if (player.buffs) {
            for (const buffId in player.buffs) {
                const buff = player.buffs[buffId];
                gameState.player.buffs.push(buff.name);
            }
        }

        gameState.isFighting = player.inFight;
    }

    function updateMapInfo() {
        const game = unsafeWindow.g.game;

        if (!game || !game.map) return;

        gameState.map.name = game.map.name || 'Nieznana';
        gameState.map.size = {
            width: game.map.width || 100,
            height: game.map.height || 100
        };

        gameState.map.monsters = [];
        if (game.map.monsters) {
            for (const monsterId in game.map.monsters) {
                const monster = game.map.monsters[monsterId];
                gameState.map.monsters.push({
                    id: monsterId,
                    name: monster.name,
                    position: { x: monster.x, y: monster.y },
                    hp: monster.hp,
                    maxHp: monster.max_hp,
                    level: monster.level,
                    distance: calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, { x: monster.x, y: monster.y }),
                    isBoss: monster.boss
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.map.monsters.sort((a, b) => {
            if (a.isBoss && !b.isBoss) return -1;
            if (!a.isBoss && b.isBoss) return 1;

            const aHpPercent = a.hp / a.maxHp;
            const bHpPercent = b.hp / b.maxHp;
            if (aHpPercent < 0.3 && bHpPercent >= 0.3) return -1;
            if (bHpPercent < 0.3 && aHpPercent >= 0.3) return 1;

            return b.level - a.level;
        });

        gameState.map.players = [];
        if (game.map.players) {
            for (const playerId in game.map.players) {
                const player = game.map.players[playerId];
                if (player.nick === game.player.nick) continue;

                gameState.map.players.push({
                    name: player.nick,
                    position: { x: player.x, y: player.y },
                    distance: calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, { x: player.x, y: player.y }),
                    isHeros: player.nick.includes('[Heros]') || player.nick.includes('Heros')
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.map.npcs = [];
        if (game.map.npcs) {
            for (const npcId in game.map.npcs) {
                const npc = game.map.npcs[npcId];
                gameState.map.npcs.push({
                    id: npcId,
                    name: npc.name,
                    position: { x: npc.x, y: npc.y },
                    distance: calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, { x: npc.x, y: npc.y }),
                    isQuestNpc: npc.quest
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.map.items = [];
        if (game.map.items) {
            for (const itemId in game.map.items) {
                const item = game.map.items[itemId];
                gameState.map.items.push({
                    id: itemId,
                    name: item.name,
                    position: { x: item.x, y: item.y },
                    distance: calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, { x: item.x, y: item.y }),
                    isGold: item.name.includes('Złoto'),
                    isQuestItem: item.quest
                });
            }
        }

        gameState.map.obstacles = [];
        if (game.map.collision) {
            const collision = game.map.collision;
            for (let y = 0; y < collision.length; y++) {
                for (let x = 0; x < collision[y].length; x++) {
                    if (collision[y][x]) {
                        gameState.map.obstacles.push({ x, y });
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function updateUIStatus() {
        const statusElement = document.getElementById('gargonem-bot-status');
        if (statusElement) {
            const modeText = {
                'exp': 'Expienie',
                'quest': 'Robienie questów',
                'heros': 'Szukanie herosów',
                'e2': 'Stanie na E2'
            }[gameState.mode] || gameState.mode;

            statusElement.textContent = `Status: ${gameState.isFighting ? 'Walka' : 'Spokój'} | Tryb: ${modeText} | Poziom: ${gameState.player.level}`;
        }
    }

    // ====== MONITOROWANIE QUESTÓW ======
    function startQuestMonitoring() {
        setInterval(updateQuests, config.questRefreshInterval);
    }

    function updateQuests() {
        if (!unsafeWindow.g || !unsafeWindow.g.game || !unsafeWindow.g.game.quests) return;

        try {
            const quests = unsafeWindow.g.game.quests;

            gameState.quests.active = [];
            if (quests.active) {
                for (const questId in quests.active) {
                    const quest = quests.active[questId];
                    gameState.quests.active.push({
                        id: questId,
                        name: quest.name,
                        progress: quest.progress,
                        isCompleted: quest.progress.current >= quest.progress.total
                    });
                }
            }

            gameState.quests.available = [];
            if (quests.available) {
                for (const questId in quests.available) {
                    const quest = quests.available[questId];
                    gameState.quests.available.push({
                        id: questId,
                        name: quest.name,
                        giver: quest.giver
                    });
                }
            }

            gameState.quests.completed = [];
            if (quests.completed) {
                for (const questId in quests.completed) {
                    const quest = quests.completed[questId];
                    gameState.quests.completed.push({
                        id: questId,
                        name: quest.name,
                        receiver: quest.receiver
                    });
                }
            }

            log(`Zaktualizowano questy. Aktywne: ${gameState.quests.active.length}, Dostępne: ${gameState.quests.available.length}, Ukończone: ${gameState.quests.completed.length}`);
        } catch (e) {
            log(`Błąd aktualizacji questów: ${e.message}`);
        }
    }

    // ====== CYKL DECYZYJNY ======
    function startDecisionLoop() {
        setInterval(makeDecision, config.decisionInterval);
    }

    function makeDecision() {
        if (!unsafeWindow.g || !unsafeWindow.g.game || !document.getElementById('gargonem-bot-status').textContent.includes('Aktywny')) {
            return;
        }

        try {
            if (gameState.isFighting) {
                handleCombat();
                return;
            }

            switch (gameState.mode) {
                case 'exp':
                    handleExpMode();
                    break;
                case 'quest':
                    handleQuestMode();
                    break;
                case 'heros':
                    handleHerosMode();
                    break;
                case 'e2':
                    handleE2Mode();
                    break;
                default:
                    handleExpMode();
            }
        } catch (e) {
            log(`Błąd podejmowania decyzji: ${e.message}`);
        }
    }

    // ====== TRYBY DZIAŁANIA ======
    function handleExpMode() {
        const decisions = [
            checkFleeCondition(),
            checkLowHp(),
            checkLowMp(),
            checkAttackableMonster(),
            checkPickableItem(),
            checkRandomMovement()
        ];

        const bestDecision = getBestDecision(decisions);
        executeDecision(bestDecision);
    }

    function handleQuestMode() {
        if (gameState.quests.completed.length > 0) {
            const quest = gameState.quests.completed[0];
            const npc = gameState.map.npcs.find(n => n.name === quest.receiver);

            if (npc) {
                if (npc.distance <= 1) {
                    return executeDecision({
                        action: 'turn_in_quest',
                        target: quest.id,
                        reason: `Oddaję quest: ${quest.name}`,
                        priority: 10
                    });
                } else {
                    return executeDecision({
                        action: 'move_to',
                        target: npc.position,
                        reason: `Idę oddać quest: ${quest.name}`,
                        priority: 10
                    });
                }
            }
        }

        if (gameState.quests.available.length > 0) {
            const quest = gameState.quests.available[0];
            const npc = gameState.map.npcs.find(n => n.name === quest.giver);

            if (npc) {
                if (npc.distance <= 1) {
                    return executeDecision({
                        action: 'accept_quest',
                        target: quest.id,
                        reason: `Przyjmuję quest: ${quest.name}`,
                        priority: 9
                    });
                } else {
                    return executeDecision({
                        action: 'move_to',
                        target: npc.position,
                        reason: `Idę przyjąć quest: ${quest.name}`,
                        priority: 9
                    });
                }
            }
        }

        handleExpMode();
    }

    function handleHerosMode() {
        const herosPlayers = gameState.map.players.filter(p => p.isHeros);

        if (herosPlayers.length > 0) {
            const closestHeros = herosPlayers[0];

            if (closestHeros.distance <= 1) {
                return executeDecision({
                    action: 'follow_player',
                    target: closestHeros.name,
                    reason: `Podążam za herosem: ${closestHeros.name}`,
                    priority: 8
                });
            } else {
                return executeDecision({
                    action: 'move_to',
                    target: closestHeros.position,
                    reason: `Idę do herosa: ${closestHeros.name}`,
                    priority: 8
                });
            }
        }

        handleExpMode();
    }

    function handleE2Mode() {
        const e2Position = { x: 50, y: 50 };

        if (calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, e2Position) <= 1) {
            return executeDecision({
                action: 'wait',
                reason: 'Stoję na E2',
                priority: 1
            });
        } else {
            return executeDecision({
                action: 'move_to',
                target: e2Position,
                reason: 'Idę na E2',
                priority: 10
            });
        }
    }

    // ====== DECYZJE ======
    function checkFleeCondition() {
        const hpPercentage = gameState.player.hp / gameState.player.maxHp;
        if (hpPercentage < config.fleeThreshold) {
            return { action: 'flee', reason: 'Niskie HP - ucieczka', priority: 10 };
        }
        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkLowHp() {
        const hpPercentage = gameState.player.hp / gameState.player.maxHp;
        if (hpPercentage < config.minHpToFight) {
            return { action: 'use_potion', target: 'hp', reason: 'Niskie HP', priority: 9 };
        }
        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkLowMp() {
        const mpPercentage = gameState.player.mp / gameState.player.maxMp;
        if (mpPercentage < config.minMpToUseSkill) {
            return { action: 'use_potion', target: 'mp', reason: 'Niskie MP', priority: 8 };
        }
        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkAttackableMonster() {
        if (gameState.map.monsters.length === 0) {
            return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
        }

        const closestMonster = gameState.map.monsters[0];

        if (gameState.killedMonsters[closestMonster.name] &&
            gameState.killedMonsters[closestMonster.name] >= 5) {
            log(`Potwór ${closestMonster.name} został już zabity wystarczająco razy, pomijam`);
            return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
        }

        if (closestMonster.distance <= config.maxMonsterDistance) {
            return {
                action: 'attack',
                target: closestMonster.id,
                reason: `Potwór ${closestMonster.name} (Lvl ${closestMonster.level}) w zasięgu`,
                priority: 7
            };
        }

        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkPickableItem() {
        if (!document.getElementById('gargonem-auto-pick-items')?.checked) {
            return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
        }

        if (gameState.map.items.length === 0) {
            return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
        }

        const closestItem = gameState.map.items[0];
        if (closestItem.distance <= config.maxItemDistance) {
            return {
                action: 'pick_up',
                target: closestItem.id,
                reason: `Przedmiot ${closestItem.name} w zasięgu`,
                priority: 6
            };
        }

        return { action: 'wait', priority: 0 };
    }

    function checkRandomMovement() {
        return { action: 'move_random', reason: 'Brak innych akcji', priority: 1 };
    }

    function getBestDecision(decisions) {
        return decisions.reduce((best, current) =>
            (current.priority > best.priority) ? current : best,
            { action: 'wait', priority: 0 }
        );
    }

    // ====== WYKONYWANIE DECYZJI ======
    function executeDecision(decision) {
        if (!decision || !decision.action || decision.priority === 0) {
            return;
        }

        gameState.lastAction = `${decision.action} ${decision.target ? `(${decision.target})` : ''}`;
        gameState.lastActionTime = Date.now();

        log(`Wykonuję: ${decision.action} (${decision.reason})`);

        switch (decision.action) {
            case 'attack':
                attackMonster(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'move_to':
                moveToPosition(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'pick_up':
                pickUpItem(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'use_potion':
                usePotion(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'use_skill':
                useSkill(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'flee':
                fleeFromCombat();
                break;
            case 'talk_to_npc':
                talkToNPC(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'accept_quest':
                acceptQuest(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'turn_in_quest':
                turnInQuest(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'follow_player':
                followPlayer(decision.target);
                break;
            case 'move_random':
                moveRandomly();
                break;
            case 'wait':
            default:
                log('Czekam...');
                break;
        }
    }

    // ====== AKCJE ======
    function attackMonster(monsterId) {
        const monster = gameState.map.monsters.find(m => m.id === monsterId);
        if (!monster) {
            log(`Nie znaleziono potwora o ID: ${monsterId}`);
            return;
        }

        if (monster.distance > 1) {
            log(`Potwór ${monster.name} jest za daleko (${monster.distance.toFixed(1)})`);
            moveToPosition(monster.position);
            return;
        }

        log(`Atakuję ${monster.name} (Lvl ${monster.level}, HP: ${monster.hp}/${monster.maxHp})`);

        if (!gameState.killedMonsters[monster.name]) {
            gameState.killedMonsters[monster.name] = 0;
        }
        gameState.killedMonsters[monster.name]++;
        saveState();

        unsafeWindow.g.game.attack(monsterId);

        if (document.getElementById('gargonem-auto-use-skills')?.checked) {
            useCombatSkills();
        }
    }

    function moveToPosition(position) {
        if (gameState.isMoving) return;

        const distance = calculateDistance(gameState.player.position, position);
        if (distance <= 1) {
            log(`Już jesteśmy przy celu (${position.x}, ${position.y})`);
            return;
        }

        log(`Poruszam się do (${position.x}, ${position.y})`);

        const path = findPath(gameState.player.position, position);
        if (path.length > 0) {
            const nextStep = path[0];
            unsafeWindow.g.game.move(nextStep.x, nextStep.y);
            gameState.isMoving = true;

            setTimeout(() => {
                gameState.isMoving = false;
            }, 1000);
        } else {
            log('Nie znaleziono ścieżki!');
            unsafeWindow.g.game.move(position.x, position.y);
        }
    }

    function findPath(start, end) {
        const openSet = [start];
        const cameFrom = {};
        const gScore = {};
        const fScore = {};

        gScore[start.x + ',' + start.y] = 0;
        fScore[start.x + ',' + start.y] = calculateDistance(start, end);

        while (openSet.length > 0) {
            let current = openSet[0];
            for (const node of openSet) {
                if (fScore[node.x + ',' + node.y] < fScore[current.x + ',' + current.y]) {
                    current = node;
                }
            }

            if (current.x === end.x && current.y === end.y) {
                const path = [];
                let temp = current;
                while (temp.x !== start.x || temp.y !== start.y) {
                    path.push(temp);
                    temp = cameFrom[temp.x + ',' + temp.y];
                }
                return path.reverse();
            }

            openSet.splice(openSet.indexOf(current), 1);

            const neighbors = [
                { x: current.x + 1, y: current.y },
                { x: current.x - 1, y: current.y },
                { x: current.x, y: current.y + 1 },
                { x: current.x, y: current.y - 1 }
            ];

            for (const neighbor of neighbors) {
                if (neighbor.x < 0 || neighbor.x >= gameState.map.size.width ||
                    neighbor.y < 0 || neighbor.y >= gameState.map.size.height) {
                    continue;
                }

                if (config.pathfinding.avoidObstacles && !isPositionWalkable(neighbor)) {
                    continue;
                }

                const tentativeGScore = gScore[current.x + ',' + current.y] + 1;

                if (!gScore[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y] ||
                    tentativeGScore < gScore[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y]) {
                    cameFrom[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y] = current;
                    gScore[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y] = tentativeGScore;
                    fScore[neighbor.x + ',' + neighbor.y] = tentativeGScore + calculateDistance(neighbor, end);

                    if (!openSet.some(node => node.x === neighbor.x && node.y === neighbor.y)) {
                        openSet.push(neighbor);
                    }
                }
            }

            if (Object.keys(cameFrom).length > config.pathfinding.maxSteps) {
                log('Przekroczono maksymalną liczbę kroków w szukaniu ścieżki');
                return [];
            }
        }

        log('Nie znaleziono ścieżki!');
        return [];
    }

    function pickUpItem(itemId) {
        const item = gameState.map.items.find(i => i.id === itemId);
        if (!item) {
            log(`Nie znaleziono przedmiotu o ID: ${itemId}`);
            return;
        }

        if (item.distance > 1) {
            log(`Przedmiot ${item.name} jest za daleko (${item.distance.toFixed(1)})`);
            moveToPosition(item.position);
            return;
        }

        log(`Podnoszę ${item.name}`);
        unsafeWindow.g.game.pickUpItem(itemId);
    }

    function usePotion(type) {
        log(`Używam mikstury: ${type}`);
        unsafeWindow.g.game.usePotion(type);
    }

    function useSkill(skillName) {
        if (!document.getElementById('gargonem-auto-use-skills')?.checked) {
            return;
        }

        const skill = gameState.player.skills.find(s => s.name === skillName);
        if (!skill) {
            log(`Nie znaleziono umiejętności: ${skillName}`);
            return;
        }

        log(`Używam umiejętności: ${skillName}`);
        unsafeWindow.g.game.useSkill(skillName);
    }

    function useCombatSkills() {
        if (gameState.player.hp / gameState.player.maxHp < 0.5) {
            const healSkill = gameState.player.skills.find(s =>
                s.name.includes('Leczenie') || s.name.includes('Heal')
            );
            if (healSkill) {
                useSkill(healSkill.name);
                return;
            }
        }

        const offensiveSkills = gameState.player.skills.filter(s =>
            !s.cooldown &&
            (s.name.includes('Atak') || s.name.includes('Fireball') || s.name.includes('Błyskawica'))
        );

        if (offensiveSkills.length > 0) {
            useSkill(offensiveSkills[0].name);
        }
    }

    function fleeFromCombat() {
        log('Uciekam z walki!');
        unsafeWindow.g.game.flee();
    }

    function talkToNPC(npcId) {
        log(`Rozmawiam z NPC o ID: ${npcId}`);
        unsafeWindow.g.game.talkToNPC(npcId);
    }

    function acceptQuest(questId) {
        log(`Przyjmuję quest o ID: ${questId}`);
        unsafeWindow.g.game.acceptQuest(questId);
    }

    function turnInQuest(questId) {
        log(`Oddaję quest o ID: ${questId}`);
        unsafeWindow.g.game.turnInQuest(questId);
    }

    function followPlayer(playerName) {
        const player = gameState.map.players.find(p => p.name === playerName);
        if (!player) {
            log(`Nie znaleziono gracza: ${playerName}`);
            return;
        }

        if (player.distance <= 1) {
            log(`Podążam za graczem: ${playerName}`);
        } else {
            moveToPosition(player.position);
        }
    }

    function moveRandomly() {
        if (gameState.isMoving) return;

        const directions = [
            { x: 0, y: -1 },
            { x: 1, y: 0 },
            { x: 0, y: 1 },
            { x: -1, y: 0 }
        ];

        const randomDir = directions[Math.floor(Math.random() * directions.length)];
        const newPos = {
            x: gameState.player.position.x + randomDir.x,
            y: gameState.player.position.y + randomDir.y
        };

        if (newPos.x >= 0 && newPos.x < gameState.map.size.width &&
            newPos.y >= 0 && newPos.y < gameState.map.size.height &&
            isPositionWalkable(newPos)) {
            unsafeWindow.g.game.move(newPos.x, newPos.y);
        }
    }

    // ====== INICJALIZACJA ======
    init();
})();

// ==UserScript==
// @name         Margonem E2 Bot - v4.5 HARD RESET
// @version      4.5
// @description  Wymuszanie odblokowania postaci po walce
// @author       Gemini
// @match        http://*.margonem.pl/
// @match        https://*.margonem.pl/
// @run-at       document-idle
// @grant        none
// ==/UserScript==

(function() {
    'use strict';

    class MargoBotV45 {
        constructor() {
            this.config = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("margo-bot-v45")) || {
                x: 100, y: 100, target: "", active: false
            };
            this.lastAttack = 0;
            this.battleStart = 0;
            this.init();
        }

        init() {
            this.createUI();
            setInterval(() => this.loop(), 300);
        }

        send(cmd) { if (window._g) window._g(cmd); }

        createUI() {
            if (document.getElementById("margo-v45-ui")) return;
            const ui = document.createElement("div");
            ui.id = "margo-v45-ui";
            ui.style = "position:fixed; left:"+this.config.x+"px; top:"+this.config.y+"px; width:190px; background:#111; color:#00fbff; z-index:999999; padding:10px; border:2px solid #00fbff; border-radius:5px; font-family:monospace; font-size:11px;";
            ui.innerHTML = `
                <div id="margo-drag" style="cursor:move; background:#00fbff; color:#000; padding:4px; font-weight:bold; text-align:center; margin:-10px -10px 8px -10px;">BOT E2 V4.5 (HARD)</div>
                CEL: <input type="text" id="margo-target" value="${this.config.target}" style="width:100%; background:#000; color:#fff; border:1px solid #00fbff; margin-bottom:8px; padding:2px;">
                <label style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:8px; cursor:pointer;">
                    <input type="checkbox" id="margo-active" ${this.config.active ? 'checked' : ''}> AKTYWNY
                </label>
                <div id="margo-status" style="margin-top:8px; color:#aaa; border-top:1px solid #333; padding-top:5px;">Gotowy...</div>
            `;
            document.body.appendChild(ui);
            ui.querySelector("#margo-target").oninput = (e) => { this.config.target = e.target.value; this.save(); };
            ui.querySelector("#margo-active").onchange = (e) => { this.config.active = e.target.checked; this.save(); };
            this.setupDrag(ui);
        }

        setupDrag(el) {
            const drag = el.querySelector("#margo-drag");
            drag.onmousedown = (e) => {
                let ox = e.clientX - el.offsetLeft, oy = e.clientY - el.offsetTop;
                document.onmousemove = (e) => { el.style.left = (e.clientX - ox)+'px'; el.style.top = (e.clientY - oy)+'px'; };
                document.onmouseup = () => { document.onmousemove = null; this.config.x = parseInt(el.style.left); this.config.y = parseInt(el.style.top); this.save(); };
            };
        }

        save() { localStorage.setItem("margo-bot-v45", JSON.stringify(this.config)); }

        loop() {
            const status = document.getElementById("margo-status");
            const ni = window.Engine && window.Engine.hero;
            const si = window.g && window.g.hero;

            if ((!ni && !si) || !this.config.active) {
                if (status) status.innerText = "BOT OFF";
                return;
            }

            const battle = ni ? window.Engine.battle : window.g.battle;
            
            if (battle) {
                if (this.battleStart === 0) this.battleStart = Date.now();
                status.innerText = "W WALCE (" + Math.floor((Date.now() - this.battleStart)/1000) + "s)";
                
                // 1. Próba zakończenia walki normalnie
                if (Date.now() - this.lastAttack > 1000) {
                    this.send("fight&a=f");
                    if (battle.end) this.send("fight&a=quit");
                    this.lastAttack = Date.now();
                }

                // 2. HARD RESET: Jeśli walka trwa dłużej niż 2.5 sekundy - wymuś czyszczenie
                if (Date.now() - this.battleStart > 2500) {
                    status.innerText = "WYMUSZAM KONIEC...";
                    if (ni) {
                        window.Engine.battle = null;
                        if (window.Engine.lock) window.Engine.lock.remove("battle");
                    } else {
                        window.g.battle = null;
                        if (window.g.lock) window.g.lock.remove("battle");
                    }
                    this.battleStart = 0; // Reset timera po wyczyszczeniu
                }
                return;
            } else {
                this.battleStart = 0; 
            }

            const hero = ni ? window.Engine.hero.d : window.hero;
            const targetName = this.config.target.toLowerCase().trim();
            if (!hero || !targetName) return;

            const npcs = ni ? window.Engine.npcs.check() : window.g.npc;
            let target = null;
            for (let i in npcs) {
                const n = ni ? npcs[i].d : npcs[i];
                if (n && n.nick && n.nick.toLowerCase().includes(targetName) && !n.del) {
                    target = { id: i, x: n.x, y: n.y };
                    break;
                }
            }

            if (target) {
                const dist = Math.max(Math.abs(hero.x - target.x), Math.abs(hero.y - target.y));
                status.innerText = "CEL: " + dist + "m";

                if (dist <= 1) {
                    if (Date.now() - this.lastAttack > 1200) {
                        this.send(`fight&a=attack&id=-${target.id}`);
                        this.lastAttack = Date.now();
                    }
                } else {
                    if (ni) window.Engine.hero.autoPath = [{x: target.x, y: target.y}];
                    else window.hero.beginMove(target.x, target.y);
                }
            } else {
                status.innerText = "SZUKAM: " + targetName;
            }
        }
    }

    setTimeout(() => new MargoBotV45(), 1000);
})();
// ==UserScript==
