// @name         Margonem - Bot EXP + E2 V1
// @match         https://*.margonem.pl/
// @run-at       document-end
// @grant         none
// ==/UserScript==

(function() {
    'use strict';

    function initBot() {
        if (typeof window.Engine === 'undefined' || !window.Engine.npcs) {
            setTimeout(initBot, 500);
            return;
        }

        // --- KONFIGURACJA ---
        window._botActive = false;
        window._targetList = [];
        let _lockBot = false;
        let _lastTargetName = "Nieznany NPC";
        let _lastLootId = 0;
        let _wasInBattle = false;

        const expPresets = {
            "GROBOWCE (18lvl)": ["Adept", "Duża larwa", "Trupówka pospolita", "Gacówka rogata", "Szabrownik", "Skolopendra podziemna"],
            "MRÓWKI (20lvl)": ["Mrówcza Królowa", "Brązowa mrówka tragarz", "Brązowa mrówka żołnierz", "Brązowa mrówka robotnica"],
            "PUMY/TYGRYSY (21lvl)": ["Puma", "Tygrys"],

        // GUI
        const gui = document.createElement('div');
        gui.style = "position:fixed; top:20px; left:20px; z-index:10000; background:rgba(10,10,10,0.9); color:white; padding:15px; border:2px solid #00ffff; border-radius:10px; font-family:sans-serif; width:250px; box-shadow: 0 0 20px rgba(0,255,255,0.3);";

        const sortedKeys = Object.keys(expPresets).sort((a, b) => {
            if (a.includes("---")) return 1;
            return parseInt(a.match(/\d+/) || 0) - parseInt(b.match(/\d+/) || 0);
        });

        gui.innerHTML = `
            <div id="drag" style="text-align:center; font-weight:bold; color:#00ffff; margin-bottom:10px; cursor:move;">EXP + E2 Auto</div>
            <button id="b_togl" style="width:100%; background:red; color:white; border:none; padding:8px; border-radius:5px; font-weight:bold; cursor:pointer;">BOT: OFF</button>
            <select id="b_preset" style="width:100%; margin-top:10px; background:#222; color:white; border:1px solid #444; padding:5px;">
                <option value="">-- Wybierz Exp --</option>
                ${sortedKeys.map(k => `<option value="${k}">${k}</option>`).join('')}
            </select>
            <div style="font-size:10px; margin-top:10px; color:#0f0;">Cele: <span id="b_stat">Brak</span></div>
            <button id="b_clear" style="width:100%; margin-top:5px; font-size:10px; background:#400; color:#f88; border:none; cursor:pointer;">Wyczyść cele</button>
        `;
        document.body.appendChild(gui);

        // DRAG GUI
        let isD = false, ox, oy;
        gui.onmousedown = e => { if(e.target.id==="drag") { isD = true; ox = e.clientX - gui.offsetLeft; oy = e.clientY - gui.offsetTop; }};
        document.onmousemove = e => { if(isD) { gui.style.left = (e.clientX-ox)+'px'; gui.style.top = (e.clientY-oy)+'px'; }};
        document.onmouseup = () => isD = false;

        // AKCJE GUI
        document.getElementById('b_togl').onclick = function() {
            window._botActive = !window._botActive;
            this.innerText = window._botActive ? "BOT: ON" : "BOT: OFF";
            this.style.background = window._botActive ? "green" : "red";
        };
        document.getElementById('b_preset').onchange = function() {
            if(this.value) {
                window._targetList = [...expPresets[this.value]];
                document.getElementById('b_stat').innerText = window._targetList.slice(0,3).join(", ") + "...";
            }
        };
        document.getElementById('b_clear').onclick = () => { window._targetList = []; document.getElementById('b_stat').innerText = "Brak"; };

        // PĘTLA GŁÓWNA
        setInterval(() => {
            if (!window._botActive) return;

            // OBSŁUGA LOOTU (TYLKO PODNOSZENIE)
            if (window.g?.loot && window.g.loot.id !== _lastLootId) {
                _lastLootId = window.g.loot.id;
                // Podnieś (klawisz F)
                setTimeout(() => { window.Engine.keyHandler.down(70); setTimeout(()=>window.Engine.keyHandler.up(70), 50); }, 300);
                return;
            }

            // OBSŁUGA WALKI
            if (window.Engine?.battle?.show) {
                _wasInBattle = true;

                if (window.Engine.battle.autoFight && !window.Engine.battle.isAuto)
                    window.Engine.battle.autoFight(true);

                return;
            }

            // WYKRYCIE KOŃCA WALKI
            if (_wasInBattle && !window.Engine?.battle?.show) {
                _wasInBattle = false;
                goToNextLocation();
            }           

            if (_lockBot) return;

            // SZUKANIE NPC
            const npcs = window.Engine.npcs.getDrawableList();
            const hero = window.Engine.hero;
            let nearest = null, minDist = Infinity;

            for (let id in npcs) {
                const n = npcs[id];
                if (!n?.d || n.isDead) continue;
                if (window._targetList.some(t => n.d.nick.toLowerCase().includes(t.toLowerCase()))) {
                    const d = Math.abs(hero.d.x - n.d.x) + Math.abs(hero.d.y - n.d.y);
                    if (d < minDist) { minDist = d; nearest = n; }
                }
            }

            if (nearest) {
                _lastTargetName = nearest.d.nick;
                if (minDist <= 1) {
                    _lockBot = true;
                    if (hero.heroAtackRequest) hero.heroAtackRequest(nearest.d.id);
                    else nearest.onMouseClick();
                    setTimeout(() => _lockBot = false, 800);
                } else {
                    window.Engine.hero.autoGoTo({x: nearest.d.x, y: nearest.d.y});
                }
            }
        }, 400);
    }
    function goToNextLocation() {
        console.log("Walka zakończona — przechodzę dalej");

        window.Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: 19, y: 15 }); // ← tu wpisz współrzędne wyjścia
}
    const s = document.createElement('script');
    s.textContent = `(${initBot.toString()})();`;
    document.head.appendChild(s);
})();

// ==UserScript==
// @name         AUTOX NI zestawy

(async (window, sleep) => {

    const initCSS = () => {

        const $container2 = $('<div id="p4d0k1ll"></div>').css({
            'width':'110px',
            'position':'absolute',
            'z-index':'999',
            'background':'rgba(15, 15, 15, 0.85)',
            'border':'1px solid orange',
            'color':'white'
        });
        const $head = $('<div id="p4d0k1ll-head"></div>').css({
            'width':'110px',
            'height':'25px',
        });

        const $body = $('<div id="p4d0k1ll-body"></div>').css({
            'width':'110px',
            'height':'40px',
            'font-size':'8px'
        })

        const $settings_input = $('<div id="p4d0k1ll-settings">⚙️</div>').css({
            'float':'left'
        });

        const $mode_input = $('<input type="checkbox" id="mode" tabindex="0">').css({
            'float':'left'
        });

        const $levels_input = $('<input type="text" id="levels" autocomplete="off" placeholder="MIN-MAX">').css({
            'width':'65px',
            'height':'15px',
            'background':'rgba(15, 15, 15, 0.45)',
            'border':'0',
            'border-bottom':'1px dotted orange',
            'color':'orange',
            'text-align':'center',
            'float':'left'
        });

        const $backmode_input = $('<input type="checkbox" id="backmode" tabindex="0"><small>KORDY</small>').css({
            'float':'left'
        });

        const $coords_input = $('<input type="text" id="coords" autocomplete="off" placeholder="X,Y">').css({
            'width':'55px',
            'height':'15px',
            'background':'rgba(15, 15, 15, 0.45)',
            'border':'0',
            'border-bottom':'1px dotted orange',
            'color':'orange',
            'text-align':'center',
            'float':'left'
        });

        const $automode_input = $('<span style="clear: both;"></span><input type="checkbox" id="automode"><small>AUTO F</small><br>').css({

            'text-align':'left'
        });

        const $follow_input = $('<input type="checkbox" id="follow"><small>FOLLOW</small>').css({
            'float':'left',
            'text-align':'left'
        });

        const $build_input = $('<input type="checkbox" id="build"><small>ZESTAW</small>').css({
            'float':'left',
            'text-align':'left'
        });

        $("body").append($container2);
        $("#p4d0k1ll").append($head, $body);
        $("#p4d0k1ll-head").append($settings_input, $mode_input, $levels_input);
        $("#p4d0k1ll-body").append($backmode_input, $coords_input, $automode_input, $follow_input, $build_input);

        $('#p4d0k1ll-settings').click(function () {
            $('#p4d0k1ll-body').toggle('slow');
        });

    }
    window.onload = initCSS();

    GM_getValue('p4d0k1llni') || GM_setValue('p4d0k1llni', JSON.stringify({ x: 0, y: 0 }));

    let padoPosition = JSON.parse(GM_getValue('p4d0k1llni'));

    document.querySelector('#p4d0k1ll').style.left = `${padoPosition.x}`;
    document.querySelector('#p4d0k1ll').style.top = `${padoPosition.y}`;
    document.querySelector('#p4d0k1ll').style.position = 'absolute';

    $(document.querySelector('#p4d0k1ll')).draggable({
        stop: () => {
            padoPosition.x = document.querySelector('#p4d0k1ll').style.left;
            padoPosition.y = document.querySelector('#p4d0k1ll').style.top;
            GM_setValue('p4d0k1llni', JSON.stringify(padoPosition));

            document.querySelector('#p4d0k1ll').style.left = padoPosition.x;
            document.querySelector('#p4d0k1ll').style.top = padoPosition.y;
            document.querySelector('#p4d0k1ll').style.position = 'absolute';
        }
    });

    const loadSettings = () => {
        sleep(4000);
        if (GM_getValue('status' + getCookie("mchar_id")) == true) {
            document.getElementById('mode').setAttribute('checked', 'checked');
        }
        if (GM_getValue('backmode' + getCookie("mchar_id")) == true) {
            document.getElementById('backmode').setAttribute('checked', 'checked');
        }
        if (GM_getValue('automode' + getCookie("mchar_id")) == true) {
            document.getElementById('automode').setAttribute('checked', 'checked');
        }
        if (GM_getValue('follow' + getCookie("mchar_id")) == true) {
            document.getElementById('follow').setAttribute('checked', 'checked');
        }
        if (GM_getValue('build' + getCookie("mchar_id")) == true) {
            document.getElementById('build').setAttribute('checked', 'checked');
        }
        if (GM_getValue('coords' + getCookie("mchar_id")) == null || GM_getValue('coords' + getCookie("mchar_id")) == undefined) {
            GM_setValue('coords' + getCookie("mchar_id"), '00,00');
        }
        if (GM_getValue("levels" + getCookie("mchar_id")) == null || GM_getValue('levels' + getCookie("mchar_id")) == undefined) {
            GM_setValue("levels" + getCookie("mchar_id"), '0-500');
        }
        document.getElementById("levels").value = GM_getValue("levels" + getCookie("mchar_id"));
        document.getElementById("coords").value = GM_getValue("coords" + getCookie("mchar_id"));
        console.log('[P4D0K1LL] Załadowano ustawienia.');
    }
    window.onload = loadSettings();

    document.getElementById('levels').onchange = () => {
        GM_setValue("levels" + getCookie("mchar_id"), document.getElementById("levels").value);
        console.log('[P4D0K1LL] Zapisano ustawienia.');
    }

    document.getElementById('coords').onchange = () => {
        GM_setValue("coords" + getCookie("mchar_id"), document.getElementById("coords").value);
        console.log('[P4D0K1LL] Zapisano ustawienia.');
    }

    document.getElementById('follow').addEventListener('click', () => {
        GM_setValue("follow" + getCookie("mchar_id"), document.getElementById(`follow`).checked);
        console.log('[P4D0K1LL] Zapisano ustawienia.');
    });

    document.getElementById('mode').addEventListener('click', () => {

        console.log('[P4D0K1LL] Zapisano ustawienia.');
    });

    document.getElementById('automode').addEventListener('click', () => {

        console.log('[P4D0K1LL] Zapisano ustawienia.');
    });

    document.getElementById('backmode').addEventListener('click', () => {
        GM_setValue("backmode" + getCookie("mchar_id"), document.getElementById(`backmode`).checked);
        console.log('[P4D0K1LL] Zapisano ustawienia.');
    });

    document.getElementById('build').addEventListener('click', () => {
        GM_setValue("build" + getCookie("mchar_id"), document.getElementById(`build`).checked);
        console.log('[P4D0K1LL] Zapisano ustawienia.');
    });


    let lastAttackReq = Date.now();
    const sendAttackReq = (id) => {

        const now = new Date();
        const day = String(now.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
        const month = String(now.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
        const year = now.getFullYear();
        const hours = String(now.getHours()).padStart(2, '0');
        const minutes = String(now.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0');
        const seconds = String(now.getSeconds()).padStart(2, '0');


        if ((now - lastAttackReq) < 300) return; // Sprawdza czy minelo 300ms

        _g('fight&a=attack&id=' + id);
        lastAttackReq = now; // Aktualizuje czas ostatniego wywolania
        //console.log(`Attack req sent. Time: [${day}.${month}.${year} - ${hours}:${minutes}:${seconds}]`);
    };



    const initX = async () => {
        while (true) {
            var targets = [];
            var eee = Engine.others.getDrawableList().filter(obj => {return obj.d});
            var getOthers;
            if (Engine.party) {
                const partyMembers = new Set(Object.keys(Engine.party.getMembers()));
                getOthers = eee.filter(obj => {
                    return (obj.d.relation == 6 || obj.d.relation == 3 || obj.d.relation == '' || obj.d.relation == 1) &&
                           obj.d.lvl >= document.getElementById("levels").value.split("-")[0] &&
                           obj.d.lvl <= document.getElementById("levels").value.split("-")[1] &&
                           !partyMembers.has(obj.d.id); // Sprawdzenie, czy ID jest w drużynie
                });
            } else {
                getOthers = eee.filter(obj => {
                    return (obj.d.relation == 6 || obj.d.relation == 3 || obj.d.relation == '' || obj.d.relation == 1) &&
                    obj.d.lvl >= document.getElementById("levels").value.split("-")[0] &&
                    obj.d.lvl <= document.getElementById("levels").value.split("-")[1]
                });
            }
            //const partyMembers = new Set(Object.keys(Engine.party.getMembers()));

            let isInBattle = Engine.battle.getShow();
            if (Engine.map.d.pvp == 2 && !isInBattle) {
                for (var i in getOthers) {
                    let emotesting = Engine.emotions.getList();
                    var playerEmo = "idk";
                    for(let j in emotesting)
                    {
                        if(emotesting[j].source.isPlayer == true && emotesting[j].source.d.nick == getOthers[i].d.nick)
                        {
                            playerEmo = emotesting[j];
                        }
                    }
                    if (playerEmo.name == undefined) {
                        targets.push({
                            prof: getOthers[i].d.prof,
                            id: getOthers[i].d.id,
                            x: getOthers[i].d.x,
                            y: getOthers[i].d.y,
                            distance: Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.x - getOthers[i].d.x) + Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.y - getOthers[i].d.y)
                        });
                    } else if (playerEmo.name != 'battle' && playerEmo.name != 'pvpprotected') {
                        targets.push({
                            prof: getOthers[i].d.prof,
                            id: getOthers[i].d.id,
                            x: getOthers[i].d.x,
                            y: getOthers[i].d.y,
                            distance: Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.x - getOthers[i].d.x) + Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.y - getOthers[i].d.y)
                        })
                    }
                }
                if (targets != '') {
                    targets = targets.sort((a, b) => (a.distance > b.distance) ? 1 : -1);
                    let CurrentBuildID = Engine.buildsManager.getBuildsCommons().getCurrentId();

                    // ID BOLIDOW WEDLUG PROFESJI ('t': 6  ==> ustawia 6. zestaw vs trop)
                    const buildMapping = {
                        't': 8,
                        'm': 5,
                        'w': 4,
                        'h': 6,
                        'p': 3,
                        'b': 7
                    };

                    if (targets[0].distance <= 8 && document.getElementById("build").checked) {
                        let targetProf = targets[0].prof;
                        let targetBuildId = buildMapping[targetProf];

                        if (targetBuildId !== undefined && targetBuildId !== CurrentBuildID) {
                            //console.log('Zmieniam bolid na: ', targetBuildId);
                            Engine.buildsManager.getBuildsRequests().setCurrentBuildId(targetBuildId);
                        }
                    }


                    if (targets[0].distance > 2 && document.getElementById("follow").checked) {
                        Engine.hero.autoGoTo({
                            x: targets[0].x,
                            y: targets[0].y
                        });
                    } else if (document.getElementById('mode').checked && targets[0].distance <= 4){ // && targets[0].distance < 3
                        sendAttackReq(targets[0].id);
                    }



                } else if (document.getElementById("backmode").checked) {
                    if (Engine.hero.d.x != document.getElementById("coords").value.split(",")[0] || Engine.hero.d.y != document.getElementById("coords").value.split(",")[1]) {
                        let x = parseInt(document.getElementById("coords").value.split(",")[0]);
                        let y = parseInt(document.getElementById("coords").value.split(",")[1]);
                        Engine.hero.autoGoTo({
                            x: x,
                            y: y
                        });
                    }
                } else if (document.getElementById("automode").checked) {
                    if (Engine.battle) {
                        API.addCallbackToEvent("open_battle_window", () => {
                            eval('Engine.battle.autoFight()')
                        });
                    }
                }
            }
            await sleep(35);
        }
    }
    window.onload = initX();
})(typeof unsafeWindow !== "undefined" ? unsafeWindow : window, (ms) => new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms)));

// ==UserScript==
// @name         AUTOX NI zestawy

    });


    let lastAttackReq = Date.now();
    const sendAttackReq = (id) => {

        const now = new Date();
        const day = String(now.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
        const month = String(now.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
        const year = now.getFullYear();
        const hours = String(now.getHours()).padStart(2, '0');
        const minutes = String(now.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0');
        const seconds = String(now.getSeconds()).padStart(2, '0');


        if ((now - lastAttackReq) < 300) return; // Sprawdza czy minelo 300ms

        _g('fight&a=attack&id=' + id);
        lastAttackReq = now; // Aktualizuje czas ostatniego wywolania
        //console.log(`Attack req sent. Time: [${day}.${month}.${year} - ${hours}:${minutes}:${seconds}]`);
    };



    const initX = async () => {
        while (true) {
            var targets = [];
            var eee = Engine.others.getDrawableList().filter(obj => {return obj.d});
            var getOthers;
            if (Engine.party) {
                const partyMembers = new Set(Object.keys(Engine.party.getMembers()));
                getOthers = eee.filter(obj => {
                    return (obj.d.relation == 6 || obj.d.relation == 3 || obj.d.relation == '' || obj.d.relation == 1) &&
                           obj.d.lvl >= document.getElementById("levels").value.split("-")[0] &&
                           obj.d.lvl <= document.getElementById("levels").value.split("-")[1] &&
                           !partyMembers.has(obj.d.id); // Sprawdzenie, czy ID jest w drużynie
                });
            } else {
                getOthers = eee.filter(obj => {
                    return (obj.d.relation == 6 || obj.d.relation == 3 || obj.d.relation == '' || obj.d.relation == 1) &&
                    obj.d.lvl >= document.getElementById("levels").value.split("-")[0] &&
                    obj.d.lvl <= document.getElementById("levels").value.split("-")[1]
                });
            }
            //const partyMembers = new Set(Object.keys(Engine.party.getMembers()));

            let isInBattle = Engine.battle.getShow();
            if (Engine.map.d.pvp == 2 && !isInBattle) {
                for (var i in getOthers) {
                    let emotesting = Engine.emotions.getList();
                    var playerEmo = "idk";
                    for(let j in emotesting)
                    {
                        if(emotesting[j].source.isPlayer == true && emotesting[j].source.d.nick == getOthers[i].d.nick)
                        {
                            playerEmo = emotesting[j];
                        }
                    }
                    if (playerEmo.name == undefined) {
                        targets.push({
                            prof: getOthers[i].d.prof,
                            id: getOthers[i].d.id,
                            x: getOthers[i].d.x,
                            y: getOthers[i].d.y,
                            distance: Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.x - getOthers[i].d.x) + Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.y - getOthers[i].d.y)
                        });
                    } else if (playerEmo.name != 'battle' && playerEmo.name != 'pvpprotected') {
                        targets.push({
                            prof: getOthers[i].d.prof,
                            id: getOthers[i].d.id,
                            x: getOthers[i].d.x,
                            y: getOthers[i].d.y,
                            distance: Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.x - getOthers[i].d.x) + Math.abs(Engine.hero.d.y - getOthers[i].d.y)
                        })
                    }
                }
                if (targets != '') {
                    targets = targets.sort((a, b) => (a.distance > b.distance) ? 1 : -1);
                    let CurrentBuildID = Engine.buildsManager.getBuildsCommons().getCurrentId();

                    // ID BOLIDOW WEDLUG PROFESJI ('t': 6  ==> ustawia 6. zestaw vs trop)
                    const buildMapping = {
                        't': 4,
                        'm': 4,
                        'w': 4,
                        'h': 4,
                        'p': 5,
                        'b': 4
                    };

                    if (targets[0].distance <= 8 && document.getElementById("build").checked) {
                        let targetProf = targets[0].prof;
                        let targetBuildId = buildMapping[targetProf];

                        if (targetBuildId !== undefined && targetBuildId !== CurrentBuildID) {
                            //console.log('Zmieniam bolid na: ', targetBuildId);
                            Engine.buildsManager.getBuildsRequests().setCurrentBuildId(targetBuildId);
                        }
                    }


                    if (targets[0].distance > 2 && document.getElementById("follow").checked) {
                        Engine.hero.autoGoTo({
                            x: targets[0].x,
                            y: targets[0].y
                        });
                    } else if (document.getElementById('mode').checked && targets[0].distance <= 4){ // && targets[0].distance < 3
                        sendAttackReq(targets[0].id);
                    }



                } else if (document.getElementById("backmode").checked) {
                    if (Engine.hero.d.x != document.getElementById("coords").value.split(",")[0] || Engine.hero.d.y != document.getElementById("coords").value.split(",")[1]) {
                        let x = parseInt(document.getElementById("coords").value.split(",")[0]);
                        let y = parseInt(document.getElementById("coords").value.split(",")[1]);
                        Engine.hero.autoGoTo({
                            x: x,
                            y: y
                        });
                    }
                } else if (document.getElementById("automode").checked) {
                    if (Engine.battle) {
                        API.addCallbackToEvent("open_battle_window", () => {
                            eval('Engine.battle.autoFight()')
                        });
                    }
                }
            }
            await sleep(35);
        }
    }
    window.onload = initX();
})(typeof unsafeWindow !== "undefined" ? unsafeWindow : window, (ms) => new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms)));

// ==UserScript==
// @name         ZENTRIX - Margonem Hunter V1.2.8 (Fast)
// @version      1.2.8
// @description  Szybkie przechodzenie między mapami, gdy brak mobów.
// @author       Zentrix Team
// @match        https://*.margonem.pl/
// @run-at       document-end
// @grant        none
// ==/UserScript==

(function() {
    'use strict';

    function initZentrix() {
        if (typeof window.Engine === 'undefined' || !window.Engine.npcs || !window.Engine.map) {
            setTimeout(initZentrix, 500);
            return;
        }

        // --- KONFIGURACJA TRAS ---
        const routes = {
            "ANDARUM (70lvl)": ["Andarum Ilami", "Skały Mroźnych Śpiewów", "Cmentarzysko Szerpów", "Śnieżna Granica"]
        };

        const hardcodedGates = {
            "Andarum Ilami": { "Skały Mroźnych Śpiewów": [0, 6] },
            "Skały Mroźnych Śpiewów": { "Andarum Ilami": [63, 5], "Cmentarzysko Szerpów": [10, 0] },
            "Cmentarzysko Szerpów": { "Skały Mroźnych Śpiewów": [12, 63], "Śnieżna Granica": [0, 26] },
            "Śnieżna Granica": { "Cmentarzysko Szerpów": [95, 26] }
        };

        window._botActive = false;
        window._targetList = [];
        window._currentPreset = "";
        let _lockBot = false;
        let _routeDirection = 1;
        let _emptyTicks = 0;

        const expPresets = {
            "TOLLOKI (45lvl)": ["Tollok Surbit", "Tollok Boger", "Tollok Tuarai", "Tollok Zibink"],
            "ORKOWIE (47lvl)": ["Thowar", "Krogor", "Ork zhaghokk", "Ork bashwooz", "Ork trarroll", "Ork wuakl", "Ork kuurgh"],
            "GALARETY (51lvl)": ["Zgniła galareta", "Przeźroczysta galareta", "Wodna galareta", "Pąsowa galareta", "Morska galareta"],
            "KOBOLDY (54lvl)": ["Kobold", "Kobold łucznik", "Kobold nożownik"],
            "ŻĄDŁAKI (58lvl)": ["Żądłak rogaty", "Nieżłopka wątpia", "Żądłak", "Wściekłówka"],
            "BAZYLISZKI (61lvl)": ["Magiczny bazyliszek", "Srebrny bazyliszek", "Bazyliszek Mroku", "Purpurowy bazyliszek"],
            "GNOLLE (64lvl)": ["Gnoll strażnik", "Gnoll łowca", "Gnoll łucznik", "Gnoll wojownik", "Gnoll mistrz ostrzy"],
            "OLBRZYMY (67lvl)": ["Wiekowy olbrzym", "Olbrzym miotający", "Olbrzym z maczugą"],
            "ANDARUM (70lvl)": ["Lazurowy tygrys", "Śnieżny tygrys", "Strażnik Andarum", "Śnieżny wilk", "Śnieżny niedźwiedź", "Śnieżny kocur"],
            "MNISI (74lvl)": ["Klasztorny brodacz", "Strażnik cennych ksiąg", "Władca pastorału", "Sługa ołtarza", "Zakonnik wyższego kręgu", "Bardzo wściekły mnich", "Zamyślony mnich", "Zakapturzony mędrzec", "Pokutujący zakonnik", "Członek zakonu", "Brat andaryjski", "Wojownik w habicie"],
            "WODNIKI (75lvl)": ["Wodnik", "Mamuna", "Dziwożona", "Topielica rzęsy", "Topielec oczeretu", "Topielica tataraku"],
            "Magazynierzy (78)": ["Świątynny kucharz", "Kawał chłopa", "Nadęty dryblas", "Magazynier z halabardą", "Wytatuowany osiłek", "Łowca Skór", "Zarządca magazynu"],
            "EREM (80lvl)": ["Śmierć magazyniera", "Kościste straszydło", "Przerażający mnich", "Duchowy rozpruwacz", "Mnich chybione zaklęcie"],
            "Dławiki (83lvl)": ["Dławiciel jaskiniowy", "Szary dławiciel"],
            "KRASNOLUDY (86lvl)": ["Krasnoludzki górnik", "Krasnoludzki strażnik", "Krasnoludzki kowal"],
            "BANDYCI (100lvl)": ["Celne oko", "Sprytny bandzior", "Cwany bandyta", "Łowca naiwniaków", "Rudy twardziel"],
            "--- ELITY II (ALL) ---": ["Mushita", "Kotołak Tropiciel", "Shae Phu", "Zorg Jednooki Baron", "Lisz", "Grabarz świątynny", "Wielka Stopa", "Morthen", "Leśne Widmo", "Goplana", "Adariel", "Burkog Lorulk", "Sheba Orcza Szamanka", "Królowa Śniegu", "Sataniel Skrytobójca", "Annaniel Wysysacz Marzeń", "Arachniregina Colosseus", "Fangaj", "Dendroculus", "Quetzalcoatl", "Zorin"]
        };

        const gui = document.createElement('div');
        gui.id = "zentrix_hud";
        gui.style = "position: fixed; top: 40px; left: 40px; z-index: 10001; background: rgba(10, 10, 12, 0.98); color: #00f2ff; padding: 20px; border: 1px solid #00f2ff; border-radius: 12px; width: 260px; font-family: sans-serif; box-shadow: 0 0 20px rgba(0,242,255,0.4);";
        gui.innerHTML = `
            <div id="zentrix_drag" style="text-align:center; font-weight:bold; margin-bottom:10px; cursor:move; border-bottom:1px solid #333; padding-bottom:5px;">ZENTRIX v1.2.8</div>
            <button id="z_togl" style="width:100%; background:#500; color:white; border:none; padding:10px; cursor:pointer; font-weight:bold; border-radius:4px;">BOT: OFF</button>
            <select id="z_preset" style="width:100%; margin-top:10px; background:#1a1a1d; color:#00f2ff; border:1px solid #444; padding:6px; border-radius:4px; font-size:12px;">
                <option value="">-- WYBIERZ SEKTOR --</option>
                ${Object.keys(expPresets).map(k => `<option value="${k}">${k}</option>`).join('')}
            </select>
            <div style="font-size:11px; margin-top:10px; background:rgba(0,0,0,0.3); padding:8px; border-radius:4px;">
                <div>📍 MAPA: <span id="z_map" style="color:#fff;">-</span></div>
                <div>📡 STATUS: <span id="z_mode" style="font-weight:bold; color:#00f2ff;">IDLE</span></div>
            </div>
        `;
        document.body.appendChild(gui);

        function updateStatus(txt, color = "#00f2ff") {
            const el = document.getElementById('z_mode');
            if(el) { el.innerText = txt.toUpperCase(); el.style.color = color; }
        }

        function traverseMaps() {
            const currentRoute = routes[window._currentPreset];
            if (!currentRoute) return;

            const currentMap = window.Engine.map.d.name;
            const currentIndex = currentRoute.indexOf(currentMap);
            if (currentIndex === -1) return;

            if (currentIndex === currentRoute.length - 1) _routeDirection = -1;
            else if (currentIndex === 0) _routeDirection = 1;

            const nextMapName = currentRoute[currentIndex + _routeDirection];

            if (hardcodedGates[currentMap] && hardcodedGates[currentMap][nextMapName]) {
                const [gx, gy] = hardcodedGates[currentMap][nextMapName];
                updateStatus("PRZECHODZENIE...", "#0af");
                window.Engine.hero.autoGoTo({x: gx, y: gy});
            }
        }

        document.getElementById('z_togl').onclick = function() {
            window._botActive = !window._botActive;
            this.innerText = window._botActive ? "BOT: ACTIVE" : "BOT: OFF";
            this.style.background = window._botActive ? "#050" : "#500";
            _emptyTicks = 0;
        };

        document.getElementById('z_preset').onchange = function() {
            window._currentPreset = this.value;
            window._targetList = expPresets[this.value] || [];
        };

        // GŁÓWNA PĘTLA BOTA
        setInterval(() => {
            if (!window._botActive) return;

            const mapName = window.Engine.map.d.name;
            document.getElementById('z_map').innerText = mapName;

            // 1. Lootowanie
            if (window.g?.loot) {
                window.Engine.keyHandler.down(70);
                setTimeout(()=>window.Engine.keyHandler.up(70), 50);
                return;
            }

            // 2. Walka
            if (window.Engine.battle?.show) {
                _emptyTicks = 0;
                if (!window.Engine.battle.isAuto) window.Engine.battle.autoFight(true);
                return;
            }

            if (_lockBot) return;

            // 3. Szukanie Celu
            const npcs = window.Engine.npcs.getDrawableList();
            let nearest = null, minDist = Infinity;

            for (let id in npcs) {
                const n = npcs[id];
                // Ignoruj martwe, graczy i nie-targety
                if (!n?.d || n.d.hp <= 0 || n.d.type === 0) continue;

                if (window._targetList.some(t => n.d.nick.toLowerCase().includes(t.toLowerCase()))) {
                    const d = Math.abs(window.Engine.hero.d.x - n.d.x) + Math.abs(window.Engine.hero.d.y - n.d.y);
                    if (d < minDist) { minDist = d; nearest = n; }
                }
            }

            if (nearest) {
                _emptyTicks = 0; // Znaleziono moba, reset licznika
                if (minDist <= 1) {
                    _lockBot = true;
                    updateStatus("ATAK!", "#f44");
                    window.Engine.hero.heroAtackRequest(nearest.d.id);
                    setTimeout(() => _lockBot = false, 800);
                } else {
                    updateStatus("IDĘ DO CELU", "#0f0");
                    window.Engine.hero.autoGoTo({x: nearest.d.x, y: nearest.d.y});
                }
            } else {
                // 4. Obsługa pstej mapy (NATYCHMIASTOWA)
                if (!window.Engine.hero.isMoving) {
                    _emptyTicks++;
                    // Próg ustawiony na 1 cykl (400ms) - bot reaguje od razu po braku mobów
                    if (_emptyTicks >= 1) {
                        updateStatus("SZUKAM DROGI", "#ff0");
                        traverseMaps();
                        _emptyTicks = 0;
                    }
                }
            }
        }, 400);
    }

    // Wstrzyknięcie kodu do silnika gry
    const s = document.createElement('script');
    s.textContent = `(${initZentrix.toString()})();`;
    document.head.appendChild(s);
})();

// ==UserScript==
// @name         bot
// @namespace    http://tampermonkey.net/
// @version      2024-07-25
// @description  try to take over the world!
// @author       chatlxrd
// @match        https://*.margonem.pl
// @icon         https://www.google.com/s2/favicons?sz=64&domain=margonem.pl
// @grant        none
// ==/UserScript==

var isFighting = false;
var botActive = false;

// Funkcja do wyświetlania wiadomości
function message(text) {
    console.log("[Bot]: " + text);
    if (typeof Engine?.message === "function") {
        Engine.message(text);
    }
}

// Funkcja do uruchamiania i zatrzymywania bota
function toggleBot() {
    botActive = !botActive;
    if (botActive) {
        message("Bot jest włączony");
        startBot();
    } else {
        message("Bot jest wyłączony");
    }
}

// Nasłuchiwacz zdarzeń dla klawisza "J"
document.addEventListener('keydown', function(event) {
    if (event.key === 'j' || event.key === 'J') {
        toggleBot();
    }
});

// Główna funkcja bota
function startBot() {
    if (!botActive || isFighting) return;

    var npcs = Engine.npcs.check();
    var mobs = [];
    var heroLevel = Engine.hero.d.lvl;

    // Filtrowanie tylko mobów typu 2 lub 3 i odpowiedniego poziomu
    for (var id in npcs) {
        var npc = npcs[id];
        if ((npc.d.type === 2 || npc.d.type === 3) && npc.d.lvl >= heroLevel - 10) {
            mobs.push(npc);
        } else {
            console.log(`[Pominięto] ${npc.d.nick} (lvl ${npc.d.lvl})`);
        }
    }

    if (mobs.length === 0) {
        console.log("Nie znaleziono odpowiednich mobów.");
        if (botActive) setTimeout(startBot, 1000);
        return;
    }

    // Szukanie najbliższego moba
    var heroX = Engine.hero.d.x;
    var heroY = Engine.hero.d.y;
    var nearestMob = null;
    var shortestDistance = Infinity;

    mobs.forEach(function (mob) {
        var distance = Math.sqrt(
            Math.pow(mob.d.x - heroX, 2) + Math.pow(mob.d.y - heroY, 2)
        );
        if (distance < shortestDistance) {
            shortestDistance = distance;
            nearestMob = mob;
        }
    });

    if (!nearestMob) {
        console.log("Brak odpowiedniego moba.");
        if (botActive) setTimeout(startBot, 1000);
        return;
    }

    console.log(`Najbliższy mob: ${nearestMob.d.nick} (lvl ${nearestMob.d.lvl})`);

    // Podejście do moba
    Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: nearestMob.d.x, y: nearestMob.d.y }, false);

    // Czekanie aż postać podejdzie
    setTimeout(function () {
        // Atak na moba
        Engine.hero.atackNearMob(nearestMob.d.id);
        console.log(`Atakuję: ${nearestMob.d.nick}`);
        isFighting = true;

        // Monitorowanie walki
        var checkBattleInterval = setInterval(function () {
            if (Engine.battle.endBattle === false) {
                console.log('Walka trwa... naciskam "F"');
                document.dispatchEvent(new KeyboardEvent('keydown', { key: 'F' }));
            }

            if (Engine.battle.canLeaveBattle === true) {
                clearInterval(checkBattleInterval);
                console.log("Walka zakończona. Zamykanie okna walki...");
                Engine.battle.leaveBattle();
                isFighting = false;
                if (botActive) startBot();
            }
        }, 1000);
    }, 200);
}


// ==UserScript==
// @name         Margonem - E2 Hunter v131.2 + FF HOOK & LOGS
// @match        https://*.margonem.pl/
// @run-at       document-end
// @grant        none
// ==/UserScript==

(function() {
    'use strict';
    const script = document.createElement('script');
    script.textContent = `
        (function() {
            window._botActive = false;
            window._targetList = [];
            window._blackList = ["brąz1-slp", "brąz", "sys_"];
            let _lockBot = false;

            // --- FUNKCJA LOGOWANIA DO KONSOLI ---
            const botLog = (msg, color = "#00ffff") => {
                const now = new Date();
                const time = now.getHours().toString().padStart(2, '0') + ":" +
                             now.getMinutes().toString().padStart(2, '0') + ":" +
                             now.getSeconds().toString().padStart(2, '0');
                console.log("%c[" + time + "] [HUNTER] " + msg, "color:" + color + "; font-weight:bold;");
            };

            // --- FAST FIGHT HOOK ---
            const original_g = window._g;
            window._g = (query, clb) => {
                const s = ["fight", "a=attack", "id=-"];
                if(s.every(el => query.includes(el)) && !query.includes("ff=1")){
                    query += "&ff=1";
                }
                original_g(query, clb);
            };

            // UI
            const gui = document.createElement('div');
            gui.style = "position:fixed; top:10px; left:10px; z-index:10000; background:rgba(20,20,20,0.95); color:white; padding:15px; border:2px solid #00ffff; border-radius:10px; font-family:sans-serif; width:220px; pointer-events: auto;";
            gui.innerHTML = \`
                <div style="text-align:center; font-weight:bold; color:#00ffff; border-bottom:1px solid #444; margin-bottom:10px; padding-bottom:5px;">HUNTER v131.2 LOGS</div>
                <button id="b_toggle" style="background:#444; color:white; border:none; cursor:pointer; width:100%; padding:5px;">OFF</button>
                <div id="b_npc_list" style="max-height:120px; overflow-y:auto; background:#111; padding:5px; border-radius:4px; font-size:11px; margin:10px 0; border:1px solid #333;"></div>
                <div style="font-size:11px;">Cele: <span id="b_active_targets" style="color:#00ff00;">---</span></div>
                <button id="b_clear" style="width:100%; font-size:10px; background:#622; color:white; border:none; cursor:pointer; padding:5px; margin-top:5px;">WYCZYŚĆ</button>
            \`;
            document.body.appendChild(gui);

            document.getElementById('b_toggle').onclick = (e) => {
                window._botActive = !window._botActive;
                e.target.innerText = window._botActive ? "ON" : "OFF";
                e.target.style.background = window._botActive ? "#060" : "#444";
                botLog("Bot został " + (window._botActive ? "URUCHOMIONY" : "ZATRZYMANY"), window._botActive ? "#00ff00" : "#ff0000");
            };

            document.getElementById('b_clear').onclick = () => {
                window._targetList = [];
                document.getElementById('b_active_targets').innerText = "---";
                botLog("Lista celów wyczyszczona.");
            };

            window._addTarget = (nick) => {
                if (nick && !window._targetList.includes(nick)) {
                    window._targetList.push(nick);
                    document.getElementById('b_active_targets').innerText = window._targetList.join(", ");
                    botLog("Dodano cel: " + nick, "#ffff00");
                }
            };

            // LISTA NPC
            setInterval(() => {
                const list = window.Engine?.npcs?.getDrawableList();
                if (!list) return;
                const container = document.getElementById('b_npc_list');
                if (!container) return;
                let html = "";
                const seen = new Set();
                for (let i in list) {
                    const n = list[i];
                    if (n && n.d && n.d.nick && !seen.has(n.d.nick) && n.d.type !== 0) {
                        if (!window._blackList.some(b => n.d.nick.toLowerCase().includes(b.toLowerCase()))) {
                            seen.add(n.d.nick);
                            html += \`<div style="cursor:pointer; padding:3px; border-bottom:1px solid #222;" onclick="window._addTarget('\${n.d.nick}')">\${n.d.nick}</div>\`;
                        }
                    }
                }
                container.innerHTML = html;
            }, 1500);

            // LOGIKA ATAKU
            const attackLogic = function() {
                if (!window._botActive || _lockBot) return;

                const list = window.Engine?.npcs?.getDrawableList();
                const hero = window.Engine?.hero;
                if (!list || !hero || !hero.d || !hero.d.id) return;

                for (let i in list) {
                    const n = list[i];
                    if (!n || !n.d || !n.d.id || n.isDead || n.d.id === hero.d.id) continue;

                    if (window._targetList.includes(n.d.nick)) {
                        const dist = Math.abs(hero.d.x - n.d.x) + Math.abs(hero.d.y - n.d.y);
                        if (dist <= 1) {
                            _lockBot = true;

                            // LOG ZANIM WYŚLEMY ATACK
                            botLog("ATAKUJĘ: " + n.d.nick + " (ID: " + n.d.id + ")", "#ffaa00");

                            if (window.Engine.hero.heroAtackRequest) window.Engine.hero.heroAtackRequest(n.d.id);

                            setTimeout(() => {
                                _lockBot = false;
                                if (window.Engine?.battle?.finished) window.Engine.battle.close();
                            }, 3000);
                        } else {
                            window.Engine.hero.autoGoTo({x: n.d.x, y: n.d.y}, {type: "click"});
                        }
                        return;
                    }
                }
            };
            setInterval(attackLogic, 500);

            // LOOTER
            setInterval(() => {
                if (window._botActive) {
                    const kh = window.Engine?.keyHandler;
                    if (kh) {
                        kh.down(70); // F
                        kh.down(27); // ESC
                    }
                }
            }, 600);
        })();
    `;
    (document.head || document.documentElement).appendChild(script);
})();

// ==UserScript==
// @name         Margonem - E2 Hunter v131.2 SMART TARGET
// @match        https://*.margonem.pl/
// @run-at       document-end
// @grant        none
// ==/UserScript==

(function() {
    'use strict';
    
    function initBot() {
        if (typeof window.Engine === 'undefined' || !window.Engine.npcs) {
            setTimeout(initBot, 500);
            return;
        }

        window._botActive = false;
        window._targetList = [];
        window._blackList = ["brąz1-slp", "brąz", "sys_"];
        let _lockBot = false;

        // UI
        const gui = document.createElement('div');
        gui.style = "position:fixed; top:10px; left:10px; z-index:10000; background:rgba(15,15,15,0.95); color:white; padding:12px; border:1px solid #00ffff; border-radius:8px; font-family:Arial; width:200px; pointer-events:auto; box-shadow: 0 0 10px black;";
        gui.innerHTML = `
            <div style="text-align:center;font-weight:bold;color:#00ffff;border-bottom:1px solid #333;margin-bottom:8px;padding-bottom:5px;font-size:12px;">HUNTER SMART TARGET</div>
            <button id="b_toggle" style="background:#cc0000;color:white;border:none;cursor:pointer;width:100%;padding:6px;border-radius:4px;font-weight:bold;">OFF</button>
            <div id="b_npc_list" style="max-height:100px; overflow-y:auto; background:#050505; padding:5px; border-radius:4px; font-size:11px; margin:8px 0; border:1px solid #222;"></div>
            <div style="font-size:11px;">Cele: <span id="b_active_targets" style="color:#00ff00;">---</span></div>
            <button id="b_clear" style="width:100%; font-size:10px; background:#422; color:#faa; border:none; cursor:pointer; padding:4px; margin-top:8px;">WYCZYŚĆ</button>
        `;
        document.body.appendChild(gui);

        document.getElementById('b_toggle').onclick = function() {
            window._botActive = !window._botActive;
            this.innerText = window._botActive ? "ON" : "OFF";
            this.style.background = window._botActive ? "#006600" : "#cc0000";
        };

        document.getElementById('b_clear').onclick = function() {
            window._targetList = [];
            document.getElementById('b_active_targets').innerText = "---";
        };

        window._addTarget = function(nick) {
            if (nick && !window._targetList.includes(nick)) {
                window._targetList.push(nick);
                document.getElementById('b_active_targets').innerText = window._targetList.join(", ");
            }
        };

        // --- SZYBKA WALKA ---
        const fastFightLogic = function() {
            if (!window._botActive) return false;
            const isFight = window.Engine.battle && (window.Engine.battle.show === true || window.Engine.battle.isBattleShow?.());
            if (isFight) {
                if (typeof window.Engine.battle.autoFight === 'function' && !window.Engine.battle.isAuto) {
                    window.Engine.battle.autoFight(true);
                }
                if (window._g) window._g("fight&a=f");
                return true;
            }
            return false;
        };

        // NPC List Refresh
        setInterval(function() {
            const list = window.Engine.npcs.getDrawableList();
            const container = document.getElementById('b_npc_list');
            if (!list || !container) return;
            let html = "";
            const seen = new Set();
            for (const id in list) {
                const n = list[id];
                if (n?.d?.nick && n.d.type !== 0 && !seen.has(n.d.nick)) {
                    if (!window._blackList.some(b => n.d.nick.toLowerCase().includes(b.toLowerCase()))) {
                        seen.add(n.d.nick);
                        html += `<div style="cursor:pointer;padding:2px;border-bottom:1px solid #1a1a1a;" onclick="window._addTarget('${n.d.nick}')">${n.d.nick}</div>`;
                    }
                }
            }
            container.innerHTML = html || "Szukanie mobów...";
        }, 1000);

        // --- GŁÓWNA LOGIKA SZUKANIA NAJBLIŻSZEGO CELU ---
        setInterval(function() {
            if (!window._botActive || _lockBot) return;
            if (fastFightLogic()) return;

            const list = window.Engine.npcs.getDrawableList();
            const hero = window.Engine.hero;
            if (!list || !hero?.d || hero.d.hp <= 0) return;

            let nearestTarget = null;
            let minDistance = Infinity;

            // 1. Znajdź wszystkie pasujące moby i oblicz, który jest najbliżej
            for (const id in list) {
                const n = list[id];
                if (!n?.d || n.isDead || n.d.id === hero.d.id) continue;

                if (window._targetList.includes(n.d.nick)) {
                    // Obliczamy dystans Manhattan (x1-x2 + y1-y2)
                    const dist = Math.abs(hero.d.x - n.d.x) + Math.abs(hero.d.y - n.d.y);
                    
                    if (dist < minDistance) {
                        minDistance = dist;
                        nearestTarget = n;
                    }
                }
            }

            // 2. Jeśli znaleźliśmy jakikolwiek cel z listy
            if (nearestTarget) {
                if (minDistance <= 1) {
                    _lockBot = true;
                    if (hero.heroAtackRequest) hero.heroAtackRequest(nearestTarget.d.id);
                    else nearestTarget.onMouseClick();
                    setTimeout(() => { _lockBot = false; }, 1000);
                } else {
                    window.Engine.hero.autoGoTo({x: nearestTarget.d.x, y: nearestTarget.d.y});
                }
            }
        }, 350);

        // Looter
        setInterval(function() {
            const isFight = window.Engine.battle && (window.Engine.battle.show === true || window.Engine.battle.isBattleShow?.());
            if (window._botActive && window.Engine.keyHandler && !isFight) {
                window.Engine.keyHandler.down(70);
                setTimeout(() => window.Engine.keyHandler.up(70), 50);
            }
        }, 500);
    }

    const script = document.createElement('script');
    script.textContent = "(" + initBot.toString() + ")();";
    document.head.appendChild(script);
})();

            "--- ELITY II (ALL) ---": ["Mushita", "Kotołak Tropiciel", "Shae Phu", "Zorg Jednooki Baron", "Władca rzek", "Gobbos", "Tyrtajos", "Tollok Shimger", "Szczęt alias Gładki", "Agar", "Razuglag Oklash", "Foverk Turrim", "Owadzia Matka", "Furruk Kozug", "Vari Kruger", "Jotun", "Tollok Utumutu", "Tollok Atamatu", "Lisz", "Grabarz świątynny", "Wielka Stopa", "Podły zbrojmistrz", "Choukker", "Nadzorczyni krasnoludów", "Morthen", "Leśne Widmo", "Żelazoręki Ohydziarz", "Goplana", "Gnom Figlid", "Centaur Zyfryd", "Kambion", "Jertek Moxos", "Miłośnik rycerzy", "Miłośnik magii", "Miłośnik łowców", "Łowca czaszek", "Ozirus Władca Hieroglifów", "Morski potwór", "Krab pustelnik", "Borgoros Garamir III", "Stworzyciel", "Ifryt", "Jack Truciciel", "Helga Opiekunka Rumu", "Henry Kaprawe Oko", "Eol", "Grubber Ochlaj", "Mistrz Worundriel", "Wójt Fistuła", "Teściowa Rumcajsa", "Berserker Amuno", "Fodug Zolash", "Goons Asterus", "Adariel", "Burkog Lorulk", "Sheba Orcza Szamanka", "Shakkru", "Duch Władcy Klanów", "Bragarth Myśliwy Dusz", "Fursharag Pożeracz Umysłów", "Ziuggrael Strażnik Królowej", "Lusgrathera Królowa Pramatka", "Królowa Śniegu", "Wrzosera", "Chryzoprenia", "Cantedewia", "Ogr Stalowy Pazur", "Torunia Ankelwald", "Pięknotka Mięsożerna", "Breheret Żelazny Łeb", "Cerasus", "Mysiur Myświórowy Król", "Sadolia Nadzorczyni Hurys", "Sataniel Skrytobójca", "Bergermona Krwawa Hrabina", "Annaniel Wysysacz Marzeń", "Gothardus Kolekcjoner Głów", "Zufulus Smakosz Serc", "Czempion Furboli", "Arachniregina Colosseus", "Rycerz z za małym mieczem", "Al'diphrin Ilythirahel", "Marlloth Malignitas", "Arytodam olbrzymi", "Mocny Maddoks", "Fangaj", "Dendroculus", "Tolypeutes", "Cuaitl Citlalin", "Yaotl", "Quetzalcoatl", "Wabicielka", "Pogardliwa Sybilla", "Chopesz", "Neferkar Set", "Terrozaur", "Vaenra Charkhaam", "Chaegd Agnrakh", "Nymphemonia", "Artenius", "Furion", "Zorin"]
        };

        // GUI
        const gui = document.createElement('div');
        gui.style = "position:fixed; top:20px; left:20px; z-index:10000; background:rgba(10,10,10,0.9); color:white; padding:15px; border:2px solid #00ffff; border-radius:10px; font-family:sans-serif; width:250px; box-shadow: 0 0 20px rgba(0,255,255,0.3);";

        const sortedKeys = Object.keys(expPresets).sort((a, b) => {
            if (a.includes("---")) return 1;
            return parseInt(a.match(/\d+/) || 0) - parseInt(b.match(/\d+/) || 0);
        });

        gui.innerHTML = `
            <div id="drag" style="text-align:center; font-weight:bold; color:#00ffff; margin-bottom:10px; cursor:move;">EXP + E2 Auto</div>
            <button id="b_togl" style="width:100%; background:red; color:white; border:none; padding:8px; border-radius:5px; font-weight:bold; cursor:pointer;">BOT: OFF</button>
            <select id="b_preset" style="width:100%; margin-top:10px; background:#222; color:white; border:1px solid #444; padding:5px;">
                <option value="">-- Wybierz Exp --</option>
                ${sortedKeys.map(k => `<option value="${k}">${k}</option>`).join('')}
            </select>
            <div style="font-size:10px; margin-top:10px; color:#0f0;">Cele: <span id="b_stat">Brak</span></div>
            <button id="b_clear" style="width:100%; margin-top:5px; font-size:10px; background:#400; color:#f88; border:none; cursor:pointer;">Wyczyść cele</button>
        `;
        document.body.appendChild(gui);

        // DRAG GUI
        let isD = false, ox, oy;
        gui.onmousedown = e => { if(e.target.id==="drag") { isD = true; ox = e.clientX - gui.offsetLeft; oy = e.clientY - gui.offsetTop; }};
        document.onmousemove = e => { if(isD) { gui.style.left = (e.clientX-ox)+'px'; gui.style.top = (e.clientY-oy)+'px'; }};
        document.onmouseup = () => isD = false;

        // AKCJE GUI
        document.getElementById('b_togl').onclick = function() {
            window._botActive = !window._botActive;
            this.innerText = window._botActive ? "BOT: ON" : "BOT: OFF";
            this.style.background = window._botActive ? "green" : "red";
        };
        document.getElementById('b_preset').onchange = function() {
            if(this.value) {
                window._targetList = [...expPresets[this.value]];
                document.getElementById('b_stat').innerText = window._targetList.slice(0,3).join(", ") + "...";
            }
        };
        document.getElementById('b_clear').onclick = () => { window._targetList = []; document.getElementById('b_stat').innerText = "Brak"; };

        // PĘTLA GŁÓWNA
        setInterval(() => {
            if (!window._botActive) return;

            // OBSŁUGA LOOTU (TYLKO PODNOSZENIE)
            if (window.g?.loot && window.g.loot.id !== _lastLootId) {
                _lastLootId = window.g.loot.id;
                // Podnieś (klawisz F)
                setTimeout(() => { window.Engine.keyHandler.down(70); setTimeout(()=>window.Engine.keyHandler.up(70), 50); }, 300);
                return;
            }

            // OBSŁUGA WALKI
            if (window.Engine.battle && window.Engine.battle.show) {
                if (window.Engine.battle.autoFight && !window.Engine.battle.isAuto) window.Engine.battle.autoFight(true);
                return;
            }

            if (_lockBot) return;

            // SZUKANIE NPC
            const npcs = window.Engine.npcs.getDrawableList();
            const hero = window.Engine.hero;
            let nearest = null, minDist = Infinity;

            for (let id in npcs) {
                const n = npcs[id];
                if (!n?.d || n.isDead) continue;
                if (window._targetList.some(t => n.d.nick.toLowerCase().includes(t.toLowerCase()))) {
                    const d = Math.abs(hero.d.x - n.d.x) + Math.abs(hero.d.y - n.d.y);
                    if (d < minDist) { minDist = d; nearest = n; }
                }
            }

            if (nearest) {
                _lastTargetName = nearest.d.nick;
                if (minDist <= 1) {
                    _lockBot = true;
                    if (hero.heroAtackRequest) hero.heroAtackRequest(nearest.d.id);
                    else nearest.onMouseClick();
                    setTimeout(() => _lockBot = false, 800);
                } else {
                    window.Engine.hero.autoGoTo({x: nearest.d.x, y: nearest.d.y});
                }
            }
        }, 400);
    }

    const s = document.createElement('script');
    s.textContent = `(${initBot.toString()})();`;
    document.head.appendChild(s);
})();

// ==UserScript==
// @name         chybalepszybot
// @namespace    http://tampermonkey.net/
// @version      2025-06-19
// @description  try to take over the world!
// @author       You
// @match        https://katahha.margonem.pl/
// @icon         https://www.google.com/s2/favicons?sz=64&domain=margonem.pl
// @grant        none
// ==/UserScript==

(function () {
    'use strict';

    let active = false;
    let attackInterval, moveInterval;
    let mobCoords = [];
    let currentIndex = 0;

    // Flaga blokująca wielokrotne wywołanie ataku na tego samego moba
    let hasAttacked = false;

    // GUI
    const guiDiv = document.createElement("div");
    guiDiv.style.position = "fixed";
    guiDiv.style.top = "10px";
    guiDiv.style.left = "10px";
    guiDiv.style.zIndex = "9999";
    guiDiv.style.backgroundColor = "#111";
    guiDiv.style.padding = "10px";
    guiDiv.style.border = "1px solid #444";
    guiDiv.style.color = "#0f0";
    guiDiv.style.fontSize = "14px";
    guiDiv.style.fontFamily = "monospace";
    guiDiv.innerText = "Uruchom Czarnucha";

    const toggleBtn = document.createElement("button");
    toggleBtn.textContent = "Start";
    toggleBtn.style.marginTop = "5px";
    toggleBtn.style.display = "block";
    toggleBtn.style.width = "100%";
    guiDiv.appendChild(toggleBtn);
    document.body.appendChild(guiDiv);

    // 🔁 Szuka mobów typu 2,3 i zapisuje ich pozycje
    function searchMobs() {
        const mobs = Engine.npcs.check();
        mobCoords = [];

        for (const mobID in mobs) {
            const mob = mobs[mobID];
            if ((mob.d.type === 2 || mob.d.type === 3) && mob.d.lvl > 10) {
                console.log(`📍 Mob: ${mob.d.nick} - pozycja: (${mob.rx}, ${mob.ry})`);
                mobCoords.push([mob.rx, mob.ry]);
            }
        }

        if (mobCoords.length === 0) {
            console.log("❌ Brak mobów typu 2,3 na mapie.");
        }
    }

    // 🚶 Ruch do kolejnego moba
    function moveToNextMob() {
        if (!active) return;

        const mobs = Engine.npcs.check();
        const heroX = Engine.hero.getX();
        const heroY = Engine.hero.getY();
        let closestMob = null;
        let closestDist = Infinity;

        for (const mobID in mobs) {
            const mob = mobs[mobID];
            if ((mob.d.type === 2 || mob.d.type === 3) && mob.d.lvl > 10) {
                const dist = Math.hypot(mob.rx - heroX, mob.ry - heroY);
                if (dist < closestDist) {
                    closestDist = dist;
                    closestMob = mob;
                }
            }
        }

        if (!closestMob) {
            console.log("✅ Wszystkie moby zabite lub brak mobów typu 2,3.");
            return;
        }

        const mobX = closestMob.rx;
        const mobY = closestMob.ry;

        if (Math.abs(heroX - mobX) < 1 && Math.abs(heroY - mobY) < 1) {
            // jesteśmy już przy mobie
            return;
        }

        Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: mobX, y: mobY });
    }

    // ⚔️ Sprawdza, czy można zaatakować moba (±1 kratka) i odpala autofight tylko 1 raz na walkę
    function attackIfNear() {
        const heroX = Engine.hero.getX();
        const heroY = Engine.hero.getY();

        if (hasAttacked) {
            // Jeśli już atakowaliśmy, sprawdzamy czy mob jest nadal blisko
            if (!isMobNearHero(heroX, heroY)) {
                // Mob zniknął, resetujemy flagę
                hasAttacked = false;
                console.log("ℹ️ Mob zniknął, można atakować ponownie.");
            }
            return; // nie wysyłamy nowego ataku
        }

        for (const mobID in Engine.npcs.check()) {
            const mob = Engine.npcs.check()[mobID];
            if (mob.d.type === 2) {
                const mobX = mob.rx;
                const mobY = mob.ry;

                if (Math.abs(heroX - mobX) <= 1 && Math.abs(heroY - mobY) <= 1) {
                    triggerAutoFight();
                    hasAttacked = true;  // ustawiamy flagę, że atak został wykonany
                    console.log("✅ Atak na moba wykonany.");
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    // Sprawdza, czy mob typu 2 stoi obok postaci (±1 kratka)
    function isMobNearHero(heroX, heroY) {
        for (const mobID in Engine.npcs.check()) {
            const mob = Engine.npcs.check()[mobID];
            if (mob.d.type === 2) {
                const mobX = mob.rx;
                const mobY = mob.ry;
                if (Math.abs(heroX - mobX) <= 1 && Math.abs(heroY - mobY) <= 1) {
                    return true; // mob jest blisko
                }
            }
        }
        return false; // mob nie jest blisko
    }

    // 🟢 Kliknięcie przycisku autofight (symulacja)
    function triggerAutoFight() {
        const autoFightBtn = document.querySelector(".widget-button:has(.icon.auto-fight-near-mob):not(.from-settings-panel)");
        if (autoFightBtn) {
            setTimeout(() => {
                autoFightBtn.click();
                console.log("✅ AutoFight Near Mob aktywowany (po 500ms)");
            }, 500);
        } else {
            console.warn("❌ Nie znaleziono przycisku AutoFight");
        }
    }

    // Funkcja włączająca autofight
    function startAutoFight() {
        if (!active) {
            active = true;
            toggleBtn.textContent = "Stop";
            console.clear();
            console.log("🚀 Startuję skanowanie i atakowanie mobów typu 2...");
            searchMobs();
            currentIndex = 0;
            moveInterval = setInterval(moveToNextMob, 1);
            attackInterval = setInterval(attackIfNear, 1);
        }
    }

    // Funkcja zatrzymująca autofight
    function stopAutoFight() {
        if (active) {
            active = false;
            toggleBtn.textContent = "Start";
            clearInterval(moveInterval);
            clearInterval(attackInterval);
            console.log("⛔ Zatrzymano skrypt.");
        }
    }

    // Monitoruje Engine.battle.endBattle i resetuje flagę po zakończeniu walki
    let lastEndBattleState = null;
    function battleObserver() {
        if (typeof Engine.battle === "undefined" || typeof Engine.battle.endBattle === "undefined") {
            return; // jeszcze niedostępne
        }
        const currentState = Engine.battle.endBattle;
        if (lastEndBattleState !== currentState) {
            console.log(`🔍 Engine.battle.endBattle zmieniło się na: ${currentState}`);
            if (currentState === true) {
                // Bitwa zakończona - resetujemy flagę ataku i ewentualnie wznawiamy autofight
                hasAttacked = false;
                if (!active) {
                    startAutoFight();
                }
            } else {
                // Bitwa trwa - zatrzymaj autofight
                stopAutoFight();
            }
            lastEndBattleState = currentState;
        }
    }

    // 🔘 Start/Stop (manualny toggle)
    toggleBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
        if (active) {
            stopAutoFight();
        } else {
            startAutoFight();
        }
    });

    // Start monitoringu bitwy w tle
    setInterval(battleObserver, 1);

})();


// ==UserScript==
// @name         bot
// @namespace    http://tampermonkey.net/
// @version      2024-07-25
// @description  try to take over the world!
// @author       You
// @match        https://*.margonem.pl
// @icon         https://www.google.com/s2/favicons?sz=64&domain=margonem.pl
// @grant        none
// ==/UserScript==

var isFighting = false;
var botActive = false;

// Funkcja do wyświetlania wiadomości
function message(text) {
    console.log("[Bot]: " + text);
    if (typeof Engine?.message === "function") {
        Engine.message(text);
    }
}

// Funkcja do uruchamiania i zatrzymywania bota
function toggleBot() {
    botActive = !botActive;
    if (botActive) {
        message("Bot jest włączony");
        startBot();
    } else {
        message("Bot jest wyłączony");
    }
}

// Nasłuchiwacz zdarzeń dla klawisza "J"
document.addEventListener('keydown', function(event) {
    if (event.key === 'j' || event.key === 'J') {
        toggleBot();
    }
});

// Główna funkcja bota
function startBot() {
    if (!botActive || isFighting) return;

    var npcs = Engine.npcs.check();
    var mobs = [];
    var heroLevel = Engine.hero.d.lvl;

    // Filtrowanie tylko mobów typu 2 lub 3 i odpowiedniego poziomu
    for (var id in npcs) {
        var npc = npcs[id];
        if ((npc.d.type === 2 || npc.d.type === 3) && npc.d.lvl >= heroLevel - 10) {
            mobs.push(npc);
        } else {
            console.log(`[Pominięto] ${npc.d.nick} (lvl ${npc.d.lvl})`);
        }
    }

    if (mobs.length === 0) {
        console.log("Nie znaleziono odpowiednich mobów.");
        if (botActive) setTimeout(startBot, 1000);
        return;
    }

    // Szukanie najbliższego moba
    var heroX = Engine.hero.d.x;
    var heroY = Engine.hero.d.y;
    var nearestMob = null;
    var shortestDistance = Infinity;

    mobs.forEach(function (mob) {
        var distance = Math.sqrt(
            Math.pow(mob.d.x - heroX, 2) + Math.pow(mob.d.y - heroY, 2)
        );
        if (distance < shortestDistance) {
            shortestDistance = distance;
            nearestMob = mob;
        }
    });

    if (!nearestMob) {
        console.log("Brak odpowiedniego moba.");
        if (botActive) setTimeout(startBot, 1000);
        return;
    }

    console.log(`Najbliższy mob: ${nearestMob.d.nick} (lvl ${nearestMob.d.lvl})`);

    // Podejście do moba
    Engine.hero.autoGoTo({ x: nearestMob.d.x, y: nearestMob.d.y }, false);

    // Czekanie aż postać podejdzie
    setTimeout(function () {
        // Atak na moba
        Engine.hero.atackNearMob(nearestMob.d.id);
        console.log(`Atakuję: ${nearestMob.d.nick}`);
        isFighting = true;

        // Monitorowanie walki
        var checkBattleInterval = setInterval(function () {
            if (Engine.battle.endBattle === false) {
                console.log('Walka trwa... naciskam "F"');
                document.dispatchEvent(new KeyboardEvent('keydown', { key: 'F' }));
            }

            if (Engine.battle.canLeaveBattle === true) {
                clearInterval(checkBattleInterval);
                console.log("Walka zakończona. Zamykanie okna walki...");
                Engine.battle.leaveBattle();
                isFighting = false;
                if (botActive) startBot();
            }
        }, 1000);
    }, 200);
}
